<script>
// ── Global GAS error handler ──
function _onGasError(err) {
  var msg = (err && err.message) ? err.message : String(err || 'Erreur inconnue');
  if (typeof showToast === 'function') {
    showToast('Erreur serveur: ' + msg, 'error');
  } else {
    alert('Erreur serveur: ' + msg);
  }
  console.error('GAS Error:', err);
}
function _gas() {
  return google.script.run.withFailureHandler(_onGasError);
}

let allTransactions = [];
var _startupTab = "budget";
var _currentPlanId = null;
var _allPlans = [];

// ── Sélecteur de plan ──
function _initPlans(plans, currentPlanId) {
  _allPlans = plans || [];
  _currentPlanId = currentPlanId || (_allPlans[0] && _allPlans[0].id) || null;
  _renderPlanSelector();
}

function _renderPlanSelector() {
  const sel = document.getElementById("planDrawerSelect");
  if (!sel) return;
  // Rebrancher l'event (évite les doublons)
  sel.onchange = function() { _switchPlan(this.value); };
  sel.innerHTML = "";
  _allPlans.forEach(function(p) {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = p.id;
    opt.textContent = p.name;
    if (p.id === _currentPlanId) opt.selected = true;
    sel.appendChild(opt);
  });
}

function _switchPlan(planId) {
  if (planId === _currentPlanId) { closeDrawer(); return; }
  var _sp = document.getElementById("spinnerOverlay");
  if (_sp) _sp.classList.add("active");
  // Un seul appel GAS (audit perf : 2 RTT → 1 RTT)
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
      _currentPlanId  = data.currentPlanId;
      _allPlans       = data.plans || _allPlans;
      allCategories   = data.categories;
      allBuckets      = data.buckets;
      allDebtors      = data.debtors;
      allTransactions = _normalizeTxList(data.transactions);
      allPrevisions   = data.previsions || [];
      allProjects     = data.projects     || [];
      _totalSavings   = data.totalSavings || 0;
      _savingsCatId   = data.savingsCatId  || _savingsCatId;
      _assignCatId    = data.assignCatId   || _assignCatId;
      historyLoaded   = true;
      _renderPlanSelector();
      invalidateBudgetCache();
      renderSettings();
      if (_currentSettingsTab === "plans") _renderPlansSettings();
      loadBudget(true);
      // Reset des filtres Banque avant refresh (évite affichage vide si période absente du nouveau plan)
      ["filterPeriod","filterCategory","filterDebtor","filterSense"].forEach(function(id){
        var el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.selectedIndex = 0;
      });
      var fu = document.getElementById("filterUncleared"); if (fu) fu.checked = false;
      var fl = document.getElementById("filterLocked");    if (fl) fl.checked = true; // défaut : masquer verrouillées
      refreshHistory(allTransactions);
      computeSoldes();
      updateDrawerSolde();
      _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
      if (_sp) _sp.classList.remove("active");
      closeDrawer();
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function() { if (_sp) _sp.classList.remove("active"); })
    .switchPlanAndLoad(planId);
}

// ── Modal nouveau plan ──
function _openNewPlanModal() {
  // Remplir le select de copie
  const sel = document.getElementById("newPlanCopyFromSelect");
  if (sel) {
    sel.innerHTML = "";
    _allPlans.forEach(function(p) {
      const opt = document.createElement("option");
      opt.value = p.id;
      opt.textContent = p.name;
      sel.appendChild(opt);
    });
  }
  document.getElementById("newPlanName").value = "";
  const none = document.getElementById("planCopyNone");
  if (none) { none.checked = true; _planRadioSync(); }
  const btn = document.querySelector("#newPlanModal .btn-primary");
  if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = "Créer"; }
  document.getElementById("newPlanModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeNewPlanModal() {
  document.getElementById("newPlanModal").classList.remove("active");
}

function _createNewPlan() {
  const name = document.getElementById("newPlanName").value.trim();
  if (!name) return;
  const isCopy = document.getElementById("planCopyFrom") && document.getElementById("planCopyFrom").checked;
  const copyFrom = isCopy ? (document.getElementById("newPlanCopyFromSelect").value || null) : null;
  const btn = document.querySelector("#newPlanModal .btn-primary");
  if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = "⏳..."; }
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = "Créer"; }
      closeNewPlanModal();
      _allPlans = result.plans;
      _renderPlanSelector();
      _renderPlansSettings();
      _switchPlan(result.newPlanId);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function() {
      if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = "Créer"; }
    })
    .addPlan(name, copyFrom);
}
// File d'attente transactions
let _txQueue         = [];   // file de saisie UI (batch)
let _txSaveQueue     = [];   // file saves avec résolution bénéficiaires inconnus
let _pendingEditForm = null; // formulaire modif en attente (bénéficiaire inconnu)

// ─── Normalisation champ debtor ─────────────────────────────────
function _normalizeTx(tx) {
  if (!tx) return tx;
  tx.debtor = tx.debtor || tx.payee || tx.beneficiary || tx.debtorName || tx.creditor || "";
  tx.linked_prevision_id = tx.linked_prevision_id || "";
  return tx;
}
function _normalizeTxList(list) { return (list || []).map(_normalizeTx); }

let allCategories   = [];
let allBuckets      = [];
let allDebtors      = [];
let allPeriods      = [];
let pendingDeleteId = null;
let openMenuId      = null;
let historyLoaded   = false;
let selectedIds       = new Set();
let _pendingUnlockIds = [];
let allPrevisions     = [];
let allProjects       = [];
let _totalSavings     = 0;
let _savingsCatId     = "CAT001";
let _assignCatId      = "";
let _editingPrevId       = null;
let _deletePrevId        = null;
window._deleteIsPrevision = false;

// ================= FORMAT € =================
function formatEuro(amount) {
  const n = Number(amount);
  if (isNaN(n)) return "0,00 €";
  return n.toLocaleString("fr-FR", { style:"currency", currency:"EUR", minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2 });
}

// ================= SPINNER =================
function showSpinner() { const el=document.getElementById("spinnerOverlay"); if(el) el.classList.add("active"); }
function hideSpinner() { const el=document.getElementById("spinnerOverlay"); if(el) el.classList.remove("active"); }

// ================= NAVIGATION =================

// Basculer le scroll du .sheet selon la section active
function _setSheetScroll(mode) {
  // mode "locked" = budget/banque gèrent leur propre scroll interne
  // mode "free"   = .sheet scrollable normalement
  const sheet = document.querySelector(".sheet");
  if (!sheet) return;
  sheet.style.overflowY = (mode === "locked") ? "hidden" : "auto";
}

// ── Filtre texte dans les panels settings ──
function filterSettingsList(type, query) {
  const listId = type === "categories" ? "categoriesSettingsList2"
               : type === "buckets"    ? "bucketsSettingsList2"
               : "debtorsSettingsList2";
  const container = document.getElementById(listId);
  if (!container) return;
  const q = (query || "").toLowerCase().trim();

  if (type === "categories") {
    // Filtrer les items et masquer les groupes vides
    const groups = container.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-bucket-header");
    groups.forEach(hdr => {
      const grpId = hdr.nextElementSibling && hdr.nextElementSibling.id;
      const body  = grpId ? document.getElementById(grpId) : null;
      if (!body) return;
      const items = body.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-item");
      let visible = 0;
      items.forEach(item => {
        const name = (item.querySelector(".smgmt-item-name") || {}).textContent || "";
        const match = !q || name.toLowerCase().includes(q);
        item.classList.toggle("hidden-by-filter", !match);
        if (match) visible++;
      });
      hdr.classList.toggle("hidden-by-filter", visible === 0 && !!q);
    });
  } else {
    // buckets / debtors : filtrage simple
    container.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-item").forEach(item => {
      const name = (item.querySelector(".smgmt-item-name") || {}).textContent || "";
      item.classList.toggle("hidden-by-filter", !!q && !name.toLowerCase().includes(q));
    });
  }
}

// ── Reset tous les filtres banque ──
function resetAllFilters() {
  ["filterPeriod","filterCategory","filterDebtor","filterSense"].forEach(id => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id); if (el) el.selectedIndex = 0;
  });
  const fu = document.getElementById("filterUncleared"); if (fu) fu.checked = false;
  const fl = document.getElementById("filterLocked"); if (fl) fl.checked = false;
  _sortCol = "date"; _sortDir = -1;
  applyFilters();
}
function hideAll() {
  ["transactionsSection","budgetSection","historySection","settingsPage","savings-page","dashboardSection"].forEach(id => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el) el.style.display = "none";
  });
  _setSheetScroll("free");
}
function setActiveNav(id) {
  // Bottom nav
  ["nav-tx","nav-budget","nav-history","nav-savings","nav-dashboard"].forEach(n => {
    const el = document.getElementById(n);
    if (el) el.classList.remove("active");
  });
  const active = document.getElementById(id);
  if (active) active.classList.add("active");
  // Header tabs
  const tabMap = { "nav-tx": "htab-tx", "nav-budget": "htab-budget", "nav-history": "htab-history" };
  ["htab-tx","htab-budget","htab-history"].forEach(t => {
    const el = document.getElementById(t);
    if (el) el.classList.remove("active");
  });
  const htab = document.getElementById(tabMap[id]);
  if (htab) htab.classList.add("active");
}
function _setTitle(t) {
  const el = document.getElementById("appTitle");
  if (el) el.textContent = t;
}


// Garde : bloque la navigation si des transactions sont sélectionnées
function _canNavigate() {
  if (selectedIds && selectedIds.size > 0) {
    showInfoModal(
      selectedIds.size + " transaction" + (selectedIds.size > 1 ? "s sélectionnées" : " sélectionnée") +
      " — Terminez ou annulez la sélection avant de changer d'onglet."
    );
    return false;
  }
  return true;
}
function showTransactions() {
  _hideOrderFloating();
  if (!_canNavigate()) return;
  hideAll();
  document.getElementById("transactionsSection").style.display = "block";
  setActiveNav("nav-tx");
  _setTitle("Saisie");
  document.getElementById("fabAdd").classList.remove("visible");
}
function showBudget() {
  _hideOrderFloating();
  if (!_canNavigate()) return;
  hideAll();
  _setSheetScroll("locked");
  const _bs=document.getElementById("budgetSection");_bs.style.display="flex";_bs.style.flexDirection="column";
  setActiveNav("nav-budget");
  _setTitle("Budget");
  document.getElementById("fabAdd").classList.remove("visible");
  loadPeriods(); // loadBudget() est déclenché par loadPeriods → reçoit data.disponible du GAS
}
function showHistory() {
  hideAll();
  _setSheetScroll("locked");
  const _hs=document.getElementById("historySection");_hs.style.display="flex";_hs.style.flexDirection="column";
  setActiveNav("nav-history");
  _setTitle("Banque");
  document.getElementById("fabAdd").classList.add("visible");
  // filterLocked coché par défaut à l'ouverture
  const fl = document.getElementById("filterLocked");
  if (fl && !fl._initialized) { fl.checked = true; fl._initialized = true; }
  refreshHistory(allTransactions);
  renderPrevisions();
}

// ================= INIT =================
// ===== ERREURS GLOBALES =====
// Capture toute erreur JS non gérée et l'affiche au lieu de bloquer silencieusement
window.onerror = function(msg, src, line, col, err) {
  hideSpinner();
  const _spErr = document.getElementById("splashScreen");
  if (_spErr) { _spErr.classList.add("hidden"); setTimeout(() => { if(_spErr.parentNode) _spErr.remove(); }, 400); }
  _showInitError("Erreur JS : " + msg + (line ? " (ligne " + line + ")" : ""));
  return false;
};

// ===== INIT =====
let _initTimeout = null;

function init() {
  const dateEl = document.getElementById("date");
  if (dateEl) dateEl.value = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];

  showSpinner();

  // Sécurité : si GAS ne répond pas dans 20s, on affiche une erreur
  _initTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
    hideSpinner();
    const _sp = document.getElementById("splashScreen");
    if (_sp) { _sp.classList.add("hidden"); setTimeout(() => { if(_sp.parentNode) _sp.remove(); }, 600); }
    _showInitError(
      "Timeout — Google Apps Script n'a pas répondu en 20 secondes.<br>" +
      "Causes possibles : déploiement non publié, quota GAS dépassé, " +
      "ou la feuille AppMeta / getInitialData() est absente du script."
    );
  }, 20000);

  // Vérification préventive : google.script.run disponible ?
  if (typeof google === "undefined" || typeof google.script === "undefined") {
    clearTimeout(_initTimeout);
    hideSpinner();
    _showInitError(
      "google.script.run introuvable — cette app doit être ouverte via son URL de déploiement GAS, " +
      "pas directement depuis l'éditeur ou un fichier local."
    );
    return;
  }

  try {
    _gas()
      .withSuccessHandler(data => {
        clearTimeout(_initTimeout);
        hideSpinner();
        if (!data) {
          _showInitError("La fonction getInitialData() a renvoyé une valeur vide (null).<br>Vérifie que le script est bien déployé et que la feuille Google Sheets est accessible.");
          return;
        }
        if (data._error) {
          _showInitError("Erreur dans getInitialData() : <strong>" + data._error + "</strong><br><small>Vérifie la console GAS (Extensions → Apps Script → Exécutions) pour plus de détails.</small>");
          return;
        }
        allCategories   = data.categories   || [];
        allBuckets      = data.buckets      || [];
        allDebtors      = data.debtors      || [];
        allPeriods      = data.periods      || [];
        allTransactions = _normalizeTxList(data.transactions);
        allPrevisions   = data.previsions   || [];
        allProjects     = data.projects     || [];
        _totalSavings   = data.totalSavings || 0;
        _savingsCatId   = data.savingsCatId  || _savingsCatId;
      _assignCatId    = data.assignCatId   || _assignCatId;
        historyLoaded   = true;
        computeSoldes();
        buildPeriodSelect(allPeriods);
        fillCategorySelect("simpleCategory", allCategories);
        fillCategorySelect("modalSimpleCategory", allCategories);
        fillDebtorDatalist();
        _checkUndoAvailable();
        renderSettings();
        _initAllTPE();
        _startupTab = data.startupTab || "budget";
        _applyTheme(data.theme || "dark");
        _showProgress = (data.showProgress !== "0");
        document.body.classList.toggle("hide-progress", !_showProgress);
        const _pb = document.getElementById("btnToggleProgress");
        if (_pb) _pb.classList.toggle("active", !_showProgress);
        _initPlans(data.plans || [], data.currentPlanId);
        const _sp=document.getElementById("splashScreen");
        if(_sp){_sp.classList.add("hidden");setTimeout(()=>_sp.remove(),600);}
        if (data.startupTab === "banque") showHistory();
        else if (data.startupTab === "saisie") showTransactions();
        else if (data.startupTab === "dashboard") showDashboard();
        else showBudget();
      })
      .withFailureHandler(err => {
        clearTimeout(_initTimeout);
        hideSpinner();
        const _sp = document.getElementById("splashScreen");
        if (_sp) { _sp.classList.add("hidden"); setTimeout(() => { if(_sp.parentNode) _sp.remove(); }, 600); }
        const msg = err && err.message ? err.message : String(err);
        _showInitError(
          "Erreur serveur GAS : <strong>" + msg + "</strong><br>" +
          "<small>Vérifie que la fonction getInitialData() existe dans Code.gs " +
          "et que le script est bien redéployé.</small>"
        );
      })
      .getInitialData();
  } catch(e) {
    clearTimeout(_initTimeout);
    hideSpinner();
    const _sp = document.getElementById("splashScreen");
    if (_sp) { _sp.classList.add("hidden"); setTimeout(() => { if(_sp.parentNode) _sp.remove(); }, 600); }
    _showInitError("Exception au lancement : " + e.message);
  }
}

function _showInitError(msg) {
  // Toujours cacher le splash screen si encore visible
  const _spInit = document.getElementById("splashScreen");
  if (_spInit) { _spInit.classList.add("hidden"); setTimeout(() => { if(_spInit.parentNode) _spInit.remove(); }, 400); }
  // Supprime une éventuelle erreur précédente
  const old = document.getElementById("_initErrorBanner");
  if (old) old.remove();

  const sheet = document.getElementById("mainSheet");
  if (!sheet) { alert("Erreur : " + msg); return; }

  const div = document.createElement("div");
  div.id = "_initErrorBanner";
  div.style.cssText = [
    "background:#FEE2E2", "color:#B91C1C",
    "padding:14px 16px", "border-radius:14px",
    "font-size:13px", "line-height:1.6",
    "border:1.5px solid #FECACA"
  ].join(";");
  div.innerHTML =
    "❌ <strong>Impossible de charger l'app</strong><br>" + msg +
    "<br><br>" +
    "<button onclick=\"document.getElementById('_initErrorBanner').remove();init();\" " +
    "style=\"padding:10px 18px;background:linear-gradient(90deg,#5B6CFF,#4C5BFF);" +
    "color:white;border:none;border-radius:12px;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer;\">↺ Réessayer</button>";
  sheet.prepend(div);
}

// ================= CATEGORIES =================
function fillCategorySelect(selectId, categories, selectedId) {
  const select = document.getElementById(selectId);
  select.innerHTML = "";
  categories.forEach(c => {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = c.id; opt.textContent = c.name;
    if (selectedId && c.id == selectedId) opt.selected = true;
    select.appendChild(opt);
  });
}

// ================= TOGGLE SENS =================
let currentSense = "sortie";
let modalSense   = "sortie";

let _splitMode = false;

function setSense(sense) {
  currentSense = sense;
  document.getElementById("btnSortie").className    = sense === "sortie"    ? "active-sortie"    : "";
  document.getElementById("btnEntree").className    = sense === "entree"    ? "active-entree"    : "";
  document.getElementById("btnPrevision").className = sense === "prevision" ? "active-prevision" : "";
  // Mode prévision → force simple (pas de split)
  if (sense === "prevision" && _splitMode) disableSplitMode();
  // Masquer le bouton split en mode prévision
  const splitToggleBtn = document.querySelector(".btn-split-toggle");
  if (splitToggleBtn) splitToggleBtn.style.display = sense === "prevision" ? "none" : "";
}

function enableSplitMode() {
  _splitMode = true;
  document.getElementById("simpleFormBlock").style.display = "none";
  document.getElementById("splitFormBlock").style.display  = "";
  // Copier valeurs simples vers split si déjà remplies
  const simpleAmt = document.getElementById("simpleAmount").value;
  const simpleCat = document.getElementById("simpleCategory").value;
  if (simpleAmt) document.getElementById("totalAmount").value = simpleAmt;
  if (!document.querySelectorAll("#splitLines .split-line").length) {
    addSplitLine();
    if (simpleCat) {
      const firstSelect = document.querySelector("#splitLines .split-line select");
      if (firstSelect) firstSelect.value = simpleCat;
    }
    if (simpleAmt) {
      const firstInput = document.querySelector("#splitLines .split-line input[type=number]");
      if (firstInput) { firstInput.value = simpleAmt; updateReste(); }
    }
  }
}

function disableSplitMode() {
  _splitMode = false;
  document.getElementById("simpleFormBlock").style.display = "";
  document.getElementById("splitFormBlock").style.display  = "none";
}

// setModalSense moved to openAddModal section

// ================= SPLIT LINES =================
function buildSplitLine(containerId, lineId) {
  const div = document.createElement("div");
  div.className = "split-line";
  div.id = "split-" + lineId;
  div.innerHTML = `
    <select id="splitCat-${lineId}"></select>
    <input type="text" inputmode="numeric" id="splitAmt-${lineId}" placeholder="0,00"
      oninput="${containerId === 'splitLines' ? 'updateReste' : 'updateModalReste'}()">
    <button class="btn-remove-split" onclick="removeSplitLine('${lineId}','${containerId}')">×</button>
  `;
  document.getElementById(containerId).appendChild(div);
  fillCategorySelect("splitCat-" + lineId, allCategories);
  var amtEl = document.getElementById("splitAmt-" + lineId);
  if (amtEl) _initTPE(amtEl);
  return lineId;
}

let splitCounter = 0;
function addSplitLine()      { buildSplitLine("splitLines",      "s" + splitCounter++); updateReste(); }
function addModalSplitLine() { buildSplitLine("modalSplitLines", "m" + splitCounter++); updateModalReste(); }

function removeSplitLine(lineId, containerId) {
  const el = document.getElementById("split-" + lineId);
  if (el) el.remove();
  containerId === "splitLines" ? updateReste() : updateModalReste();
}

function getSplitAmounts(containerId) {
  let total = 0;
  document.querySelectorAll(`#${containerId} .split-line`).forEach(line => {
    const id = line.id.replace("split-", "");
    total += Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("splitAmt-" + id).value) || 0);
  });
  return total;
}

function updateReste() {
  const total = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("totalAmount").value) || 0);
  const assigned = getSplitAmounts("splitLines");
  const reste = total - assigned;
  const badge = document.getElementById("resteBadge");
  badge.textContent = reste === 0 ? "✓ OK" : formatEuro(Math.abs(reste));
  badge.className = "reste-badge " + (reste === 0 ? "zero" : (reste > 0 ? "nok" : "nok"));
}

function updateModalReste() {
  const total = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("modalTotal").value) || 0);
  const assigned = getSplitAmounts("modalSplitLines");
  const reste = total - assigned;
  const badge = document.getElementById("modalResteBadge");
  badge.textContent = reste === 0 ? "✓ OK" : formatEuro(Math.abs(reste));
  badge.className = "reste-badge " + (reste === 0 ? "zero" : "nok");
}

function collectSplitLines(containerId, date, description, sense) {
  const lines = [];
  document.querySelectorAll(`#${containerId} .split-line`).forEach(line => {
    const id = line.id.replace("split-", "");
    const catId = document.getElementById("splitCat-" + id).value;
    const rawAmt = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("splitAmt-" + id).value) || 0);
    if (rawAmt > 0 && catId) {
      lines.push({
        date,
        description,
        category_id: catId,
        amount: sense === "entree" ? -rawAmt : rawAmt
      });
    }
  });
  return lines;
}

function resetSplitForm() {
  closeDebtorDropdown("debtorWrap");
  const dEl = document.getElementById("debtorInput");
  if (dEl) dEl.value = "";
  document.getElementById("description").value = "";
  document.getElementById("simpleAmount").value = "";
  document.getElementById("totalAmount").value = "";
  document.getElementById("splitLines").innerHTML = "";
  document.getElementById("resteBadge").textContent = "—";
  document.getElementById("resteBadge").className = "reste-badge nok";
  disableSplitMode();
  setSense("sortie");
}

// Effacer le formulaire de saisie (tout sauf la date) - pour saisie en chaîne
function clearForm() {
  closeDebtorDropdown("debtorWrap");
  document.getElementById("debtorInput").value = "";
  document.getElementById("description").value  = "";
  document.getElementById("simpleAmount").value = "";
  document.getElementById("totalAmount").value  = "";
  document.getElementById("splitLines").innerHTML = "";
  const badge = document.getElementById("resteBadge");
  if (badge) { badge.textContent = "—"; badge.className = "reste-badge nok"; }
  disableSplitMode();
  setSense("sortie");
  const inp = document.getElementById("debtorInput");
  if (inp) inp.focus();
}

// ================= FILE D'ATTENTE =================

function _collectCurrentForm() {
  const date   = document.getElementById("date").value;
  const desc   = document.getElementById("description").value;
  const sense  = currentSense;

  if (sense === "prevision") {
    const amt   = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("simpleAmount").value) || 0);
    const catId = document.getElementById("simpleCategory").value;
    const catName = document.getElementById("simpleCategory").options[
      document.getElementById("simpleCategory").selectedIndex]?.text || "";
    if (!amt || !catId) return null;
    return { type: "prevision", sense, date, desc, catId, catName, amount: amt, lines: null };
  }

  if (_splitMode) {
    const lines = collectSplitLines("splitLines", date, desc, sense);
    if (!lines.length) return null;
    const totalAmt = lines.reduce((s, l) => s + Math.abs(l.amount), 0);
    return { type: "transaction", sense, date, desc, catId: null, catName: "Split", amount: totalAmt, lines };
  }

  const amt   = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("simpleAmount").value) || 0);
  const catId = document.getElementById("simpleCategory").value;
  const catName = document.getElementById("simpleCategory").options[
    document.getElementById("simpleCategory").selectedIndex]?.text || "";
  if (!amt || !catId) return null;
  const amount = sense === "entree" ? -amt : amt;
  return { type: "transaction", sense, date, desc, catId, catName, amount, lines: null };
}

function addToQueue() {
  const item = _collectCurrentForm();
  if (!item) return;
  // Inclure le bénéficiaire dans l'item
  item.debtor = (document.getElementById("debtorInput")?.value || "").trim();
  _txQueue.push(item);
  resetSplitForm();
  _renderQueue();
}

function removeFromQueue(idx) {
  _txQueue.splice(idx, 1);
  _renderQueue();
}

function _renderQueue() {
  const section = document.getElementById("queueSection");
  const list    = document.getElementById("queueList");
  const count   = document.getElementById("queueCount");
  const btn     = document.getElementById("btnQueueSubmit");

  if (!_txQueue.length) {
    section.style.display = "none";
    btn.disabled = true;
    return;
  }

  section.style.display = "";
  count.textContent = _txQueue.length + " élément(s)";
  btn.disabled = false;
  list.innerHTML = "";

  _txQueue.forEach((item, idx) => {
    const div = document.createElement("div");
    div.className = `queue-item type-${item.sense}`;
    const sign = item.sense === "entree" ? "+" : item.sense === "prevision" ? "💰" : "-";
    const color = item.sense === "entree" ? "#27ae60" : item.sense === "prevision" ? "#3498db" : "#e74c3c";
    div.innerHTML = `
      <div class="queue-item-content">
        <div class="queue-item-main">
          <span class="queue-item-cat">${item.catName || "Split"}</span>
          <span class="queue-item-amt" style="color:${color}">${sign}${formatEuro(Math.abs(item.amount))}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="queue-item-meta">${item.date}${item.desc ? " · " + item.desc : ""}${item.lines ? " · " + item.lines.length + " lignes" : ""}</div>
      </div>
      <button class="queue-item-del" onclick="removeFromQueue(${idx})">✕</button>
    `;
    list.appendChild(div);
  });
}

function submitQueue() {
  if (!_txQueue.length) return;
  // Vérifier si des items ont un bénéficiaire inconnu
  const hasUnknown = _txQueue.some(item => {
    const deb = (item.debtor||'').trim();
    return deb && !allDebtors.some(d=>d.name.toLowerCase()===deb.toLowerCase());
  });
  if (hasUnknown) {
    // Passer chaque item par le flow _enqueueTx (détecte bénéficiaires inconnus)
    const items = _txQueue.splice(0);
    _renderQueue();
    items.forEach(item => {
      if (item.type === 'prevision') {
        _gas()
          .withSuccessHandler(u=>{allPrevisions=u;renderPrevisions();updateProjection();})
          .addPrevision({date:item.date,description:item.desc,category_id:item.catId,amount:item.amount});
        return;
      }
      if (item.lines) {
        const deb = (item.debtor||'').trim();
        if (deb) item.lines.forEach(l=>{l.debtor=deb;});
        const debtorKnown = !deb||allDebtors.some(d=>d.name.toLowerCase()===deb.toLowerCase());
        if (!debtorKnown) {
          _txSaveQueue.push({isSplit:true,lines:item.lines,debtor:deb,date:item.date,description:item.desc});
        } else {
          const fn=item.lines.length===1?'addTransaction':'addSplitTransaction';
          const pl=item.lines.length===1?item.lines[0]:item.lines;
          _txSaveQueue.push({isSplit:true,lines:item.lines,debtor:deb,_preKnown:true,_fn:fn,_pl:pl});
        }
        return;
      }
      _enqueueTx({date:item.date,description:item.desc,category_id:item.catId,amount:item.amount,debtor:item.debtor||''});
    });
    if (_txSaveQueue.length) setTimeout(_processNextInQueue,100);
    return;
  }
  if (!_txQueue.length) return;

  // Construire le batch (debtor inclus)
  const batchItems = _txQueue.map(item => {
    if (item.type === "prevision") {
      return { type: "prevision", form: { date: item.date, description: item.desc, category_id: item.catId, amount: item.amount } };
    }
    if (item.lines) {
      const deb = (item.debtor || '').trim();
      if (deb) item.lines.forEach(l => { l.debtor = deb; });
      return item.lines.map(l => ({ type: "transaction", form: l }));
    }
    return { type: "transaction", form: {
      date: item.date, description: item.desc,
      category_id: item.catId, amount: item.amount,
      debtor: item.debtor || ""
    }};
  }).flat();

  _txQueue = [];
  _renderQueue();
  showSpinner();

  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(result => {
      hideSpinner();
      if (result.transactions) {
        allTransactions = _normalizeTxList(result.transactions);
        historyLoaded   = true;
        computeSoldes();
        updateProjection();
        invalidateBudgetCache();
        if (typeof applyFilters === "function") applyFilters();
        _checkUndoAvailable();
      }
      if (result.previsions) {
        allPrevisions = result.previsions;
        renderPrevisions();
      }
      const msg = document.getElementById("txSuccess");
      msg.style.display = "block";
      setTimeout(() => msg.style.display = "none", 2500);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(err => {
      hideSpinner();
      console.error("submitQueue error:", err);
    })
    .addBatchTransactions(batchItems);
}

// ================= TRANSACTION SAVE =================


// ─── File d'attente transactions ────────────────────────────────
function _enqueueTx(payload) {
  var debtor = (payload.debtor || "").trim();
  var known  = !debtor || allDebtors.some(function(d){return d.name.toLowerCase()===debtor.toLowerCase();});
  if (known) {
    _doSaveSimpleTx(payload);
  } else {
    _txSaveQueue.push(payload);
    if (_txSaveQueue.length === 1) _processNextInQueue();
  }
}

function _processNextInQueue() {
  if (!_txSaveQueue.length) return;
  var payload = _txSaveQueue[0];
  var debtor = (payload.debtor || "").trim();
  var known = !debtor || allDebtors.some(function(d){return d.name.toLowerCase()===debtor.toLowerCase();});
  if (known) {
    _txSaveQueue.shift();
    if (payload.isSplit) {
      _doSaveSplitTx(payload);
    } else {
      _doSaveSimpleTx(payload);
    }
    if (_txSaveQueue.length) setTimeout(_processNextInQueue, 300);
  } else {
    _openNewDebtorSuggestModal(debtor, payload.category_id || (payload.lines && payload.lines[0] && payload.lines[0].category_id) || "");
  }
}

// ─── Gestion bénéficiaires inconnus — flux unifié ───────────────
// Une seule queue _txSaveQueue pour toutes les transactions.
// Chaque item : { payload, isSplit, debtor }  OU  mode edit via _pendingEditForm

function _showDebtorSuggestModal(name, defaultCatId) {
  var msg    = document.getElementById('newDebtorSuggestMsg');
  var remaining = _txSaveQueue.filter(function(it) {
    var d = (it.debtor || '').trim();
    return d && !allDebtors.some(function(dd){ return dd.name.toLowerCase() === d.toLowerCase(); });
  }).length;
  var extra = remaining > 1 ? ' (' + remaining + ' à traiter)' : '';
  if (msg) msg.textContent = '"' + name + '" n\'existe pas encore. Voulez-vous le créer ?' + extra;
  fillCategorySelect('newDebtorSuggestCat', allCategories);
  var catSel = document.getElementById('newDebtorSuggestCat');
  if (catSel && defaultCatId) catSel.value = defaultCatId;
  var modal = document.getElementById('newDebtorSuggestModal');
  if (modal) { modal.removeAttribute('data-mode'); modal.classList.add('active'); }
}

function _openNewDebtorSuggestModal(name, defaultCatId) {
  _showDebtorSuggestModal(name, defaultCatId);
}

function _openNewDebtorSuggestForEdit(name, defaultCatId) {
  var modal = document.getElementById('newDebtorSuggestModal');
  if (modal) modal.dataset.mode = 'edit';
  _showDebtorSuggestModal(name, defaultCatId);
}

function _newDebtorSuggestDecline() {
  var modal = document.getElementById('newDebtorSuggestModal');
  var mode  = (modal && modal.dataset.mode) || 'add';
  if (modal) { modal.removeAttribute('data-mode'); modal.classList.remove('active'); }
  if (mode === 'edit') {
    // Édition sans créer le bénéficiaire → on enregistre quand même
    var form = _pendingEditForm; _pendingEditForm = null;
    if (form) _doUpdateTransaction(form);
    return;
  }
  // Add : dépile et enregistre sans créer le bénéficiaire
  if (_txSaveQueue.length) {
    var item = _txSaveQueue.shift();
    if (item.isSplit) { _doSaveSplitTx(item); }
    else              { _doSaveSimpleTx(item); }
  }
  if (_txSaveQueue.length) setTimeout(_processNextInQueue, 300);
}

function _newDebtorSuggestConfirm() {
  var catId  = document.getElementById('newDebtorSuggestCat').value;
  var modal  = document.getElementById('newDebtorSuggestModal');
  var mode   = (modal && modal.dataset.mode) || 'add';
  if (modal) { modal.removeAttribute('data-mode'); modal.classList.remove('active'); }
  showSpinner();
  if (mode === 'edit') {
    var form = _pendingEditForm; _pendingEditForm = null;
    var debtorName = form ? (form.debtor || '') : '';
    _gas()
      .withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
        allCategories=s.categories; allBuckets=s.buckets; allDebtors=s.debtors;
        renderSettings(); fillDebtorDatalist(); _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
        hideSpinner();
        if (form) _doUpdateTransaction(form);
      })
      .withFailureHandler(function(e){ hideSpinner(); showInfoModal('Erreur: ' + e.message); })
      .addDebtor({ name: debtorName, default_category_id: catId });
    return;
  }
  // Mode add : prend le premier item de la queue pour récupérer le nom
  var item = _txSaveQueue.length ? _txSaveQueue[0] : null;
  var debtorName2 = item ? (item.debtor || '') : '';
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
      allCategories=s.categories; allBuckets=s.buckets; allDebtors=s.debtors;
      renderSettings(); fillDebtorDatalist(); _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
      hideSpinner();
      // Le bénéficiaire est maintenant connu → reprendre la queue
      setTimeout(_processNextInQueue, 150);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(e){ hideSpinner(); showInfoModal('Erreur: ' + e.message); })
    .addDebtor({ name: debtorName2, default_category_id: catId });
}

// ─── Sauvegarde transactions ─────────────────────────────────────

function _doSaveSimpleTx(payload) {
  showSpinner();
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(updated) {
      hideSpinner();
      afterMutation(_normalizeTxList(updated), 'Ajout transaction');
      // Continuer la queue si d'autres items
      if (_txSaveQueue.length) setTimeout(_processNextInQueue, 300);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(e){ hideSpinner(); showInfoModal('Erreur: ' + e.message); })
    .addTransaction(payload);
}

function _doSaveSplitTx(payload) {
  showSpinner();
  var lines = payload.lines;
  var fn  = lines.length === 1 ? 'addTransaction' : 'addSplitTransaction';
  var arg = lines.length === 1 ? lines[0] : lines;
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(updated) {
      hideSpinner();
      afterMutation(updated, 'Ajout transaction');
      if (_txSaveQueue.length) setTimeout(_processNextInQueue, 300);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(e) { hideSpinner(); showInfoModal('Erreur: ' + e.message); })
    [fn](arg);
}

function saveTransaction() {
  const date = document.getElementById('date').value;
  const desc = document.getElementById('description').value;

  // 1. PRÉVISION / REVENU ATTENDU
  if (currentSense === 'prevision') {
    const amt   = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById('simpleAmount').value) || 0);
    const catId = document.getElementById('simpleCategory').value;
    if (!amt || !catId) return;
    showSpinner();
    _gas().withSuccessHandler(function(updated) {
      hideSpinner(); allPrevisions = updated;
      resetSplitForm(); renderPrevisions(); computeSoldes(); updateProjection();
      invalidateBudgetCache();
      var bs = document.getElementById('budgetSection');
      if (bs && bs.style.display !== 'none') loadBudget(true);
      var msg = document.getElementById('txSuccess');
      if (msg) { msg.style.display = 'block'; setTimeout(function(){ msg.style.display = 'none'; }, 2500); }
    }).withFailureHandler(function(e){ hideSpinner(); showInfoModal('Erreur: ' + e.message); })
      .addPrevision({ date: date, description: desc, category_id: catId, amount: amt });
    return;
  }

  // 2. SPLIT
  if (_splitMode) {
    var splitLines = collectSplitLines('splitLines', date, desc, currentSense);
    if (!splitLines.length) return;
    var deb = ((document.getElementById('debtorInput') || {}).value || '').trim();
    if (deb) splitLines.forEach(function(l){ l.debtor = deb; });
    resetSplitForm();
    _txSaveQueue.push({ isSplit: true, lines: splitLines, debtor: deb });
    if (_txSaveQueue.length === 1) _processNextInQueue();
    return;
  }

  // 3. SIMPLE
  const amt   = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById('simpleAmount').value) || 0);
  const catId = document.getElementById('simpleCategory').value;
  if (!amt || !catId) return;
  const amount = currentSense === 'entree' ? -amt : amt;
  var debtor = ((document.getElementById('debtorInput') || {}).value || '').trim();
  var cleared = document.getElementById('txClearedBtn') ? document.getElementById('txClearedBtn').classList.contains('active-clr') : false;
  resetSplitForm();
  _enqueueTx({ date: date, description: desc, category_id: catId, amount: amount, debtor: debtor, cleared: cleared });
}

// ─── Historique transactions d'une catégorie ─────────────────────
function openCatHistory(catId, catName, period) {
  const [mo, yr] = period.split("/");
  const txs = allTransactions.filter(t => {
    const matchPeriod = t.period === period;
    const matchCat    = t.category_id === catId || t.category === catId;
    return matchPeriod && matchCat;
  }).sort((a,b) => {
    const toTs = s => {
      if (!s) return 0;
      const p = String(s).split("/");
      if (p.length === 3) return new Date(p[2],p[1]-1,p[0]);
      return new Date(s);
    };
    return toTs(b.date) - toTs(a.date);
  });

  const modal = document.getElementById("catHistoryModal");
  document.getElementById("catHistoryTitle").textContent = catName;
  document.getElementById("catHistoryPeriod").textContent = new Date(parseInt(yr), parseInt(mo)-1).toLocaleDateString("fr-FR", {month:"long", year:"numeric"});

  const total = txs.reduce((s,t) => s + Math.abs(Number(t.amount)||0), 0);
  document.getElementById("catHistoryTotal").textContent = formatEuro(total);

  const list = document.getElementById("catHistoryList");
  list.innerHTML = "";
  if (!txs.length) {
    list.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;color:#ccc;padding:32px;font-size:14px;">Aucune transaction ce mois</div>';
  } else {
    txs.forEach(t => {
      const amt = Number(t.amount)||0;
      const isNeg = amt > 0; // dépense
      const row = document.createElement("div");
      row.className = "cat-hist-row";
      const parts = t.date.split("/");
      const dayStr = parts.length===3 ? `${parts[0]}/${parts[1]}` : t.date.slice(5,10).split("-").reverse().join("/");
      const debtorStr = t.debtor ? `<span class="cat-hist-debtor">${t.debtor}</span>` : "";
      const descStr = t.description || "—";
      const hasDesc   = t.description && t.description.trim();
      const hasDebtor = t.debtor   && t.debtor.trim();
      row.innerHTML = `
        <div class="cat-hist-left">
          <span class="cat-hist-date">${dayStr}</span>
          <div class="cat-hist-desc">
            ${hasDesc   ? `<span class="cat-hist-label">${t.description.trim()}</span>` : ''}
            ${hasDebtor ? `<div class="cat-hist-payee"><span class="cat-hist-payee-icon">👤</span>${t.debtor.trim()}</div>` : ''}
            ${!hasDesc && !hasDebtor ? '<span class="cat-hist-label" style="color:#ccc;">—</span>' : ''}
          </div>
        </div>
        <span class="cat-hist-amt ${isNeg?'neg':'pos'}">${isNeg?"-":"+"} ${formatEuro(Math.abs(amt))}</span>
      `;
      list.appendChild(row);
    });
  }
  modal.classList.add("active");
}
function closeCatHistory() {
  document.getElementById("catHistoryModal").classList.remove("active");
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// RÉCONCILIATION
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function openReconcileModal() {
  // Toutes les tx pointées non verrouillées, toutes périodes
  const toReconcile = allTransactions.filter(t => t.cleared && !t.locked);
  if (!toReconcile.length) {
    showInfoModal("Aucune transaction pointée à verrouiller.");
    return;
  }
  // Solde pointé total (toutes périodes, pointées OU verrouillées)
  const soldePointe = allTransactions
    .filter(t => t.cleared || t.locked)
    .reduce((s, t) => s + (-(Number(t.amount) || 0)), 0);

  document.getElementById("reconcileSolde").textContent = formatEuro(soldePointe);
  document.getElementById("reconcileSolde").style.color = soldePointe >= 0 ? "#10B981" : "#EF4444";
  document.getElementById("reconcileInfo").textContent =
    `${toReconcile.length} transaction${toReconcile.length > 1 ? "s" : ""} pointée${toReconcile.length > 1 ? "s" : ""} vont être verrouillées.`;
  const modal = document.getElementById("reconcileModal");
  modal.classList.add("active");
  modal.onclick = function(e) { if (e.target === modal) closeReconcileModal(); };
}

function closeReconcileModal() {
  document.getElementById("reconcileModal").classList.remove("active");
}

function confirmReconcile() {
  const ids = allTransactions
    .filter(t => t.cleared && !t.locked)
    .map(t => t.id);
  if (!ids.length) { closeReconcileModal(); return; }
  closeReconcileModal();
  showSpinner();
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(updated) {
      hideSpinner();
      afterMutation(_normalizeTxList(updated), "Réconciliation");
      _checkUndoAvailable();
      _showReconcileAnim(ids.length);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) { hideSpinner(); showInfoModal("Erreur : " + err.message); })
    .reconcileTransactions(ids);
}

function _showReconcileAnim(count) {
  const overlay = document.getElementById("reconcileAnim");
  const sub = document.getElementById("reconcileAnimSub");
  if (!overlay) return;
  sub.textContent = count + " transaction" + (count > 1 ? "s" : "") + " verrouillée" + (count > 1 ? "s" : "") + " 🔒";
  overlay.classList.add("show");
  _launchConfetti();
  setTimeout(function() {
    overlay.classList.remove("show");
  }, 2800);
  overlay.onclick = function() { overlay.classList.remove("show"); };
}

function _launchConfetti() {
  var canvas = document.getElementById("confettiCanvas");
  if (!canvas) return;
  var ctx = canvas.getContext("2d");
  canvas.width = window.innerWidth;
  canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
  var particles = [];
  var colors = ["#FBD72F","#34D399","#60A5FA","#F87171","#fff","#C9A800"];
  for (var i = 0; i < 80; i++) {
    particles.push({
      x: Math.random() * canvas.width,
      y: -10 - Math.random() * 40,
      r: 3 + Math.random() * 5,
      d: Math.random() * 80,
      color: colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)],
      tilt: Math.floor(Math.random() * 10) - 10,
      tiltAngle: 0,
      tiltAngleInc: (Math.random() * 0.07) + 0.05
    });
  }
  var angle = 0, tick = 0;
  function draw() {
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
    angle += 0.01;
    tick++;
    particles.forEach(function(p, i) {
      p.tiltAngle += p.tiltAngleInc;
      p.y += (Math.cos(angle + p.d) + 1.5) * 1.8;
      p.x += Math.sin(angle) * 1.2;
      p.tilt = Math.sin(p.tiltAngle - i / 3) * 12;
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.lineWidth = p.r;
      ctx.strokeStyle = p.color;
      ctx.moveTo(p.x + p.tilt + p.r / 4, p.y);
      ctx.lineTo(p.x + p.tilt, p.y + p.tilt + p.r / 4);
      ctx.stroke();
    });
    if (tick < 120) requestAnimationFrame(draw);
    else ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
  }
  draw();
}

// closeReconcileModal au clic overlay — attaché après DOM via openReconcileModal
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _initTPE(el) {
  if (el._tpeReady) return;
  el._tpeReady  = true;
  el._tpeCents  = 0;
  el._tpeSkip   = false;

  // Au focus : lire la valeur existante, convertir en centimes
  el.addEventListener('focus', function() {
    var cur = parseFloat((el.value || '').replace(',', '.')) || 0;
    el._tpeCents = Math.round(cur * 100);
    el._tpeRender();
    setTimeout(function(){ el.setSelectionRange(el.value.length, el.value.length); }, 0);
  });

  // Rendre la valeur en "123.50"
  el._tpeRender = function() {
    el._tpeSkip = true;
    el.value = el._tpeCents > 0 ? (el._tpeCents / 100).toFixed(2) : '';
    el._tpeSkip = false;
  };

  // Desktop : intercepter keydown
  el._tpeOpMode = null; // null = pas d'opération en cours
  el._tpeOpBase = 0;
  el._tpeOpStr  = '';
  el.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
    if (e.key >= '0' && e.key <= '9') {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (el._tpeOpMode) {
        // En mode opération : accumuler le 2e opérande
        el._tpeOpStr += e.key;
        var b = el._tpeOpBase, v = parseFloat(el._tpeOpStr) || 0;
        var res = el._tpeOpMode === '+' ? b + v :
                  el._tpeOpMode === '-' ? Math.max(0, b - v) :
                  el._tpeOpMode === '*' ? b * v :
                  el._tpeOpMode === '/' && v ? b / v : b;
        el._tpeCents = Math.round(Math.min(res, 99999.99) * 100);
        el._tpeSkip = true; el.value = el._tpeOpBase.toFixed(2) + el._tpeOpMode + el._tpeOpStr; el._tpeSkip = false;
      } else {
        if (el._tpeCents < 9999999) {
          el._tpeCents = el._tpeCents * 10 + parseInt(e.key, 10);
          el._tpeRender();
          el.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
        }
      }
    } else if (e.key === '+' || e.key === '-' || e.key === '*' || e.key === '/') {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (!el._tpeOpMode) {
        el._tpeOpBase = el._tpeCents / 100;
        el._tpeOpMode = e.key;
        el._tpeOpStr  = '';
        el._tpeSkip = true; el.value = el._tpeOpBase.toFixed(2) + e.key; el._tpeSkip = false;
      }
    } else if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === 'Tab') {
      if (el._tpeOpMode && el._tpeOpStr) {
        // Confirmer l'opération
        var b = el._tpeOpBase, v = parseFloat(el._tpeOpStr) || 0;
        var res = el._tpeOpMode === '+' ? b + v :
                  el._tpeOpMode === '-' ? Math.max(0, b - v) :
                  el._tpeOpMode === '*' ? b * v :
                  el._tpeOpMode === '/' && v ? b / v : b;
        el._tpeCents = Math.round(Math.min(res, 99999.99) * 100);
        el._tpeOpMode = null; el._tpeOpStr = ''; el._tpeOpBase = 0;
        el._tpeRender();
        el.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
      }
      // laisser passer Enter/Tab
    } else if (e.key === 'Backspace') {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (el._tpeOpMode && el._tpeOpStr) {
        el._tpeOpStr = el._tpeOpStr.slice(0, -1);
        el._tpeSkip = true; el.value = el._tpeOpBase.toFixed(2) + el._tpeOpMode + el._tpeOpStr; el._tpeSkip = false;
      } else if (el._tpeOpMode && !el._tpeOpStr) {
        // Annuler l'opérateur
        el._tpeOpMode = null; el._tpeOpStr = ''; el._tpeOpBase = 0;
        el._tpeRender();
      } else {
        el._tpeCents = Math.floor(el._tpeCents / 10);
        el._tpeRender();
        el.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
      }
    } else if (e.key === 'Escape') {
      if (el._tpeOpMode) {
        el._tpeOpMode = null; el._tpeOpStr = ''; el._tpeOpBase = 0;
        el._tpeRender();
      }
    } else {
      e.preventDefault(); // bloquer lettres, virgule, etc.
    }
  });

  // Mobile : l'événement input arrive avec les chiffres déjà insérés
  el.addEventListener('input', function() {
    if (el._tpeSkip) return;
    var digits = el.value.replace(/[^0-9]/g, '').slice(-7);
    el._tpeCents = digits ? parseInt(digits, 10) : 0;
    el._tpeRender();
  });
}

function _tpeSet(id, numericValue) {
  var el = document.getElementById(id);
  if (!el) return;
  var v = parseFloat(numericValue) || 0;
  el._tpeCents = Math.round(v * 100);
  el.value = el._tpeCents > 0 ? (el._tpeCents / 100).toFixed(2) : '';
  if (!el._tpeReady) _initTPE(el);
}

function _initAllTPE() {
  ['simpleAmount','totalAmount','modalSimpleAmount','modalTotal',
   'prevModalAmount','editModalAmt'].forEach(function(id) {
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el) _initTPE(el);
  });
}

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function _budgetFocus(el) {
  var raw = el.value.replace(/ /g,'').replace(/\s/g,'').replace(',','.').replace(/[^0-9.-]/g,'');
  el._baseValue = parseFloat(raw) || 0;
  el.value = el._baseValue || '';
  el.select();
}
function _budgetBlur(el) {
  if (el._bcpActive) return;
  var raw = el.value.replace(/ /g,'').replace(/\s/g,'').replace(',','.').replace(/[^0-9.-]/g,'');
  var v = parseFloat(raw) || 0;
  v = Math.round(v * 100) / 100;
  el.value = _fmtBudgetVal(v);
  if (v !== (el._baseValue !== undefined ? el._baseValue : 0)) saveBudget(el.dataset.period, el.dataset.catid, v);
  el._baseValue = undefined;
}

function _bcpOpenFromBtn(btn) {
  var el = btn.previousElementSibling; // l'input juste avant le bouton
  if (!el || !el.classList.contains('budget-input')) return;
  var raw = el.value.replace(/\u00a0/g,'').replace(/\s/g,'').replace(',','.').replace(/[^0-9.-]/g,'');
  el._baseValue = parseFloat(raw) || 0;
  _bcpOpen(el);
}

var _bcpEl = null;
var _bcpOp_ = '=';
var _bcpInput = '';

function _bcpOpen(el) {
  _bcpEl = el;
  el._bcpActive = true;
  _bcpOp_ = '=';
  _bcpInput = '';
  document.getElementById('bcpDisplay').textContent = _bcpFmt(el._baseValue || 0);
  document.getElementById('bcpDisplay').style.color = '#FBD72F';
  document.querySelectorAll('.bcp-op').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('selected'); });
  var defBtn = document.querySelector('.bcp-op[data-op="="]');
  if (defBtn) defBtn.classList.add('selected');
  var pad = document.getElementById('budgetCalcPad');
  pad.classList.add('visible');
  var rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
  var padW = 214;
  var left = Math.min(rect.left, window.innerWidth - padW - 8);
  var top  = rect.bottom + 6;
  if (top + 360 > window.innerHeight) top = Math.max(8, rect.top - 366);
  pad.style.left = Math.max(8, left) + 'px';
  pad.style.top  = Math.max(8, top)  + 'px';
}

function _bcpClose() {
  document.getElementById('budgetCalcPad').classList.remove('visible');
  if (_bcpEl) { _bcpEl._bcpActive = false; _bcpEl = null; }
  _bcpOp_ = '='; _bcpInput = '';
}

function _bcpFmt(n) {
  return n.toLocaleString('fr-FR', {minimumFractionDigits:2, maximumFractionDigits:2}) + ' €';
}

function _bcpCompute(base, op, val) {
  if (op === '+') return base + val;
  if (op === '-') return Math.max(0, base - val);
  if (op === '*') return base * val;
  if (op === '/') return val !== 0 ? base / val : base;
  return val || base; // '='
}

function _bcpRefreshDisplay() {
  var base = _bcpEl ? (_bcpEl._baseValue || 0) : 0;
  var disp = document.getElementById('bcpDisplay');
  if (_bcpOp_ === '=' || !_bcpInput) {
    disp.textContent = _bcpInput ? _bcpInput + ' €' : _bcpFmt(base);
    disp.style.color = '#FBD72F';
  } else {
    var val = parseFloat(_bcpInput) || 0;
    var res = _bcpCompute(base, _bcpOp_, val);
    var opL = {'+':'+', '-':'−', '*':'×', '/':'÷'}[_bcpOp_] || _bcpOp_;
    disp.textContent = opL + ' ' + _bcpInput + ' = ' + _bcpFmt(res);
    disp.style.color = res > base ? '#10B981' : res < base ? '#FF6B6B' : '#FBD72F';
  }
}

function _bcpOp(op) {
  _bcpOp_ = op;
  _bcpInput = '';
  document.querySelectorAll('.bcp-op').forEach(function(b){ b.classList.remove('selected'); });
  var btn = document.querySelector('.bcp-op[data-op="' + op + '"]');
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('selected');
  _bcpRefreshDisplay();
}

function _bcpDigit(d) {
  if (_bcpInput.length >= 9) return;
  if (d === '.' && _bcpInput.includes('.')) return;
  if (d !== '.' && !_bcpInput && d === '0') return;
  _bcpInput += d;
  _bcpRefreshDisplay();
}

function _bcpDel() {
  _bcpInput = _bcpInput.slice(0, -1);
  _bcpRefreshDisplay();
}

function _bcpConfirm() {
  if (!_bcpEl) { _bcpClose(); return; }
  var base = _bcpEl._baseValue || 0;
  var val  = parseFloat(_bcpInput) || 0;
  var v    = _bcpCompute(base, _bcpOp_, val);
  v = Math.round(v * 100) / 100;
  var el = _bcpEl;
  _bcpClose();
  el.value = _fmtBudgetVal(v);
  if (v !== base) saveBudget(el.dataset.period, el.dataset.catid, v);
  el._baseValue = undefined;
}

document.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
  var pad = document.getElementById('budgetCalcPad');
  if (pad && pad.classList.contains('visible') && !pad.contains(e.target) && e.target !== _bcpEl) {
    _bcpClose();
  }
}, true);
document.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e) {
  var pad = document.getElementById('budgetCalcPad');
  if (pad && pad.classList.contains('visible') && !pad.contains(e.target) && e.target !== _bcpEl) {
    _bcpClose();
  }
}, true);

function _fmtBudgetVal(v){var s=String(v).trim().replace(/\u00a0/g,"").replace(/ /g,"").replace(",",".").replace(/[^0-9.-]/g,"");var n=parseFloat(s)||0;return n.toLocaleString("fr-FR",{minimumFractionDigits:2,maximumFractionDigits:2})+" €";}

function _editDebtorTyping() {
  const dd    = document.getElementById("editDebtorWrapDropdown");
  const input = document.getElementById("editDebtorInput");
  if (!dd) return;
  dd.dataset.catSelect = "";
  dd.classList.add("open");
  _renderDebtorOptions("editDebtorWrap", input);
}
// ================= BUDGET =================
function buildPeriodSelect(periods) {
  const select = document.getElementById("periodSelect");
  select.innerHTML = "";
  const now = new Date();
  const mm = String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, "0");
  const currentPeriod = `${mm}/${now.getFullYear()}`;
  periods.forEach(p => {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = p.id; opt.textContent = p.label;
    if (p.id === currentPeriod) opt.selected = true;
    select.appendChild(opt);
  });
}

function loadPeriods() {
  if (allPeriods.length > 0) { buildPeriodSelect(allPeriods); loadBudget(); return; }
  showSpinner();
  _gas().withSuccessHandler(data => {
    allPeriods = data; buildPeriodSelect(data); loadBudget();
  }).getPeriods();
}

let _budgetCache = {};
const BUDGET_CACHE_TTL = 30000;

// ── Disponible à assigner — variables cross-périodes ──
window._budgetPeriodTotals   = {}; // {period: grandAssigned} pour toutes les périodes visitées
window._budgetSummaryLoaded  = false;

// Convertit "MM/YYYY" en clé numérique comparable (YYYY*100+MM)
function _periodKey(p) {
  const parts = (p || "").split("/");
  if (parts.length !== 2) return 0;
  return parseInt(parts[1]) * 100 + parseInt(parts[0]);
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// Formule "À assigner" correcte :
//
//   disponible(P) = min(0,  totalAssigner  −  assignéCumulé(P))
//
//   • totalAssigner    = somme de TOUTES les transactions dont la
//       catégorie correspond à la catégorie "À assigner"
//       (amount < 0 = entrée, toutes périodes confondues)
//       → l'argent réel possédé, sans limite temporelle
//
//   • assignéCumulé(P) = somme des budgets assignés dans
//       TOUTES les périodes ≤ P
//       → une assignation future consomme l'argent dès maintenant
//
//   • min(0, …)  → si surplus positif : affiche 0
//       (l'argent existe mais est déjà réservé, rien à assigner ici)
//     → le déficit (négatif) apparaît UNIQUEMENT au mois où
//       le total assigné dépasse pour la première fois les revenus
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function computeDisponibleFrontend(period) {
  if (!period) return 0;

  // 1. Convertit "MM/YYYY" en nombre (ex: 202602)
  function pToNum(p) {
    if (!p) return 0;
    const parts = p.split("/");
    if (parts.length === 2) return parseInt(parts[1], 10) * 100 + parseInt(parts[0], 10);
    return 0;
  }
  const targetKey = pToNum(period);

  // 2. Trouve l'ID de la catégorie "À assigner"
  const assignerCat = allCategories.find(c => (c.name || "").trim().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, " ") === "à assigner");

  // 3. Calcul des entrées jusqu'au mois affiché UNIQUEMENT
  let totalEntreesJusquaMois = 0;
  if (assignerCat) {
    allTransactions.forEach(t => {
      const n = Number(t.amount) || 0;
      if (n >= 0) return; // On ignore les dépenses
      
      const matchById   = t.category_id && String(t.category_id) === String(assignerCat.id);
      const matchByName = t.category && t.category.trim().toLowerCase() === "à assigner";
      
      if (matchById || matchByName) {
        let tKey = 0;
        if (t.date) {
          const parts = t.date.split("-"); // Si date au format YYYY-MM-DD
          if (parts.length >= 2) {
            tKey = parseInt(parts[0], 10) * 100 + parseInt(parts[1], 10);
          } else {
            const p2 = t.date.split("/"); // Si date au format DD/MM/YYYY
            if (p2.length === 3) tKey = parseInt(p2[2], 10) * 100 + parseInt(p2[1], 10);
          }
        }
        if (tKey > 0 && tKey <= targetKey) {
          totalEntreesJusquaMois += Math.abs(n);
        }
      }
    });
  }

  // 4. Calcul de l'argent budgété
  let totalAssigneJusquaMois = 0;
  let totalAssigneGlobal = 0;

  // window._budgetPeriodTotals contient le budget assigné de chaque mois
  Object.entries(window._budgetPeriodTotals).forEach(([p, total]) => {
    const amt = Number(total) || 0;
    const bKey = pToNum(p);
    if (bKey > 0) {
      totalAssigneGlobal += amt; // Total de tout ce qui est budgété (passé, présent, futur)
      if (bKey <= targetKey) {
        totalAssigneJusquaMois += amt; // Total budgété jusqu'à ce mois-ci
      }
    }
  });

  // 5. TA LOGIQUE YNAB PARFAITE
  let disponible = 0;

  if (totalEntreesJusquaMois > totalAssigneGlobal) {
    disponible = totalEntreesJusquaMois - totalAssigneGlobal;
  } else if (totalEntreesJusquaMois === totalAssigneGlobal) {
    disponible = 0;
  } else if (totalEntreesJusquaMois < totalAssigneGlobal && totalEntreesJusquaMois >= totalAssigneJusquaMois) {
    disponible = 0;
  } else {
    disponible = totalEntreesJusquaMois - totalAssigneJusquaMois;
  }

  return disponible;
}



function invalidateBudgetCache(period) {
  if (period) delete _budgetCache[period]; else _budgetCache = {};
}

function loadBudget(force) {
  const period = document.getElementById("periodSelect").value;
  if (!period) return;
  // Reset batch
  if (_batchChanges && Object.keys(_batchChanges).length > 0) {
    _batchChanges = {};
    document.getElementById("budgetBatchBar").classList.remove("visible");
  }
  // Reset dépassement
  if (_depassementActive) {
    _depassementActive = false;
    const btn = document.getElementById("btnDepassement");
    if (btn) { btn.className = "btn-depassement"; btn.title = "Afficher les dépassements"; }
  }
  // Cache
  const cached = _budgetCache[period];
  if (!force && cached && (Date.now() - cached.ts) < BUDGET_CACHE_TTL) {
    _saveBucketStates();
    renderBudget(cached.buckets, period, cached.disponible);
    return;
  }
  showSpinner();
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(data => {
      hideSpinner();
      _saveBucketStates();
      _budgetCache[period] = { disponible: data.disponible, buckets: data.buckets, ts: Date.now() };
      renderBudget(data.buckets, period, data.disponible);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(err => {
      hideSpinner();
      showInfoModal("Erreur chargement budget : " + (err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)));
    })
    .getBudgetByPeriod(period);
}

function renderDisponible(val) {
  const card  = document.getElementById("disponibleCard");
  const value = document.getElementById("disponibleValue");
  card.style.display = "flex";
  card.className = "disponible-card " + (val >= 0 ? "pos" : "neg");
  value.textContent = formatEuro(val);
}

let _budgetCollapsed = {};
function _saveBucketStates() {
  _budgetCollapsed = {};
  document.querySelectorAll(".bucket-header").forEach(h => {
    if (h.dataset.bucket) _budgetCollapsed[h.dataset.bucket] = h.classList.contains("collapsed");
  });
}
function _restoreBucketStates() {
  Object.entries(_budgetCollapsed).forEach(([id, collapsed]) => {
    const h = document.querySelector(`.bucket-header[data-bucket="${id}"]`);
    if (!h) return;
    const arrow = h.querySelector(".bucket-toggle");
    if (collapsed) {
      h.classList.add("collapsed");
      if (arrow) arrow.style.transform = "rotate(-90deg)";
      document.querySelectorAll(`tr.cat-row[data-bucket="${id}"], tr.cat-hidden-row[data-bucket="${id}"]`).forEach(r => r.style.display = "none");
    } else {
      h.classList.remove("collapsed");
      if (arrow) arrow.style.transform = "";
      document.querySelectorAll(`tr.cat-row[data-bucket="${id}"], tr.cat-hidden-row[data-bucket="${id}"]`).forEach(r => r.style.display = "");
    }
  });
}

// ── Drag & Drop catégories dans l'onglet Budget ──
var _budDragSrc = null;
var _budDragBucketId = null;

function _getBudgetCatRows(tbody, bucketId) {
  return [...tbody.querySelectorAll("tr.cat-row[data-bucket-id='" + bucketId + "']")];
}

var _budDragAllowed = false;

function _attachBudgetCatDrag(row, tbody, bucketId) {
  row.dataset.bucketId = bucketId;
  var handle = row.querySelector(".cat-drag-handle");

  // Autoriser le drag seulement depuis la poignée
  if (handle) {
    handle.addEventListener("mousedown", function() { _budDragAllowed = true; });
    handle.addEventListener("mouseup",   function() { _budDragAllowed = false; });
  }
  document.addEventListener("mouseup", function() { _budDragAllowed = false; }, { passive: true });

  // ── Desktop ──
  row.addEventListener("dragstart", function(e) {
    if (!_budDragAllowed) { e.preventDefault(); return; }
    _budDragSrc = row;
    _budDragBucketId = bucketId;
    row.classList.add("budget-dragging");
    e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = "move";
  });

  row.addEventListener("dragend", function() {
    row.classList.remove("budget-dragging");
    tbody.querySelectorAll(".budget-drag-over").forEach(function(r) { r.classList.remove("budget-drag-over"); });
    _budDragSrc = null; _budDragBucketId = null;
  });

  row.addEventListener("dragover", function(e) {
    if (_budDragBucketId !== bucketId) return;
    e.preventDefault();
  });

  row.addEventListener("dragenter", function() {
    if (_budDragSrc && _budDragSrc !== row && _budDragBucketId === bucketId)
      row.classList.add("budget-drag-over");
  });

  row.addEventListener("dragleave", function() {
    row.classList.remove("budget-drag-over");
  });

  row.addEventListener("drop", function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    row.classList.remove("budget-drag-over");
    if (!_budDragSrc || _budDragSrc === row || _budDragBucketId !== bucketId) return;
    // Déplacer dans le DOM
    var rows = _getCatRowsForBucket(tbody, bucketId);
    var fromIdx = rows.indexOf(_budDragSrc);
    var toIdx   = rows.indexOf(row);
    if (fromIdx < toIdx) row.after(_budDragSrc);
    else                  row.before(_budDragSrc);
    _saveBudgetCatOrder(tbody, bucketId);
  });

  // ── Touch : long press sur la poignée ──
  var _tTimer = null, _tStartY = 0, _tClone = null;

  function _tStart(e) {
    _tStartY = e.touches[0].clientY;
    _tTimer = setTimeout(function() {
      _budDragSrc = row; _budDragBucketId = bucketId;
      row.classList.add("budget-dragging");
      _tClone = row.cloneNode(true);
      _tClone.style.cssText = "position:fixed;z-index:9999;width:" + row.offsetWidth + "px;opacity:0.85;pointer-events:none;background:var(--card,#fff);box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.18);";
      var r = row.getBoundingClientRect();
      _tClone.style.left = r.left + "px"; _tClone.style.top = r.top + "px";
      document.body.appendChild(_tClone);
      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(40);
    }, 400);
  }

  function _tMove(e) {
    if (!_budDragSrc) {
      if (Math.abs(e.touches[0].clientY - _tStartY) > 10) { clearTimeout(_tTimer); _tTimer = null; }
      return;
    }
    e.preventDefault();
    var y = e.touches[0].clientY;
    if (_tClone) _tClone.style.top = (y - row.offsetHeight / 2) + "px";
    var rows = _getCatRowsForBucket(tbody, bucketId);
    rows.forEach(function(r) { r.classList.remove("budget-drag-over"); });
    var target = rows.find(function(r) {
      if (r === _budDragSrc) return false;
      var rect = r.getBoundingClientRect();
      return y >= rect.top && y <= rect.bottom;
    });
    if (target) target.classList.add("budget-drag-over");
  }

  function _tEnd(e) {
    clearTimeout(_tTimer); _tTimer = null;
    if (_tClone) { document.body.removeChild(_tClone); _tClone = null; }
    if (!_budDragSrc) return;
    row.classList.remove("budget-dragging");
    var y = e.changedTouches[0].clientY;
    var rows = _getCatRowsForBucket(tbody, bucketId);
    rows.forEach(function(r) { r.classList.remove("budget-drag-over"); });
    var target = rows.find(function(r) {
      if (r === _budDragSrc) return false;
      var rect = r.getBoundingClientRect();
      return y >= rect.top && y <= rect.bottom;
    });
    if (target) {
      var fromIdx = rows.indexOf(_budDragSrc), toIdx = rows.indexOf(target);
      if (fromIdx < toIdx) target.after(_budDragSrc);
      else                  target.before(_budDragSrc);
      _saveBudgetCatOrder(tbody, bucketId);
    }
    _budDragSrc = null; _budDragBucketId = null;
  }

  if (handle) {
    handle.addEventListener("touchstart", _tStart, { passive: true });
    handle.addEventListener("touchmove",  _tMove,  { passive: false });
    handle.addEventListener("touchend",   _tEnd,   { passive: true });
  }
}

function _getCatRowsForBucket(tbody, bucketId) {
  return [...tbody.querySelectorAll("tr.cat-row[data-bucket-id='" + bucketId + "']")];
}

function _saveBudgetCatOrder(tbody, bucketId) {
  var ids = _getCatRowsForBucket(tbody, bucketId).map(function(r) { return r.dataset.catId; });
  if (!ids.length) return;
  _showOrderFloating("cat");
  // Stocker les ids en attente pour quand on clique Enregistrer
  window._pendingCatOrder = ids;
}

// Surcharger _saveCatOrderNow pour tenir compte du contexte budget
var _origSaveCatOrderNow = null;
function _saveCatOrderNow() {
  var ids;
  if (window._pendingCatOrder && window._pendingCatOrder.length) {
    ids = window._pendingCatOrder;
  } else {
    var cont = document.getElementById("categoriesSettingsList2");
    if (!cont) return;
    ids = [...cont.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-cat-draggable[data-id]")].map(function(el) { return el.dataset.id; });
  }
  if (!ids.length) return;
  var floatEl = document.getElementById("orderSaveFloating");
  if (floatEl) { floatEl.style.pointerEvents = "none"; floatEl.textContent = "⏳ Sauvegarde..."; }
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
      allCategories = s.categories; allBuckets = s.buckets; allDebtors = s.debtors;
      _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
      invalidateBudgetCache(); loadBudget(true);
      _hideOrderFloating();
      window._pendingCatOrder = null;
      // Re-render settings si on est dessus
      if (document.getElementById("settings-panel-categories") &&
          document.getElementById("settings-panel-categories").style.display !== "none") {
        switchSettingsTab("categories");
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function() {
      var floatEl = document.getElementById("orderSaveFloating");
      if (floatEl) { floatEl.textContent = "⚠️ Réessayer"; floatEl.style.pointerEvents = "auto"; }
    })
    .reorderCategories(ids);
}

function renderBudget(data, period, serverDisponible) {
  const container = document.getElementById("budgetContainer");
  container.innerHTML = "";

  // Table globale
  const table = document.createElement("table");
  table.className = "budget-table";

  // En-tête colonnes
  table.innerHTML = `
    <thead>
      <tr>
        <th style="text-align:left;">Catégorie</th>
        <th>Assigné</th>
        <th>Dépensé</th>
        <th title="Σ(Assigné − Dépensé) des périodes précédentes.&#10;Positif = surplus antérieur qui vient augmenter ton Restant.&#10;Négatif = déficit antérieur qui réduit ton Restant.&#10;Non affecté par les dépenses du mois en cours." style="cursor:help;">Report ↩ ℹ</th>
        <th title="Assigné − Dépensé + Report&#10;Ce que tu peux encore dépenser en tenant compte des reports." style="cursor:help;">Restant</th>
      </tr>
    </thead>
    <tbody id="budgetTbody"></tbody>
  `;
  container.appendChild(table);
  const tbody = table.querySelector("#budgetTbody");
  const tfoot = document.createElement("tfoot");
  table.appendChild(tfoot);

  let grandAssigned = 0, grandSpent = 0, grandCarry = 0, grandRemaining = 0;

  data.forEach((bucket, bIdx) => {
    // Masquer le bucket système "To Assign" / "Non assigné"
    const _bucketNameLow = (bucket.bucket_name || "").toLowerCase().trim();
    if (_bucketNameLow === "to assign" || _bucketNameLow === "non assigné" ||
        _bucketNameLow === "non assigne" || _bucketNameLow === "à assigner") return;

    const bucketId = "bucket-" + bIdx;

    // Totaux bucket
    let totalAssigned = 0, totalSpent = 0, totalCarry = 0, totalRemaining = 0;
    bucket.categories.forEach(cat => {
      totalAssigned  += cat.budgeted;
      totalSpent     += cat.spent;
      totalCarry     += (cat.carry || 0);
      totalRemaining += cat.remaining;
    });
    grandAssigned  += totalAssigned;
    grandSpent     += totalSpent;
    grandCarry     += totalCarry;
    grandRemaining += totalRemaining;

    // Header bucket (cliquable) avec totaux intégrés
    const _bTot = totalAssigned;
    const _rTot = totalRemaining;
    let availClass;
    if (_rTot < 0)                availClass = "amt-neg";
    else if (_rTot === 0)          availClass = "amt-zero";
    else if (_bTot > 0 && (_rTot/_bTot) < 0.15) availClass = "amt-warn";
    else                           availClass = "amt-ok";
    const headerRow = document.createElement("tr");
    headerRow.className = "bucket-header";
    headerRow.dataset.bucket = bucketId;
    headerRow.innerHTML = `
      <td><span class="bucket-toggle">▼</span>${bucket.bucket_name}</td>
      <td>${formatEuro(totalAssigned)}</td>
      <td>${formatEuro(totalSpent)}</td>
      <td class="${totalCarry < 0 ? 'amt-neg' : totalCarry > 0 ? 'amt-ok' : 'amt-zero'}">${formatEuro(totalCarry)}</td>
      <td class="${availClass}">${formatEuro(totalRemaining)}</td>
    `;
    headerRow.addEventListener("click", () => toggleBucket(bucketId, headerRow));
    tbody.appendChild(headerRow);

    // Lignes catégories
    bucket.categories.forEach(cat => {
      if (cat.category_id === "CAT001" ||
          (cat.name || "").trim().toLowerCase() === "à assigner") return;
      // Masquer les catégories inactives uniquement si budgeted=0 et remaining=0
      const _catMeta = allCategories.find(ac => ac.id === cat.category_id);
      if (_catMeta && _catMeta.active === false &&
          Number(cat.budgeted) === 0 && Number(cat.remaining) === 0) return;
      const isOver      = Number(cat.remaining) < 0;
      // Code couleur 3 niveaux : rouge < 0, orange 0..20% du budget, vert > 20%
      const _bud = Number(cat.budgeted);
      const _rem = Number(cat.remaining);
      let availClass;
      if (_rem < 0)               availClass = "amt-neg";   // dépassement → rouge
      else if (_rem === 0)         availClass = "amt-zero";  // pile à 0 → gris
      else if (_bud > 0 && (_rem / _bud) < 0.20) availClass = "amt-warn"; // < 20% → orange
      else                         availClass = "amt-ok";    // confortable → vert
      const canTransfer = cat.remaining > 0;
      const catRow = document.createElement("tr");
      catRow.className = "cat-row" + (isOver ? " over-budget" : "");
      catRow.dataset.bucket   = bucketId;
      catRow.dataset.catId    = cat.category_id;
      catRow.dataset.spent    = cat.spent;
      catRow.dataset.budgeted = cat.budgeted;
      catRow.dataset.isOver   = isOver ? "1" : "0";   // pour le filtre

      // On enregistre les données du budget courant pour le modal transfert
      const catJson = JSON.stringify(cat).replace(/'/g,"&#39;");
      const canTransferStr = canTransfer ? "1" : "0";

      catRow.draggable = true;
      catRow.dataset.bucketName = bucket.bucket_name || "";
      // Barre de progression — capacité réelle = assigné + report
      const _capacity = _bud + (Number(cat.carry) || 0);
      const _pct = _capacity > 0 ? Math.min(100, Math.round((Number(cat.spent) / _capacity) * 100)) : (_rem < 0 ? 100 : 0);
      let _barColor;
      if (_rem < 0)        _barColor = 'var(--red)';    // dépassement → rouge
      else if (_pct >= 90) _barColor = '#E67E22';        // > 90% → orange vif
      else if (_pct >= 70) _barColor = '#F39C12';        // > 70% → orange doux
      else                 _barColor = 'var(--green)';   // confortable → vert
      const _carryVal = cat.carry || 0;
      const _carrySign = _carryVal > 0 ? '+' : '';

      catRow.innerHTML = `
        <td class="cat-name">
          <span class="cat-drag-handle" title="Maintenir pour déplacer">⠿</span>
          <span class="cat-name-link" onclick="event.stopPropagation();openBudgetCatModal('${cat.category_id}','${period}')" style="cursor:pointer;">${cat.category_name}</span>
          <button class="cat-note-btn${cat.note ? ' has-note' : ''}" onclick="event.stopPropagation();_toggleCatNote(this,'${cat.category_id}','${period}')" title="${cat.note ? cat.note.replace(/"/g,'&quot;') : 'Ajouter une note'}">💬</button>
          <div class="cat-progress-bar"><div class="cat-progress-fill" style="width:${_pct}%;background:${_barColor};"></div></div>
        </td>
        <td onclick="event.stopPropagation()" style="white-space:nowrap">
          <input class="budget-input" type="text" inputmode="decimal"
            data-period="${period}" data-catid="${cat.category_id}"
            value="${_fmtBudgetVal(cat.budgeted)}"
            onfocus="_budgetFocus(this)"
            onblur="_budgetBlur(this)"
            onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter'){this.blur();}"
            onclick="event.stopPropagation()"><button class="bcp-trigger" onclick="event.stopPropagation();_bcpOpenFromBtn(this)" title="Calculatrice">⊕</button>
        </td>
        <td class="amt-spent amt-spent-link" onclick="openCatHistory('${cat.category_id}','${cat.category_name}','${period}')" title="Voir les transactions">
          <span class="cat-badge cat-badge-spent">${formatEuro(cat.spent)}</span>
        </td>
        <td class="${_carryVal < 0 ? 'amt-neg' : _carryVal > 0 ? 'amt-ok' : 'amt-zero'}">
          ${_carryVal !== 0 ? `<span class="cat-badge cat-badge-carry ${_carryVal < 0 ? 'neg' : 'pos'}">${_carrySign}${formatEuro(_carryVal)}</span>` : '<span style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:13px;">—</span>'}
        </td>
        <td class="${availClass} amt-avail${(canTransfer || cat.remaining < 0) ? ' td-avail-click' : ''}"
            title="${canTransfer ? 'Cliquer pour transférer ce disponible' : (cat.remaining < 0 ? 'Cliquer pour compenser ce dépassement' : '')}"
            ${(canTransfer || cat.remaining < 0) ? `onclick="event.stopPropagation(); openTransfertFromRow(this)"` : ""}
            data-cat='${catJson}'
            data-period="${period}"
        ><span class="cat-badge cat-badge-rem ${availClass}">${formatEuro(cat.remaining)}</span></td>
      `;
      _attachBudgetCatDrag(catRow, tbody, bucket.bucket_id);
      tbody.appendChild(catRow);
    });

    // Bandeau catégories masquées pour ce groupe
    const hiddenCats = bucket.categories.filter(cat => {
      if (cat.category_id === "CAT001") return false;
      const _m = allCategories.find(ac => ac.id === cat.category_id);
      return _m && _m.active === false && Number(cat.budgeted) === 0 && Number(cat.remaining) === 0;
    });
    if (hiddenCats.length) {
      const hiddenRow = document.createElement("tr");
      hiddenRow.className = "cat-hidden-row";
      hiddenRow.dataset.bucket = bucketId;
      hiddenRow.innerHTML = `<td colspan="5" style="padding:6px 14px 8px;"><button class="btn-show-hidden" onclick="event.stopPropagation();_toggleHiddenCats(this,'${bucketId}','${period}')">👁 ${hiddenCats.length} catégorie${hiddenCats.length>1?'s':''} masquée${hiddenCats.length>1?'s':''}</button></td>`;
      // Stocker les ids masquées pour les afficher au clic
      hiddenRow.dataset.hiddenIds = JSON.stringify(hiddenCats.map(c => c.category_id));
      tbody.appendChild(hiddenRow);
    }
  });

  // Stocker pour la projection + pour le transfert
  window._budgetPeriodAssigned = grandAssigned;
  window._budgetPeriodSpent    = grandSpent;
  window._budgetGrandCarry     = grandCarry;
  window._lastBudgetData       = data;
  // Détails par catégorie pour le calcul du reste à dépenser
  window._budgetCatDetails = data.flatMap(b => b.categories);
  window._budgetCatPeriod  = period;
  // Pré-charger les notes dans le cache local
  _preloadBudgetNotes(data, period);
  // Mémoriser le total assigné pour ce mois (calcul cross-périodes du disponible)
  window._budgetPeriodTotals[period] = grandAssigned;
  // Disponible = toujours la valeur calculée par le serveur (logique exacte)
  renderDisponible(typeof serverDisponible === "number" ? serverDisponible : 0);
  updateProjection();

  // Alerte dépassements
  const overBudgetCats = [];
  data.forEach(bucket => {
    bucket.categories.forEach(cat => {
      if (cat.category_id === "CAT001") return;
      if (Number(cat.remaining) < 0) overBudgetCats.push(cat.name || "?");
    });
  });
  const alertEl = document.getElementById("budgetOverAlert");
  if (alertEl) {
    if (overBudgetCats.length > 0) {
      const names = overBudgetCats.join(", ");
      alertEl.innerHTML =
        `<span style="margin-right:8px;">⚠️ ${overBudgetCats.length} catégorie(s) en dépassement : <em>${names}</em></span>` +
        `<span style="font-size:12px;opacity:.75;margin-left:auto;white-space:nowrap;">Cliquer pour filtrer →</span>`;
      alertEl.style.display = "flex";
      alertEl.style.alignItems = "center";
      alertEl.onclick = () => {
        // Active le filtre dépassements si pas déjà actif
        if (!_depassementActive) toggleDepassement();
        // Scroll vers le premier dépassement
        const firstOver = document.querySelector("tr.cat-row[data-is-over='1']");
        if (firstOver) firstOver.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth", block: "center" });
      };
      alertEl.title = "Cliquer pour afficher uniquement les dépassements";
    } else {
      alertEl.style.display = "none";
      alertEl.onclick = null;
      // Si le filtre dépassement était actif et plus aucun dépassement, le désactiver
      if (_depassementActive) toggleDepassement();
    }
  }

  // Ligne grand total (utilise le tfoot créé au début)
  const _gRem2 = grandRemaining;
  let _gClass2;
  if (_gRem2 < 0)                                           _gClass2 = "amt-neg";
