  else if (_gRem2 === 0)                                    _gClass2 = "amt-zero";
  else if (grandAssigned > 0 && (_gRem2/grandAssigned) < 0.15) _gClass2 = "amt-warn";
  else                                                      _gClass2 = "amt-ok";

  const gtRow = document.createElement("tr");
  gtRow.className = "budget-grand-total";
  gtRow.innerHTML = `
    <td>Total période</td>
    <td>${formatEuro(grandAssigned)}</td>
    <td>${formatEuro(grandSpent)}</td>
    <td class="${grandCarry < 0 ? 'amt-neg' : grandCarry > 0 ? 'amt-ok' : 'amt-zero'}">${formatEuro(grandCarry)}</td>
    <td class="${_gClass2}">${formatEuro(grandRemaining)}</td>
  `;
  (tfoot || tbody).appendChild(gtRow);

  // Carte récap Dépensé / Report / Restant sous le tableau
  const _carryClass = grandCarry < 0 ? "amt-neg" : grandCarry > 0 ? "amt-ok" : "amt-zero";
  const _remColor   = _gClass2 === "amt-neg" ? "var(--red)" : _gClass2 === "amt-warn" ? "#C17B2A" : _gClass2 === "amt-ok" ? "var(--green)" : "var(--text-muted)";
  const _carryColor = grandCarry < 0 ? "var(--red)" : grandCarry > 0 ? "var(--green)" : "var(--text-muted)";
  const summaryCard = document.createElement("div");
  summaryCard.className = "budget-summary-card";
  summaryCard.innerHTML = `
    <div class="bsc-item">
      <span class="bsc-label">Dépensé</span>
      <span class="bsc-value" style="color:var(--text);">${formatEuro(grandSpent)}</span>
    </div>
    <div class="bsc-divider"></div>
    <div class="bsc-item">
      <span class="bsc-label">Report</span>
      <span class="bsc-value" style="color:${_carryColor};">${grandCarry > 0 ? "+" : ""}${formatEuro(grandCarry)}</span>
    </div>
    <div class="bsc-divider"></div>
    <div class="bsc-item bsc-item-main">
      <span class="bsc-label">Restant</span>
      <span class="bsc-value bsc-value-main" style="color:${_remColor};">${formatEuro(grandRemaining)}</span>
    </div>
  `;
  container.appendChild(summaryCard);
  _restoreBucketStates();
}

function toggleBucket(bucketId, headerRow) {
  const isCollapsed = headerRow.classList.toggle("collapsed");
  const arrow = headerRow.querySelector(".bucket-toggle");
  if (arrow) arrow.style.transform = isCollapsed ? "rotate(-90deg)" : "";
  // Cacher les lignes catégories ET le bandeau masquées
  document.querySelectorAll(`tr.cat-row[data-bucket="${bucketId}"], tr.cat-hidden-row[data-bucket="${bucketId}"]`)
    .forEach(row => { row.style.display = isCollapsed ? "none" : ""; });
  _budgetCollapsed[bucketId] = isCollapsed;
}

function expandAllBuckets() {
  document.querySelectorAll(".bucket-header").forEach(header => {
    header.classList.remove("collapsed");
  });
  document.querySelectorAll("tr.cat-row, tr.cat-hidden-row").forEach(row => {
    row.style.display = "";
  });
}

function collapseAllBuckets() {
  document.querySelectorAll(".bucket-header").forEach(header => {
    header.classList.add("collapsed");
  });
  document.querySelectorAll("tr.cat-row, tr.cat-hidden-row").forEach(row => {
    row.style.display = "none";
  });
}

function parseDate(dd_mm_yyyy) {
  const parts = (dd_mm_yyyy || "").split("/");
  if (parts.length === 3) return new Date(parts[2], parts[1]-1, parts[0]);
  return null;
}

function periodEndDate(period) {
  // period = "MM/YYYY"
  const parts = (period || "").split("/");
  if (parts.length !== 2) return null;
  const m = parseInt(parts[0]), y = parseInt(parts[1]);
  return new Date(y, m, 0); // dernier jour du mois
}

function updateProjection() {
  const card = document.getElementById("projectionCard");
  if (!card) return;

  const today   = new Date(); today.setHours(23,59,59,999);
  const period  = document.getElementById("periodSelect")?.value || "";
  const endDate = periodEndDate(period) || today;

  // ── 1. Solde prévisionnel = pointés + TOUS non-pointés
  //    (même valeur que l'affichage dans l'onglet Banque)
  let soldePointe = 0, soldeNonPointe = 0;
  allTransactions.forEach(t => {
    const val = -(Number(t.amount) || 0);
    if (t.cleared || t.locked) soldePointe    += val;
    else                        soldeNonPointe += val;
  });
  const soldePrev = soldePointe + soldeNonPointe;

  // ── 2. Revenus attendus non reçus jusqu'à fin de période
  //    On inclut TOUTES les prévisions dont la période <= période affichée
  function _cmpPeriod(p1, p2) {
    // retourne <0 si p1 < p2, 0 si égal, >0 si p1 > p2
    const [m1,y1] = p1.split('/').map(Number);
    const [m2,y2] = p2.split('/').map(Number);
    return (y1*12+m1) - (y2*12+m2);
  }
  // Calculer amount_received par prévision depuis les transactions liées
  const _prvRcvMap = {};
  allTransactions.forEach(t => {
    if (t.linked_prevision_id) {
      _prvRcvMap[t.linked_prevision_id] = (_prvRcvMap[t.linked_prevision_id] || 0) + Math.abs(Number(t.amount) || 0);
    }
  });
  const entreesAttendues = allPrevisions
    .filter(p => {
      if (period && p.period && _cmpPeriod(p.period, period) > 0) return false;
      return true;
    })
    .reduce((s, p) => {
      const amtTotal    = Math.abs(Number(p.amount) || 0);
      const amtReceived = _prvRcvMap[p.id] || 0;
      const remaining   = Math.max(0, amtTotal - amtReceived);
      return s + remaining;
    }, 0);

  // ── 3. Reste à dépenser CUMULATIF
  //    = sum(max(0, remaining)) par catégorie, où remaining = budgeted - spent + carry
  let resteADepenser = 0;
  if (window._budgetCatDetails && window._budgetCatPeriod === period) {
    resteADepenser = window._budgetCatDetails.reduce((s, cat) => {
      if (cat.category_id === 'CAT001') return s;
      const r = Number(cat.remaining);  // already includes carry from server
      return s + Math.max(0, r);
    }, 0);
  } else if (window._budgetPeriodAssigned !== undefined) {
    // fallback : période seule + carry global si dispo
    const carry = window._budgetGrandCarry || 0;
    resteADepenser = Math.max(0, (window._budgetPeriodAssigned||0) - (window._budgetPeriodSpent||0) + carry);
  }

  // ── 4. Projection
  const projection = soldePrev + entreesAttendues - resteADepenser;

  const el = id => document.getElementById(id);
  if (el('projSoldePrev'))     el('projSoldePrev').textContent     = formatEuro(soldePrev);
  if (el('projEntreesValue'))  el('projEntreesValue').textContent  = formatEuro(entreesAttendues);
  if (el('projResteDepenser')) el('projResteDepenser').textContent = formatEuro(resteADepenser);

  const resultEl  = el('projResult');
  const resultVal = el('projResultValue');
  if (resultVal) resultVal.textContent = formatEuro(projection);
  if (resultEl)  resultEl.className = 'projection-result ' + (projection >= 0 ? 'pos' : 'neg');

  card.style.display = 'block';
}

function openResetBudgetModal() {
  const period = document.getElementById("periodSelect").value;
  if (!period) return;
  document.getElementById("resetBudgetDesc").textContent =
    `Tous les montants assignés de la période ${period} seront remis à 0. Cette action est irréversible.`;
  document.getElementById("resetBudgetModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeResetBudgetModal() {
  document.getElementById("resetBudgetModal").classList.remove("active");
}

(function() {
  const _rm = document.getElementById("resetBudgetModal");
  if (_rm) _rm.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeResetBudgetModal();
  });
})();

function confirmResetBudget() {
  const period = document.getElementById("periodSelect").value;
  closeResetBudgetModal();
  showSpinner();
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(data => {
      hideSpinner();
      if (data && data.buckets) {
        invalidateBudgetCache();
        _budgetCache[period] = { disponible: data.disponible, buckets: data.buckets, ts: Date.now() };
        renderBudget(data.buckets, period, data.disponible);
      }
    })
    .withFailureHandler(err => {
      hideSpinner();
      showInfoModal("Erreur RAZ: " + (err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)));
    })
    .resetBudgetPeriod(period);
}

function shiftPeriod(dir) {
  const select = document.getElementById("periodSelect");
  const idx = select.selectedIndex + dir;
  if (idx < 0 || idx >= select.options.length) return;
  select.selectedIndex = idx;
  loadBudget();
}

// ================= BUDGET BATCH =================
let _batchChanges = {}; // {catId: {period, categoryId, amount, originalAmount}}
let _batchPeriod  = "";

function saveBudget(period, categoryId, rawAmount) {
  const amount = parseFloat(rawAmount) || 0;
  _batchPeriod = period;

  if (!_batchChanges[categoryId]) {
    _batchChanges[categoryId] = { period, categoryId, amount, _new: true };
  } else {
    _batchChanges[categoryId].amount = amount;
  }

  const count = Object.keys(_batchChanges).length;
  document.getElementById("batchInfo").textContent =
    count + " modification" + (count > 1 ? "s" : "") + " en attente";
  document.getElementById("budgetBatchBar").classList.add("visible");
  _lockNav();

  // Mise à jour optimiste de la projection (recalcul local)
  _recomputeLocalBudget();
}

function _recomputeLocalBudget() {
  if (!window._budgetCatDetails) return;
  // Appliquer les changements batch en local pour la projection + disponible
  // IMPORTANT: on préserve cat.carry — le report n'affecte PAS le calcul de "À assigner"
  const patched = window._budgetCatDetails.map(cat => {
    const change = _batchChanges[cat.category_id];
    if (!change) return cat;
    const newBudgeted = change.amount;
    // remaining = période seule (pour delta disponible) + carry inchangé
    return { ...cat, budgeted: newBudgeted, remaining: newBudgeted - cat.spent + (cat.carry || 0) };
  });
  const tempDetails = window._budgetCatDetails;
  window._budgetCatDetails = patched;
  // _budgetPeriodAssigned = somme des budgets PÉRIODE uniquement (sans carry)
  // → sert uniquement à calculer le delta d'assignation pour "À assigner"
  window._budgetPeriodAssigned = patched.reduce((s, c) => s + c.budgeted, 0);

  // Ajustement optimiste: disponible = valeur GAS du cache - delta d'assignation locale
  // Le carry n'entre JAMAIS dans ce calcul : "À assigner" = revenus - budgété
  if (_batchPeriod) {
    const cacheEntry = _budgetCache[_batchPeriod];
    const baseDisp   = cacheEntry ? (cacheEntry.disponible || 0) : 0;
    const origAss    = window._budgetPeriodTotals[_batchPeriod] || 0;
    const delta      = window._budgetPeriodAssigned - origAss;
    renderDisponible(Math.round((baseDisp - delta) * 100) / 100);
  }
  updateProjection();
  window._budgetCatDetails = tempDetails; // on ne persiste pas, juste pour la projection
}

function saveBatchBudget() {
  const changes = Object.values(_batchChanges);
  if (!changes.length) return;
  const bar = document.getElementById("budgetBatchBar");
  showSpinner();

  // 1 seul appel GAS pour toutes les modifications
  const payload = changes.map(c => ({
    period: c.period, category_id: c.categoryId, amount: c.amount
  }));

  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(() => {
      hideSpinner();
      _batchChanges = {};
      bar.classList.remove("visible");
      _unlockNav();
      // Invalider le résumé cross-périodes pour forcer rechargement
      window._budgetSummaryLoaded = false;
      invalidateBudgetCache(_batchPeriod);
      loadBudget(true);
      _checkUndoAvailable();
    })
    .withFailureHandler(err => {
      hideSpinner();
      console.error("Batch save error:", err);
    })
    .saveBudgetBatch(payload);
}

function cancelBatchBudget() {
  _batchChanges = {};
  document.getElementById("budgetBatchBar").classList.remove("visible");
  _unlockNav();
  invalidateBudgetCache();
  loadBudget(true);
}

// ================= HISTORIQUE =================
function refreshHistory(transactions) {
  allTransactions = transactions;
  historyLoaded = true;
  clearSelection();
  populateFilters();
  computeSoldes();
  applyFilters();
  renderPrevisions();
}

function populateFilters() {
  const periods = [], categories = [];
  const seenP = new Set(), seenC = new Set();
  allTransactions.forEach(t => {
    if (t.period   && !seenP.has(t.period))   { seenP.add(t.period);   periods.push(t.period); }
    if (t.category && !seenC.has(t.category)) { seenC.add(t.category); categories.push(t.category); }
  });

  // Mémoriser la sélection courante avant de reconstruire
  const fp = document.getElementById("filterPeriod");
  const prevPeriod = fp ? fp.value : "";

  fillSelect("filterPeriod", periods);
  fillSelect("filterCategory", categories);

  // Restaurer la sélection précédente si elle existe encore
  if (fp && prevPeriod) {
    for (let i = 0; i < fp.options.length; i++) {
      if (fp.options[i].value === prevPeriod) { fp.selectedIndex = i; break; }
    }
  }

  // Filtre Tiers depuis allDebtors
  const dSel = document.getElementById("filterDebtor");
  if (dSel) {
    const cur = dSel.value;
    dSel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Tous tiers</option>';
    [...(allDebtors || [])].sort((a,b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name)).forEach(d => {
      const o = document.createElement("option");
      o.value = d.name; o.textContent = d.name;
      dSel.appendChild(o);
    });
    if (cur) dSel.value = cur;
  }
}

function fillSelect(id, values) {
  const select = document.getElementById(id);
  select.innerHTML = "<option value=''>Tous</option>";
  values.forEach(v => {
    const opt = document.createElement("option");
    opt.value = v; opt.textContent = v;
    select.appendChild(opt);
  });
}

function toggleUnclearedFilter(e) {
  if (e && (e.target.tagName === "INPUT" || e.target.tagName === "LABEL")) return;
  const cb = document.getElementById("filterUncleared");
  cb.checked = !cb.checked;
  applyFilters();
}

let _sortCol = "date", _sortDir = -1;

function applyFilters() {
  const period      = document.getElementById("filterPeriod").value;
  const category    = document.getElementById("filterCategory").value;
  const debtor      = (document.getElementById("filterDebtor")||{}).value || "";
  const unclearedOnly = document.getElementById("filterUncleared").checked;
  const hideLocked    = (document.getElementById("filterLocked")||{}).checked || false;
  const sense       = (document.getElementById("filterSense")||{}).value || "";
  const searchQ     = ((document.getElementById("txSearchInput")||{}).value || "").trim().toLowerCase();
  let filtered = allTransactions;
  if (period)        filtered = filtered.filter(t => t.period == period);
  if (category)      filtered = filtered.filter(t => t.category == category);
  if (debtor)        filtered = filtered.filter(t => (t.debtor||"").toLowerCase() === debtor.toLowerCase());
  if (unclearedOnly) filtered = filtered.filter(t => !t.cleared);
  if (hideLocked)    filtered = filtered.filter(t => !t.locked);
  if (sense === "entree") filtered = filtered.filter(t => (Number(t.amount)||0) < 0);
  if (sense === "sortie") filtered = filtered.filter(t => (Number(t.amount)||0) >= 0);
  if (searchQ) filtered = filtered.filter(t => {
    const hay = ((t.description||"") + " " + (t.category||"") + " " + (t.debtor||"")).toLowerCase();
    return hay.includes(searchQ);
  });
  filtered = _sortTransactions(filtered);
  renderTransactions(filtered);
  _updateFilterHighlights();
}

function _updateFilterHighlights() {
  // Selects : gold si valeur sélectionnée
  ["filterPeriod","filterCategory","filterDebtor","filterSense"].forEach(id => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    el.classList.toggle("filter-active", !!el.value);
  });
  // Checkboxes : gold si cochée
  ["filterUncleared","filterLocked"].forEach(id => {
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (!el) return;
    el.closest(".filter-uncleared")?.classList.toggle("filter-active", el.checked);
  });
}
function _sortTransactions(list) {
  return [...list].sort((a, b) => {
    let va, vb;
    if      (_sortCol === "date")     { va = a.rawDate||0;                      vb = b.rawDate||0; }
    else if (_sortCol === "category") { va = (a.category||"").toLowerCase();    vb = (b.category||"").toLowerCase(); }
    else if (_sortCol === "debtor")   { va = (a.debtor||"").toLowerCase();      vb = (b.debtor||"").toLowerCase(); }
    else if (_sortCol === "amount")   { va = Math.abs(Number(a.amount)||0);     vb = Math.abs(Number(b.amount)||0); }
    else                              { va = a.rawDate||0;                      vb = b.rawDate||0; }
    return va < vb ? _sortDir : va > vb ? -_sortDir : 0;
  });
}
function _setSortCol(col) {
  _sortDir = (_sortCol === col) ? -_sortDir : 1;
  _sortCol = col;
  applyFilters();
  document.querySelectorAll(".tx-th-sort").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("active-asc","active-desc"));
  const th = document.querySelector(`.tx-th-sort[data-col="${col}"]`);
  if (th) th.classList.add(_sortDir === 1 ? "active-asc" : "active-desc");
}

function computeSubtotal(data) {
  let entrees = 0, sorties = 0;
  data.forEach(t => {
    const n = Number(t.amount) || 0;
    if (n < 0) entrees += Math.abs(n); // négatif = entrée
    else sorties += n;                  // positif = sortie
  });
  const solde = entrees - sorties;

  const bar = document.getElementById("txSubtotal");
  bar.style.display = data.length > 0 ? "flex" : "none";

  document.getElementById("subEntrees").textContent = formatEuro(entrees);
  document.getElementById("subSorties").textContent = formatEuro(sorties);
  const soldeEl = document.getElementById("subSolde");
  soldeEl.textContent = formatEuro(solde);
  soldeEl.className = "tx-subtotal-value " + (solde >= 0 ? "pos" : "neg");
}

// Menu contextuel flottant unique (réutilisé pour toutes les lignes)
const _menu = document.createElement("div");
_menu.className = "tx-menu";
_menu.id = "floatingMenu";
document.body.appendChild(_menu);
let _menuTxId = null;

function renderTransactions(data) {
  if (!data) data = allTransactions;  // défaut : toutes les transactions
  computeSubtotal(data);
  const container = document.getElementById("historyContainer");
  container.innerHTML = "";

  if (!data.length) return;

  // Tableau
  const table = document.createElement("table");
  table.className = "tx-table";
  const _si = c => `<span class="th-sort-icon${_sortCol===c?' active':''}">${_sortCol!==c?'⇅':_sortDir===1?'↑':'↓'}</span>`;
  table.innerHTML = `
    <thead>
      <tr>
        <th class="td-check"></th>
        <th class="td-date tx-th-sort" data-col="date"     onclick="_setSortCol('date')">Date ${_si("date")}</th>
        <th class="td-cat tx-th-sort"  data-col="category" onclick="_setSortCol('category')">Catégorie ${_si("category")}</th>
        <th class="td-debtor tx-th-sort" data-col="debtor" onclick="_setSortCol('debtor')">Bénéf. ${_si("debtor")}</th>
        <th class="td-desc">Note</th>
        <th class="td-amt tx-th-sort"  data-col="amount"   onclick="_setSortCol('amount')">Montant ${_si("amount")}</th>
        <th class="td-icons"></th>
      </tr>
    </thead>
    <tbody id="txTbody"></tbody>
  `;
  container.appendChild(table);
  const tbody = table.querySelector("#txTbody");

  data.forEach(t => {
    const isSelected = selectedIds.has(t.id);
    const amountNum  = Number(t.amount);
    const isSortie   = amountNum >= 0;
    const amtColor   = isSortie ? "#c0392b" : "#27ae60";
    const amtLabel   = (isSortie ? "−" : "+") + formatEuro(Math.abs(amountNum));

    const tr = document.createElement("tr");
    tr.id = "row-" + t.id;
    let cls = [];
    if (isSelected) cls.push("row-selected");
    if (t.cleared)  cls.push("row-cleared");
    if (t.locked)   cls.push("row-locked");
    tr.className = cls.join(" ");

    tr.innerHTML = `
      <td class="td-check">
        <div class="tx-checkbox ${isSelected ? 'checked':''}" id="chk-${t.id}">${isSelected ? '✓':''}</div>
      </td>
      <td class="td-date">${t.date}</td>
      <td class="td-cat"  title="${t.category}">${t.category}</td>
      <td class="td-debtor" title="${t.debtor||''}">${t.debtor||''}</td>
      <td class="td-desc" title="${t.description||''}">${t.description||''}</td>
      <td class="td-amt"  style="color:${amtColor}">${amtLabel}</td>
      <td class="td-icons">
        <span class="icon-cleared ${t.cleared?'on':''}"
          title="${t.locked ? 'Verrouillée — pointage protégé' : (t.cleared?'Pointée':'Non pointée')}"
          style="${t.locked ? 'cursor:default;opacity:0.5;' : ''}"
          onclick="handleToggleCleared('${t.id}',event)">✓</span>
        <span class="icon-locked ${t.locked?'on':''}" title="${t.locked?'Verrouillée':'Verrouiller'}"
          onclick="handleToggleLocked('${t.id}',event)">${t.locked?'🔒':'🔓'}</span>
      </td>
    `;

    // Checkbox click
    tr.querySelector(".tx-checkbox").addEventListener("click", e => {
      e.stopPropagation();
      toggleSelect(t.id, e);
    });

    // Row click → menu ou sélection
    tr.addEventListener("click", e => {
      if (selectedIds.size > 0) { toggleSelect(t.id, e); return; }
      if (t.locked) return; // transactions verrouillées non éditables
      const parts   = (t.date||"").split("/");
      const isoDate = parts.length===3 ? `${parts[2]}-${parts[1]}-${parts[0]}` : t.date;
      startEditRow(t.id, isoDate, e);
    });

    tbody.appendChild(tr);
  });
}

function openRowMenu(t, e) {
  e.stopPropagation();
  closeAllMenus();
  _menuTxId = t.id;

  const parts   = (t.date||"").split("/");
  const isoDate = parts.length===3 ? `${parts[2]}-${parts[1]}-${parts[0]}` : t.date;

  const _isIncoming = Number(t.amount) < 0;
  const _skipLabel  = t.skip_link ? '🔗 Marquer comme attendu' : '🚫 Marquer comme ponctuel';
  _menu.innerHTML = `
    <button class="tx-menu-item ${t.locked?'disabled':''}"
      onclick="startEditRow('${t.id}','${isoDate}',event)">✏️ Modifier</button>
    <button class="tx-menu-item danger ${t.locked?'disabled':''}"
      onclick="openDeleteModal('${t.id}',event)">Supprimer</button>
    <button class="tx-menu-item"
      onclick="handleToggleLocked('${t.id}',event)">${t.locked?'🔓 Déverrouiller':'🔒 Verrouiller'}</button>
    ${_isIncoming ? `<button class="tx-menu-item" onclick="_setTxSkipLink('${t.id}', ${!t.skip_link}, event)">${_skipLabel}</button>` : ''}
  `;

  // Position menu near click
  const x = Math.min(e.clientX, window.innerWidth  - 180);
  const y = Math.min(e.clientY, window.innerHeight - 140);
  _menu.style.left = x + "px";
  _menu.style.top  = y + "px";
  _menu.classList.add("open");
}

// ================= SELECTION MULTIPLE =================
function toggleSelect(id, e) {
  e.stopPropagation();
  closeAllMenus();

  if (selectedIds.has(id)) {
    selectedIds.delete(id);
  } else {
    selectedIds.add(id);
  }

  // Mettre à jour visuellement sans re-render complet
  const row = document.getElementById("row-" + id);
  const chk = document.getElementById("chk-" + id);
  if (row && chk) {
    if (selectedIds.has(id)) {
      row.classList.add("row-selected");
      chk.classList.add("checked");
      chk.textContent = "✓";
    } else {
      row.classList.remove("row-selected");
      chk.classList.remove("checked");
      chk.textContent = "";
    }
  }

  updateSelectionBar();
}

function updateSelectionBar() {
  const bar  = document.getElementById("selectionBar");
  const info = document.getElementById("selectionInfo");
  if (selectedIds.size === 0) { bar.classList.remove("active"); return; }

  bar.classList.add("active");
  _syncSelectionBar();
  const n = selectedIds.size;
  info.textContent = `${n} transaction${n>1?"s":""} sélectionnée${n>1?"s":""}`;

  // Analyser la sélection
  const selected = [...selectedIds].map(id => allTransactions.find(x => x.id===id)).filter(Boolean);
  const hasUnlocked = selected.some(t => !t.locked);
  const hasLocked   = selected.some(t =>  t.locked);

  // Activer/désactiver selon contexte
  document.getElementById("btnBulkClear").disabled  = !hasUnlocked;
  document.getElementById("btnBulkDup").disabled    = !hasUnlocked;
  document.getElementById("btnBulkDel").disabled    = !hasUnlocked;
  document.getElementById("btnBulkLock").disabled   = !hasUnlocked; // lock si au moins une non verrouillée
  document.getElementById("btnBulkUnlock").disabled = !hasLocked;   // unlock si au moins une verrouillée
}

function clearSelection() {
  selectedIds.forEach(id => {
    const row = document.getElementById("row-" + id);
    const chk = document.getElementById("chk-" + id);
    if (row) row.classList.remove("row-selected");
    if (chk) { chk.classList.remove("checked"); chk.textContent = ""; }
  });
  selectedIds.clear();
  updateSelectionBar();
}

// ================= ACTIONS EN MASSE =================
function bulkLock() {
  const selected = [...selectedIds].map(id => allTransactions.find(x => x.id===id)).filter(Boolean);
  const cleared   = selected.filter(t => t.cleared && !t.locked);
  const uncleared = selected.filter(t => !t.cleared && !t.locked);
  const alreadyLocked = selected.filter(t => t.locked);

  if (!cleared.length && !uncleared.length) {
    showInfoModal("ℹ️ Toutes les transactions sélectionnées sont déjà verrouillées.");
    return;
  }
  if (!cleared.length && uncleared.length) {
    showInfoModal("⚠️ Seules les transactions <strong>pointées</strong> peuvent être verrouillées.<br><br>Pointez d'abord vos transactions (✓ Pointer), puis verrouillez.");
    return;
  }
  if (uncleared.length > 0) {
    // Mix: some cleared, some not — demander confirmation
    const msg = `${cleared.length} transaction(s) pointée(s) vont être verrouillées.<br>`
      + `<span style="color:#F59E0B;font-size:13px;">⚠️ ${uncleared.length} transaction(s) non pointée(s) seront ignorées.</span>`;
    document.getElementById("infoModalText").innerHTML = msg;
    document.getElementById("infoModal").classList.add("active");
    // Remplacer temporairement le bouton OK par Verrouiller + Annuler
    const modal = document.getElementById("infoModal").querySelector(".modal");
    const origContent = modal.innerHTML;
    modal.innerHTML = `
      <p style="font-size:15px;line-height:1.6;">${msg}</p>
      <div class="modal-buttons">
        <button class="btn-cancel" onclick="document.getElementById('infoModal').classList.remove('active')">Annuler</button>
        <button style="background:#374151;color:white;border-radius:14px;" onclick="_doBulkLock()">🔒 Verrouiller les pointées</button>
      </div>
    `;
    window._pendingBulkLockIds = cleared.map(t => t.id);
    return;
  }
  // Seulement des pointées → direct
  window._pendingBulkLockIds = cleared.map(t => t.id);
  _doBulkLock();
}

function _doBulkLock() {
  document.getElementById("infoModal").classList.remove("active");
  const ids = window._pendingBulkLockIds || [];
  if (!ids.length) return;
  window._pendingBulkLockIds = [];
  showSpinner();
  _gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
    hideSpinner();
    afterMutation(updated, "Verrouillage");
  }).lockMultiple(ids);
}

function bulkUnlock() {
  const ids = [...selectedIds].filter(id => {
    const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id===id);
    return t && t.locked;
  });
  if (!ids.length) return;
  const n = ids.length;
  document.getElementById("unlockModalDesc").textContent =
    `Vous êtes sur le point de déverrouiller ${n} transaction${n>1?"s":""}.`
    + ` Ces transactions pourront à nouveau être modifiées et supprimées.`;
  document.getElementById("unlockModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeUnlockModal() {
  document.getElementById("unlockModal").classList.remove("active");
  _pendingUnlockIds = [];
}

document.getElementById("unlockModal").addEventListener("click", function(e) {
  if (e.target === this) closeUnlockModal();
});

function confirmBulkUnlock() {
  // Utilise _pendingUnlockIds si défini (unlock unitaire), sinon filtre la sélection
  const ids = _pendingUnlockIds.length
    ? _pendingUnlockIds
    : [...selectedIds].filter(id => {
        const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id===id);
        return t && t.locked;
      });
  _pendingUnlockIds = [];
  closeUnlockModal();
  if (!ids.length) return;
  showSpinner();
  _gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
    hideSpinner();
    afterMutation(updated, "Déverrouillage");
  }).unlockMultiple(ids);
}

function bulkToggleCleared() {
  if (!selectedIds.size) return;
  // Exclure les transactions verrouillées
  const ids = [...selectedIds].filter(id => {
    const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === id);
    return t && !t.locked;
  });
  if (!ids.length) return;
  showSpinner();
  _gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
    hideSpinner();
    afterMutation(updated, "Pointage multiple");
  }).toggleClearedMultiple(ids);
}

function bulkDuplicate() {
  if (!selectedIds.size) return;
  const ids = [...selectedIds].filter(id => {
    const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === id);
    return t && !t.locked;
  });
  if (!ids.length) return;
  showSpinner();
  _gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
    hideSpinner();
    afterMutation(updated, "Duplication multiple");
  }).duplicateMultiple(ids);
}

function bulkDeleteConfirm() {
  if (!selectedIds.size) return;
  const unlocked = [...selectedIds].filter(id => {
    const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === id);
    return t && !t.locked;
  });
  if (!unlocked.length) return;
  const locked = selectedIds.size - unlocked.length;
  const msg = locked > 0
    ? `${unlocked.length} transaction${unlocked.length>1?"s":""} vont être supprimées (${locked} verrouillée${locked>1?"s":""} ignorée${locked>1?"s":""}).`
    : `${unlocked.length} transaction${unlocked.length>1?"s":""} vont être supprimées définitivement.`;
  document.getElementById("bulkDeleteDesc").textContent = msg;
  document.getElementById("bulkDeleteModal").classList.add("active");
}

function confirmBulkDelete() {
  const ids = [...selectedIds].filter(id => {
    const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === id);
    return t && !t.locked;
  });
  if (!ids.length) { closeBulkDeleteModal(); showInfoModal("🔒 Toutes les transactions sélectionnées sont verrouillées."); return; }
  closeBulkDeleteModal();
  showSpinner();
  _gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
    hideSpinner();
    clearSelection();
    afterMutation(updated, "Suppression multiple");
  }).deleteMultiple(ids);
}

function closeBulkDeleteModal() {
  document.getElementById("bulkDeleteModal").classList.remove("active");
}

(function() {
  const _m = document.getElementById("bulkDeleteModal");
  if (_m) _m.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeBulkDeleteModal();
  });
})();

// ================= POINTAGE SIMPLE =================
function handleToggleCleared(id, e) {
  if (e) e.stopPropagation();
  closeAllMenus();
  const tx = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === id);
  if (!tx || tx.locked) return;

  // Optimistic UI: mise à jour visuelle immédiate, sans re-render complet
  tx.cleared = !tx.cleared;
  _patchRow(id);
  computeSoldes();

  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(updated => {
      // Mise à jour silencieuse des données — pas de re-render (évite clignotement)
      allTransactions = updated;
      computeSoldes();
      _checkUndoAvailable();
      _patchRow(id); // confirmer l'état depuis le serveur
    })
    .withFailureHandler(() => {
      tx.cleared = !tx.cleared; // rollback visuel
      _patchRow(id);
      computeSoldes();
    })
    .toggleCleared(id);
}

function _patchRow(id) {
  const tx  = allTransactions.find(t => t.id === id);
  if (!tx) return;
  const row = document.getElementById("row-" + id);
  if (!row) return;
  const cls = [];
  if (selectedIds && selectedIds.has(id)) cls.push("row-selected");
  if (tx.cleared) cls.push("row-cleared");
  if (tx.locked)  cls.push("row-locked");
  row.className = cls.join(" ");
  const clrIcon = row.querySelector(".icon-cleared");
  if (clrIcon) {
    clrIcon.className = "icon-cleared" + (tx.cleared ? " on" : "");
    clrIcon.title = tx.locked ? "Verrouillée — pointage protégé" : (tx.cleared ? "Pointée" : "Non pointée");
    clrIcon.style.cssText = tx.locked ? "cursor:default;opacity:0.5;" : "";
  }
  const lckIcon = row.querySelector(".icon-locked");
  if (lckIcon) {
    lckIcon.className = "icon-locked" + (tx.locked ? " on" : "");
    lckIcon.textContent = tx.locked ? "🔒" : "🔓";
  }
}

// ================= VERROUILLAGE =================
function handleToggleLocked(id, e) {
  if (e) e.stopPropagation();
  closeAllMenus();
  const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === id);
  if (!t) return;

  if (t.locked) {
    // Déverrouillage → confirmation
    document.getElementById("unlockModalDesc").textContent =
      `Vous êtes sur le point de déverrouiller cette transaction : ${t.date} — ${t.category} — ${formatEuro(t.amount)}. Elle pourra à nouveau être modifiée et supprimée.`;
    _pendingUnlockIds = [id];
    document.getElementById("unlockModal").classList.add("active");
  } else {
    if (!t.cleared) {
      showInfoModal("⚠️ Seules les transactions <strong>pointées</strong> (✓) peuvent être verrouillées.<br>Pointez d'abord cette transaction.");
      return;
    }
    showSpinner();
    _gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
      hideSpinner();
      afterMutation(updated, "Verrouillage transaction");
    }).lockMultiple([id]);
  }
}

// ================= MENU CONTEXTUEL =================
function closeAllMenus() {
  document.getElementById("floatingMenu").classList.remove("open");
  openMenuId = null;
}

document.addEventListener("click", () => closeAllMenus());
document.getElementById("editModal").addEventListener("click", function(e) {
  if (e.target === this) closeEditModal();
});

// ================= EDITION VIA MODAL =================
let _editingId = null;

function startEditRow(id, isoDate, e) {
  if (e) e.stopPropagation();
  closeAllMenus();
  const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === id);
  if (!t || t.locked) return;
  _editingId = id;

  document.getElementById("editModalDate").value  = isoDate;
  document.getElementById("editModalDesc").value  = t.description || "";
  _tpeSet("editModalAmt", Math.abs(t.amount));

  // Payee (debtor)
  const debtorInput = document.getElementById("editDebtorInput");
  if (debtorInput) debtorInput.value = t.debtor || "";

  // Sense
  const sense = t.amount >= 0 ? "sortie" : "entree";
  document.getElementById("editModalBtnSortie").className = sense==="sortie"?"active-sortie":"";
  document.getElementById("editModalBtnEntree").className = sense==="entree"?"active-entree":"";
  _editModalSense = sense;

  fillCategorySelect("editModalCat", allCategories, t.category_id);
  const _isAttend = Number(t.amount) < 0
    && (t.category_id === "CAT001" || (t.category||"").trim().toLowerCase() === "à assigner");
  if (_isAttend) setEditModalSense("attendu");
  else { const bA = document.getElementById("editModalBtnAttend"); if(bA) bA.className = ""; }

  // Boutons Supprimer et Dupliquer
  const delBtn = document.getElementById("editModalDeleteBtn");
  if (delBtn) delBtn.style.display = t.locked ? "none" : "block";
  const dupBtn = document.getElementById("editModalDupBtn");
  if (dupBtn) dupBtn.style.display = t.locked ? "none" : "block";

  // Badge skip_link
  const skipBadge = document.getElementById("editSkipLinkBadge");
  if (skipBadge) skipBadge.style.display = t.skip_link ? "flex" : "none";

  document.getElementById("editModal").classList.add("active");
}

let _editModalSense = "sortie";
function setEditModalSense(s) {
  _editModalSense = s;
  document.getElementById("editModalBtnSortie").className = s==="sortie"?"active-sortie":"";
  document.getElementById("editModalBtnEntree").className = s==="entree"?"active-entree":"";
  const btnA = document.getElementById("editModalBtnAttend");
  if (btnA) btnA.className = s==="attendu"?"active-prevision":"";
  // Mode attendu: forcer catégorie "À assigner" (CAT001)
  const catSel = document.getElementById("editModalCat");
  if (!catSel) return;
  if (s === "attendu") {
    const ac = allCategories.find(c => c.id === "CAT001" || (c.name||"").trim().toLowerCase() === "à assigner");
    if (ac) { catSel.value = ac.id; catSel.disabled = true; }
  } else {
    catSel.disabled = false;
  }
}

function _toggleAllDebtors(checked) {
  // Respecter le filtre de recherche actif
  const filterInput = document.getElementById("settingsMgmtSearch");
  const filterVal = filterInput ? filterInput.value.trim().toLowerCase() : "";
  document.querySelectorAll(".debtor-sel-chk").forEach(chk => {
    const item = chk.closest(".smgmt-item");
    if (!item) { chk.checked = checked; return; }
    if (filterVal) {
      const name = (item.querySelector(".smgmt-item-name")?.textContent || "").toLowerCase();
      if (!name.includes(filterVal)) return; // pas dans le filtre → ignorer
    }
    chk.checked = checked;
  });
  _updateDebtorBulkBtn();
}
function _updateDebtorBulkBtn() {
  const selected = document.querySelectorAll(".debtor-sel-chk:checked");
  const btn = document.getElementById("debtorBulkDelBtn");
  if (btn) {
    btn.style.display = selected.length > 0 ? "" : "none";
    btn.textContent = selected.length > 0 ? `🗑 Supprimer (${selected.length})` : "🗑 Supprimer";
  }
}
function _bulkDeleteDebtors() {
  const ids = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(".debtor-sel-chk:checked")).map(c => c.dataset.id);
  if (!ids.length) return;
  // Utiliser la modal custom au lieu de confirm()
  const names = ids.map(id => {
    const d = allDebtors.find(x => x.id===id);
    return d ? d.name : id;
  }).join(", ");
  _showConfirmModal(
    `🗑 Supprimer ${ids.length} bénéficiaire(s) ?`,
    `<strong>${names}</strong><br><br>Cette action est irréversible.`,
    () => {
  showSpinner();
  // Supprimer un par un séquentiellement
    showSpinner();
    let remaining = [...ids];
    function _deleteNext() {
      if (!remaining.length) { hideSpinner(); _refreshSettingsMgmtIfOpen(); return; }
      const id = remaining.shift();
      _gas()
        .withSuccessHandler(s => {
          allCategories=s.categories; allBuckets=s.buckets; allDebtors=s.debtors;
          fillDebtorDatalist(); _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
          _deleteNext();
        })
        .withFailureHandler(e => { hideSpinner(); showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message); })
        .deleteDebtor(id);
    }
    _deleteNext();
  });
}

// Modal de confirmation générique
// Callback stocké pour la modal de confirmation
window._confirmModalCallback = null;
function _confirmModalDo() {
  const cb = window._confirmModalCallback;
  window._confirmModalCallback = null;
  const m = document.getElementById("_genericConfirmModal");
  if (m) m.remove();
  if (cb) cb();
}
function _showConfirmModal(title, body, onConfirm) {
  const existing = document.getElementById("_genericConfirmModal");
  if (existing) existing.remove();
  window._confirmModalCallback = onConfirm;
  const overlay = document.createElement("div");
  overlay.id = "_genericConfirmModal";
  overlay.className = "modal-overlay active";
  overlay.innerHTML = `
    <div class="modal" style="background:var(--card)" onclick="event.stopPropagation()">
      <h3 style="color:var(--text);margin:0 0 12px">${title}</h3>
      <div style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:14px;line-height:1.6;margin-bottom:20px">${body}</div>
      <div class="modal-buttons">
        <button onclick="document.getElementById('_genericConfirmModal').remove()" style="background:var(--segment);color:var(--text);border:none;border-radius:12px;padding:10px 18px;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer;">Annuler</button>
        <button onclick="_confirmModalDo()" style="background:var(--red);color:white;border:none;border-radius:12px;padding:10px 20px;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer;">🗑 Confirmer</button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  overlay.addEventListener("click", (e) => { if(e.target===overlay) overlay.remove(); });
  document.body.appendChild(overlay);
}

// ─── Rollover : reporter les restes à dépenser ───────────────
function openRolloverModal() {
  const period = document.getElementById('periodSelect')?.value || '';
  if (!period) { showInfoModal('Sélectionnez d\'abord une période.'); return; }
  const parts = period.split('/');
  if (parts.length!==2) return;
  const [m,y] = [parseInt(parts[0]),parseInt(parts[1])];
  const prevM = m===1?12:m-1;
  const prevY = m===1?y-1:y;
  const prevPeriod = String('0'+prevM).slice(-2)+'/'+prevY;
  _showConfirmModal(
    `🔄 Reporter les restes`,
    `Reporter les restes à dépenser positifs de <b>${prevPeriod}</b> vers <b>${period}</b> ?<br><small style="color:var(--text-muted)">Seuls les soldes positifs seront reportés.</small>`,
    () => {
      showSpinner();
      _gas()
        .withSuccessHandler(result => {
          hideSpinner();
          if (result.error) { showInfoModal('Erreur: '+result.error); return; }
          showInfoModal(`✅ ${result.rolled} catégorie(s) reportée(s) de ${result.from} vers ${result.to}.`);
          invalidateBudgetCache();
          loadBudget(true);
        })
        .withFailureHandler(e => { hideSpinner(); showInfoModal('Erreur: '+e.message); })
        .rolloverBudget({ from: prevPeriod, to: period });
    }
  );
}

function _togglePrevisionsSection() {
  const container = document.getElementById("previsionsContainer");
  const icon = document.getElementById("previsionsToggleIcon");
  if (!container) return;
  const hidden = container.style.display === "none";
  container.style.display = hidden ? "" : "none";
  if (icon) icon.textContent = hidden ? "▼" : "▶";
}

function _updatePrevisionsCount() {
  const countEl = document.getElementById("previsionsCount");
  if (!countEl) return;
  const pending = allPrevisions.filter(p => !p.received).length;
  countEl.textContent = pending > 0 ? pending : "";
  countEl.style.display = pending > 0 ? "" : "none";
}

function closeEditModal() {
  document.getElementById("editModal").classList.remove("active");
  _editingId = null;
}

function duplicateFromEdit() {
  if (!_editingId) return;
  const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === _editingId);
  if (!t) return;
  closeEditModal();
  const today = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
  const payload = {
    date:        today,
    description: t.description || "",
    category_id: t.category_id || "",
    amount:      t.amount,
    debtor:      t.debtor || ""
  };
  showSpinner();
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(updated) {
      hideSpinner();
      afterMutation(updated, "Duplication transaction");
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(e) { hideSpinner(); showInfoModal("Erreur: " + e.message); })
    .addTransaction(payload);
}

function _doUpdateTransaction(form) {
  showSpinner();
  _gas()
    .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
      hideSpinner();
      var updated = result.transactions || result;
      afterMutation(Array.isArray(updated) ? updated : (result.transactions || []), 'Modification transaction');
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(e) { hideSpinner(); showInfoModal('Erreur: ' + e.message); })
    .updateTransaction(form);
}

function confirmEdit() {
  if (!_editingId) return;
  const rawAmt = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("editModalAmt").value));
  let _eCatId = document.getElementById("editModalCat").value;
  let _eAmt;
  if (_editModalSense === "attendu") {
    _eAmt = -rawAmt; // entrée
    const _ac = allCategories.find(c => c.id === "CAT001" || (c.name||"").trim().toLowerCase() === "à assigner");
    if (_ac) _eCatId = _ac.id;
  } else {
    _eAmt = _editModalSense === "entree" ? -rawAmt : rawAmt;
  }
  const eDebtor = ((document.getElementById("editDebtorInput") || {}).value || "").trim();
  var eDebtorKnown = !eDebtor || allDebtors.some(function(d){return d.name.toLowerCase()===eDebtor.toLowerCase();});
  const eClearedBtn = document.getElementById('editClearedBtn');
  var editForm = {
    id:          _editingId,
    date:        document.getElementById('editModalDate').value,
    category_id: _eCatId,
    amount:      _eAmt,
    description: document.getElementById('editModalDesc').value,
    debtor:      eDebtor,
    cleared:     eClearedBtn ? eClearedBtn.classList.contains('active-clr') : false
  };
  closeEditModal();
  if (!eDebtorKnown) {
    _pendingEditForm = editForm;
    _openNewDebtorSuggestForEdit(eDebtor, _eCatId);
    return;
  }
  _doUpdateTransaction(editForm);
}


function _confirmEditDelete() {
  if (!_editingId) return;
  const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === _editingId);
  const desc = t ? `${t.date} — ${t.category} — ${formatEuro(t.amount)}` : _editingId;
  closeEditModal();
  // Réutiliser la modale de confirmation de suppression existante
  pendingDeleteId = t ? t.id : _editingId;
  document.getElementById("deleteModalDesc").textContent = desc;
  document.getElementById("deleteModal").classList.add("active");
}
// ================= SUPPRESSION SIMPLE =================
function openDeleteModal(id, e) {
  e.stopPropagation();
  closeAllMenus();
  const t = allTransactions.find(x => x.id === id);
  pendingDeleteId = id;
  document.getElementById("deleteModalDesc").textContent =
    t ? `${t.date} — ${t.category} — ${formatEuro(t.amount)}` : id;
  document.getElementById("deleteModal").classList.add("active");
}

function confirmDelete() {
  if (window._deleteIsPrevision) {
    window._deleteIsPrevision = false;
    const id = _deletePrevId;
    _deletePrevId = null;
    closeDeleteModal();
    showSpinner();
    _gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
      hideSpinner();
      allPrevisions = updated;
      renderPrevisions();
    }).deletePrevision(id);
    return;
  }
  if (!pendingDeleteId) return;
  showSpinner();
  _gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
    hideSpinner(); closeDeleteModal(); afterMutation(updated, "Suppression transaction");
  }).deleteTransaction(pendingDeleteId);
}

function closeDeleteModal() {
  document.getElementById("deleteModal").classList.remove("active");
  pendingDeleteId = null;
}

(function() {
  const _m = document.getElementById("deleteModal");
  if (_m) _m.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
    if (e.target === this) closeDeleteModal();
  });
})();

// ================= SOLDES =================
// Positif = Sortie (charge), Négatif = Entrée (revenu)
// Un solde "sain" = plus d'entrées que de sorties = somme négative dans le sheet
// On inverse pour l'affichage : solde affiché = -somme (positif = bon)
// ================= NOTES CATÉGORIES BUDGET =================
// Cache local : { "period|catId": "texte de la note" }
window._budgetNotes = window._budgetNotes || {};

function _toggleCatNote(btn, catId, period) {
  const existing = document.getElementById('_catNotePopup');

  // Si le popup est déjà ouvert pour cette même catégorie → le fermer
  if (existing) {
    if (existing.dataset.catId === catId && existing.dataset.period === period) {
      existing.remove();
      return;
    }
    existing.remove();
  }

  const key = period + '|' + catId;
  const currentNote = window._budgetNotes[key] !== undefined
    ? window._budgetNotes[key]
    : (btn.title !== 'Ajouter une note' ? btn.title : '');

  const catName = btn.closest('tr')?.querySelector('.cat-name-link')?.textContent || '';

  const popup = document.createElement('div');
  popup.id = '_catNotePopup';
  popup.className = 'cat-note-popup';
  popup.dataset.catId  = catId;
  popup.dataset.period = period;
  popup.innerHTML = `
    <div class="cat-note-popup-header">
      <span class="cat-note-popup-label">📝 ${catName} — ${period}</span>
      <button class="cat-note-popup-close" onclick="document.getElementById('_catNotePopup')?.remove()">✕</button>
    </div>
    <textarea id="_catNoteTextarea" placeholder="Ajouter une note pour ce mois…">${currentNote}</textarea>

```
<div class="cat-note-popup-actions">
  <button class="cat-note-btn-clear" onclick="_clearCatNote('${catId}','${period}')">Effacer</button>
  <button class="cat-note-btn-save"  onclick="_saveCatNote('${catId}','${period}')">Enregistrer</button>
</div>
```

`;

// Positionnement : sous le bouton, recadré si hors écran
const rect = btn.getBoundingClientRect();
let top  = rect.bottom + 6;
let left = rect.left - 10;
if (left + 300 > window.innerWidth - 8) left = window.innerWidth - 308;
if (left < 8) left = 8;
if (top + 180 > window.innerHeight) top = rect.top - 186;
popup.style.top  = top  + 'px';
popup.style.left = left + 'px';

document.body.appendChild(popup);
const ta = document.getElementById('_catNoteTextarea');
if (ta) { ta.focus(); ta.setSelectionRange(ta.value.length, ta.value.length); }

// Fermer au clic extérieur
setTimeout(() => {
document.addEventListener('click', function _noteOutside(e) {
const p = document.getElementById('_catNotePopup');
if (!p) { document.removeEventListener('click', _noteOutside); return; }
if (!p.contains(e.target) && e.target !== btn) {
p.remove();
document.removeEventListener('click', _noteOutside);
}
});
}, 80);
}

function _saveCatNote(catId, period) {
const ta = document.getElementById('_catNoteTextarea');
if (!ta) return;
const note = ta.value.trim();
_applyNoteToUI(catId, period, note);
document.getElementById('_catNotePopup')?.remove();

// Persister en arrière-plan (silencieux)
_gas()
.withFailureHandler(err => console.warn('saveBudgetNote failed:', err))
.saveBudgetNote(period, catId, note);
}

function _clearCatNote(catId, period) {
const ta = document.getElementById('_catNoteTextarea');
if (ta) ta.value = '';
_applyNoteToUI(catId, period, '');
document.getElementById('_catNotePopup')?.remove();

_gas()
.withFailureHandler(err => console.warn('saveBudgetNote failed:', err))
.saveBudgetNote(period, catId, '');
}

function _applyNoteToUI(catId, period, note) {
const key = period + '|' + catId;
window._budgetNotes[key] = note;

// Mettre à jour l'icône 💬 dans la ligne
const row = document.querySelector(`.cat-row[data-cat-id="${catId}"]`);
if (row) {
const btn = row.querySelector('.cat-note-btn');
if (btn) {
btn.classList.toggle('has-note', !!note);
btn.title = note || 'Ajouter une note';
}
}
}

// Pré-charger les notes dans le cache local depuis les données serveur
function _preloadBudgetNotes(buckets, period) {
if (!buckets) return;
buckets.forEach(bucket => {
(bucket.categories || []).forEach(cat => {
if (cat.note !== undefined) {
window._budgetNotes[period + '|' + cat.category_id] = cat.note;
}
});
});
}

function _recomputeSavingsFromTx() {
// Recalcule _totalSavings depuis allTransactions en mémoire (sans appel GAS)
const catId = _savingsCatId || "CAT001";
let total = 0;
allTransactions.forEach(t => {
if (String(t.category_id) === String(catId)) {
total += Number(t.amount) || 0;
}
});
_totalSavings = Math.round(total * 100) / 100;
// NE PAS appeler _renderSavings ici — risque de corrompre l'affichage des autres onglets
// _renderSavings sera appelé naturellement à la prochaine visite de l'onglet Épargne
}

function computeSoldes() {
const today = new Date();
today.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

let pointe = 0, nonPointe = 0, previsionnel = 0;

allTransactions.forEach(t => {
const amount = Number(t.amount) || 0;
// On inverse : entrée (+) améliore le solde, sortie (-) le diminue
const val = -amount;
if (t.cleared) {
pointe += val;
} else {
nonPointe += val;
const parts = (t.date || "").split("/");
if (parts.length === 3) {
const txDate = new Date(`${parts[2]}-${parts[1]}-${parts[0]}`);
if (txDate <= today) previsionnel += val;
}
}
});

const setVal = (id, val, clickable) => {
const el = document.getElementById(id);
el.textContent = formatEuro(val);
el.className = "solde-value " + (val >= 0 ? "pos" : "neg");
if (clickable && val < 0) {
el.style.cursor = "pointer";
el.title = "Cliquer pour voir les transactions non pointées";
el.onclick = () => {
const cb = document.getElementById("filterUncleared");
if (cb) { cb.checked = true; applyFilters(); }
// Flash visuel
el.style.background = "#FEF3C7";
setTimeout(() => el.style.background = "", 800);
};
} else {
el.style.cursor = "";
el.title = "";
el.onclick = null;
}
};

setVal("soldePointe", pointe);
setVal("soldeNonPointe", nonPointe, true);
setVal("soldePrevisionnel", pointe + nonPointe); // = total toutes tx
// Sync avec le drawer si ouvert
updateDrawerSolde();
}

// ================= SELECT ALL =================
function selectAll() {
// Sélectionne UNIQUEMENT les transactions visibles (tous filtres actifs)
const period      = document.getElementById("filterPeriod")?.value || "";
const category    = document.getElementById("filterCategory")?.value || "";
const debtor      = document.getElementById("filterDebtor")?.value || "";
const unclearedOnly = document.getElementById("filterUncleared")?.checked || false;
const sense       = document.getElementById("filterSense")?.value || "";
let visible = allTransactions;
if (period)        visible = visible.filter(t => t.period == period);
if (category)      visible = visible.filter(t => t.category == category);
if (debtor)        visible = visible.filter(t => (t.description||"").toLowerCase() === debtor.toLowerCase());
if (unclearedOnly) visible = visible.filter(t => !t.cleared);
if (sense === "entree") visible = visible.filter(t => (Number(t.amount)||0) < 0);
if (sense === "sortie") visible = visible.filter(t => (Number(t.amount)||0) >= 0);

visible.forEach(t => {
if (!selectedIds.has(t.id)) {
selectedIds.add(t.id);
const row = document.getElementById("row-" + t.id);
const chk = document.getElementById("chk-" + t.id);
if (row) row.classList.add("row-selected");
if (chk) { chk.classList.add("checked"); chk.textContent = "✓"; }
}
});
updateSelectionBar();
}

// ================= MODAL AJOUT (depuis Banque) =================
let _modalSplitMode = false;

function openAddModal() {
document.getElementById("modalDate").value = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
document.getElementById("modalDesc").value = "";
document.getElementById("modalSimpleAmount").value = "";
var mdi=document.getElementById("modalDebtorInput"); if(mdi) mdi.value="";
document.getElementById("modalTotal").value = "";
document.getElementById("modalSplitLines").innerHTML = "";
document.getElementById("modalResteBadge").textContent = "—";
document.getElementById("modalResteBadge").className = "reste-badge nok";
_modalSplitMode = false;
document.getElementById("modalSimpleBlock").style.display = "";
document.getElementById("modalSplitBlock").style.display  = "none";
fillCategorySelect("modalSimpleCategory", allCategories);
setModalSense("sortie");
var _mdi = document.getElementById("modalDebtorInput");
if (_mdi) _mdi.value = "";
document.getElementById("addModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeAddModal() {
const b = document.getElementById("modalClearedBtn");
if (b) b.classList.remove("active-clr");
document.getElementById("addModal").classList.remove("active");
}

document.getElementById("addModal").addEventListener("click", function(e) {
if (e.target === this) closeAddModal();
});

function enableModalSplitMode() {
_modalSplitMode = true;
// Pré-remplir montant total depuis simple si déjà saisi
const simpleAmt = document.getElementById("modalSimpleAmount").value;
const simpleCat = document.getElementById("modalSimpleCategory").value;
if (simpleAmt) document.getElementById("modalTotal").value = simpleAmt;
document.getElementById("modalSimpleBlock").style.display = "none";
document.getElementById("modalSplitBlock").style.display  = "";
if (!document.querySelectorAll("#modalSplitLines .split-line").length) {
addModalSplitLine();
if (simpleCat) {
const s = document.querySelector("#modalSplitLines .split-line select");
if (s) s.value = simpleCat;
}
if (simpleAmt) {
const inp = document.querySelector("#modalSplitLines .split-line input[type=number]");
if (inp) { inp.value = simpleAmt; updateModalReste(); }
}
}
}

function disableModalSplitMode() {
_modalSplitMode = false;
document.getElementById("modalSimpleBlock").style.display = "";
document.getElementById("modalSplitBlock").style.display  = "none";
}

function setModalSense(sense) {
modalSense = sense;
document.getElementById("modalBtnSortie").className    = sense === "sortie"    ? "active-sortie"    : "";
document.getElementById("modalBtnEntree").className    = sense === "entree"    ? "active-entree"    : "";
document.getElementById("modalBtnPrevision").className = sense === "prevision" ? "active-prevision" : "";
// Mode prévision = toujours simple, pas de split
const splitBtn = document.getElementById("modalSplitToggleBtn");
if (splitBtn) splitBtn.style.display = sense === "prevision" ? "none" : "";
if (sense === "prevision" && _modalSplitMode) disableModalSplitMode();
updateModalReste();
}

function saveModalTransaction() {
const date = document.getElementById("modalDate").value;
const desc = document.getElementById("modalDesc").value;

// MODE PRÉVISION
if (modalSense === "prevision") {
const amt   = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("modalSimpleAmount").value) || 0);
const catId = document.getElementById("modalSimpleCategory").value;
if (!amt || !catId) return;
closeAddModal();
showSpinner();
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(updated => {
hideSpinner();
allPrevisions = updated;
renderPrevisions();
updateProjection();
})
.withFailureHandler(err => { hideSpinner(); console.error(err); })
.addPrevision({ date, description: desc, category_id: catId, amount: amt });
return;
}

// MODE SPLIT
if (_modalSplitMode) {
const lines = collectSplitLines("modalSplitLines", date, desc, modalSense);
if (!lines.length) return;
const mDebtor = ((document.getElementById("modalDebtorInput")||{}).value||"").trim();
// Ajouter le debtor dans chaque ligne
if (mDebtor) lines.forEach(l => { l.debtor = mDebtor; });
closeAddModal();
const debtorKnown = !mDebtor || allDebtors.some(d => d.name.toLowerCase()===mDebtor.toLowerCase());
if (!debtorKnown) {
// Debtor inconnu: stocker comme item split dans _txSaveQueue
_txSaveQueue.push({ isSplit: true, lines, debtor: mDebtor, date, description: desc });
if (_txSaveQueue.length === 1) _processNextInQueue();
return;
}
showSpinner();
const fn      = lines.length === 1 ? "addTransaction" : "addSplitTransaction";
const payload = lines.length === 1 ? lines[0] : lines;
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(updated => { hideSpinner(); afterMutation(updated, "Ajout transaction"); })
.withFailureHandler(err => { hideSpinner(); console.error(err); })
[fn](payload);
return;
}

// MODE SIMPLE
const amt   = Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("modalSimpleAmount").value) || 0);
const catId = document.getElementById("modalSimpleCategory").value;
if (!amt || !catId) return;
const amount = modalSense === "entree" ? -amt : amt;
const mDebtor = ((document.getElementById("modalDebtorInput") || {}).value || "").trim();
const mCleared = document.getElementById("modalClearedBtn") ? document.getElementById("modalClearedBtn").classList.contains("active-clr") : false;
closeAddModal();
_enqueueTx({date:date, description:desc, category_id:catId, amount:amount, debtor:mDebtor, cleared:mCleared});
}
