if (e.target === this) closeInfoModal();
});

let _pendingCopyPeriod = null;

function copyFromPrevious() {
const period = document.getElementById("periodSelect").value;
if (!period) return;
_pendingCopyPeriod = period;
const [m, y] = period.split("/");
const prevM = m === "01" ? "12" : String(Number(m)-1).padStart(2,"0");
const prevY = m === "01" ? String(Number(y)-1) : y;
const prevPeriod = prevM + "/" + prevY;
document.getElementById("copyPrevDesc").innerHTML =
`Reporter les montants du budget de <strong>${prevPeriod}</strong> vers <strong>${period}</strong> ?<br> <span style="color:#e67e22;font-size:12px;">Les valeurs déjà saisies pour ce mois seront écrasées.</span>`;
document.getElementById("copyPrevModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeCopyPrevModal() {
document.getElementById("copyPrevModal").classList.remove("active");
_pendingCopyPeriod = null;
}
document.getElementById("copyPrevModal").addEventListener("click", function(e) {
if (e.target === this) closeCopyPrevModal();
});

function confirmCopyPrev() {
const period = _pendingCopyPeriod;
closeCopyPrevModal();
if (!period) return;
showSpinner();
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(result => {
hideSpinner();
if (result.error) {
showInfoModal("❌ " + result.error);
return;
}
invalidateBudgetCache(period);
loadBudget(true);
showInfoModal(`✅ <strong>${result.copied}</strong> catégorie(s) reportée(s) depuis <strong>${result.from}</strong>.`);
})
.withFailureHandler(err => {
hideSpinner();
showInfoModal("❌ Erreur lors du report : " + (err.message || err));
})
.copyBudgetFromPrevious(period);
}

// ================= DÉPASSEMENT BUDGET =================
let _depassementActive = false;

function toggleDepassement() {
_depassementActive = !_depassementActive;
const btn = document.getElementById("btnDepassement");
btn.className = "btn-depassement" + (_depassementActive ? " active" : "");
btn.title     = _depassementActive ? "Afficher tout" : "Afficher les dépassements";

document.querySelectorAll("tr.cat-row").forEach(row => {
if (_depassementActive) {
row.style.display = row.dataset.isOver === "1" ? "" : "none";
} else {
const header = document.querySelector(`tr.bucket-header[data-bucket="${row.dataset.bucket}"]`);
row.style.display = (header && header.classList.contains("collapsed")) ? "none" : "";
}
});

document.querySelectorAll("tr.bucket-header").forEach(h => {
if (_depassementActive) {
const hasOver = […document.querySelectorAll(`tr.cat-row[data-bucket="${h.dataset.bucket}"]`)]
.some(r => r.dataset.isOver === "1");
h.style.display = hasOver ? "" : "none";
} else {
h.style.display = "";
}
});
}

// ================= TRANSFERT BUDGET =================

// openTransfertFromRow moved to transfert section

// ================= TRANSFERT BUDGET =================
let _transfertSrc    = null;
let _transfertPeriod = null;
let _transfertData   = null;
let _transfertMode   = "simple"; // "simple" | "split"
let _transfertMax    = 0;        // montant max pour le slider

function openTransfertFromRow(tdEl) {
try {
const cat    = JSON.parse(tdEl.getAttribute("data-cat"));
const period = tdEl.getAttribute("data-period");
const allBkts = window._lastBudgetData || [];
openTransfertModal(cat, period, allBkts);
} catch(e) { console.error("openTransfertFromRow:", e); }
}

function openTransfertModal(cat, period, allBuckets) {
_transfertSrc    = cat;
_transfertPeriod = period;
_transfertData   = allBuckets;

const isDeficit = cat.remaining < 0;
const absRem    = Math.abs(cat.remaining);

// Titre + info
document.getElementById("transfertTitle").textContent = isDeficit ? "⚠️ Compenser le dépassement" : "↔️ Transférer le disponible";
document.getElementById("transfertInfo").innerHTML = isDeficit
? `Dépassement de <strong style="color:#D14343;">${formatEuro(absRem)}</strong> dans <strong>${cat.category_name}</strong>. Prélevez du budget d'une autre catégorie.`
: `<strong style="color:#10B981;">${formatEuro(cat.remaining)}</strong> disponible dans <strong>${cat.category_name}</strong>. Transférez vers une autre catégorie.`;

document.getElementById("transfertDestLabel").textContent = isDeficit ? "Prélever depuis :" : "Transférer vers :";

// Slider
const absRem_num = isDeficit ? absRem : Number(cat.remaining);
// Pour déficit : max global = total disponible de toutes les catégories positives de la période
const totalPeriodAvail = isDeficit
? (allBuckets || []).flatMap(b => b.categories).filter(c => c.remaining > 0 && c.category_id !== cat.category_id).reduce((s, c) => s + c.remaining, 0)
: absRem_num;
_transfertMax = isDeficit ? Math.min(absRem_num, totalPeriodAvail) : absRem_num;

const slider  = document.getElementById("transfertSlider");
const inp     = document.getElementById("transfertAmount");
slider.max    = _transfertMax;
slider.step   = _transfertMax > 100 ? 1 : 0.01;
document.getElementById("transfertSliderMax").textContent = formatEuro(_transfertMax);
if (isDeficit) {
// Départ au max (tout compenser) — sera recalibré quand source sélectionnée
slider.value = _transfertMax;
inp.value    = _transfertMax.toFixed(2);
_updateTransfertPct(_transfertMax);
} else {
slider.value = 0;
inp.value    = "";
_updateTransfertPct(0);
}

// Remplir select destination / source
_fillTransfertSelect(isDeficit);

// Reset mode simple
setTransfertMode("simple");
document.getElementById("transfertSplitLines").innerHTML = "";
document.getElementById("transfertSplitTotal").value = isDeficit ? _transfertMax.toFixed(2) : "";
updateTransfertReste();

document.getElementById("transfertModal").classList.add("active");
}

function _fillTransfertSelect(isDeficit) {
const sel = document.getElementById("transfertDest");
sel.innerHTML = "";
const placeholder = document.createElement("option");
placeholder.disabled = true; placeholder.selected = true;
placeholder.textContent = isDeficit ? "— Prélever depuis… —" : "— Choisir une catégorie —";
sel.appendChild(placeholder);

(_transfertData || []).forEach(bucket => {
const grp = document.createElement("optgroup");
grp.label = bucket.bucket_name;
bucket.categories.forEach(c => {
if (c.category_id === (_transfertSrc && _transfertSrc.category_id)) return;
if (isDeficit && c.remaining <= 0) return; // source doit avoir du budget
const opt = document.createElement("option");
opt.value = c.category_id;
// Stocker remaining en data-attr pour mise à jour dynamique du slider
opt.dataset.remaining = c.remaining;
opt.textContent = c.category_name + (isDeficit ? ` — dispo ${formatEuro(c.remaining)}` : "");
grp.appendChild(opt);
});
if (grp.children.length) sel.appendChild(grp);
});

// Sur changement de source (mode compensation) → recalibrer le slider
sel.onchange = () => _onTransfertSourceChange();
}

// Recalibrer slider quand la catégorie source change (mode déficit)
function _onTransfertSourceChange() {
const isDeficit = _transfertSrc && _transfertSrc.remaining < 0;
if (!isDeficit) return;

const sel     = document.getElementById("transfertDest");
const opt     = sel.options[sel.selectedIndex];
const srcAvail = opt ? Number(opt.dataset.remaining || 0) : 0;
const absDeficit = Math.abs(_transfertSrc.remaining);

// Max = min(disponible source, montant à compenser)
const newMax = Math.min(srcAvail, absDeficit);
_transfertMax = newMax;

const slider = document.getElementById("transfertSlider");
slider.max   = newMax;
slider.step  = Math.max(0.01, Math.round(newMax / 100) / 100 * 100);

document.getElementById("transfertSliderMax").textContent = formatEuro(newMax);

// Valeur de départ = min(disponible source, montant à compenser)
const startVal = newMax;
slider.value = startVal;
document.getElementById("transfertAmount").value = startVal.toFixed(2);
_updateTransfertPct(startVal);

// Mettre à jour le champ total ventilé aussi
const splitTotal = document.getElementById("transfertSplitTotal");
if (splitTotal) splitTotal.value = startVal.toFixed(2);
updateTransfertReste();
}

function setTransfertMode(mode) {
_transfertMode = mode;
document.getElementById("transfertSimpleBlock").style.display = mode === "simple" ? "" : "none";
document.getElementById("transfertSplitBlock").style.display  = mode === "split"  ? "" : "none";
document.getElementById("tBtnSimple").className = mode === "simple" ? "active-sortie" : "";
document.getElementById("tBtnSplit").className  = mode === "split"  ? "active-sortie" : "";
if (mode === "split" && !document.querySelectorAll("#transfertSplitLines .transfert-split-line").length) {
addTransfertSplitLine();
}
}

function onTransfertSlider(val) {
const v = Number(val);
document.getElementById("transfertAmount").value = v.toFixed(2);
_updateTransfertPct(v);
}
function onTransfertAmountInput(val) {
const v = Math.min(Number(val) || 0, _transfertMax);
const slider = document.getElementById("transfertSlider");
if (slider) slider.value = v;
_updateTransfertPct(v);
}
function _updateTransfertPct(v) {
const pct = _transfertMax > 0 ? Math.round((v / _transfertMax) * 100) : 0;
document.getElementById("transfertPct").textContent = pct + "%";
}

function addTransfertSplitLine() {
const container = document.getElementById("transfertSplitLines");
const idx = container.querySelectorAll(".transfert-split-line").length;
const div = document.createElement("div");
div.className = "transfert-split-line";
const isDeficit = _transfertSrc && _transfertSrc.remaining < 0;

// Select catégorie
let selectHTML = `<select>`;
selectHTML += `<option value="" disabled selected>${isDeficit ? "Prélever depuis…" : "Vers…"}</option>`;
(_transfertData || []).forEach(bucket => {
selectHTML += `<optgroup label="${bucket.bucket_name}">`;
bucket.categories.forEach(c => {
if (_transfertSrc && c.category_id === _transfertSrc.category_id) return;
if (isDeficit && c.remaining <= 0) return;
selectHTML += `<option value="${c.category_id}">${c.category_name}${isDeficit ? ` (${formatEuro(c.remaining)})` : ""}</option>`;
});
selectHTML += `</optgroup>`;
});
selectHTML += `</select>`;

div.innerHTML = selectHTML +
`<input type="number" placeholder="Montant" min="0" step="0.01" oninput="updateTransfertReste()">` +
`<button class="btn-del-split" onclick="this.closest('.transfert-split-line').remove(); updateTransfertReste();">✕</button>`;
container.appendChild(div);
}

function updateTransfertReste() {
const total  = Number(document.getElementById("transfertSplitTotal").value) || 0;
const lines  = […document.querySelectorAll("#transfertSplitLines .transfert-split-line")];
const used   = lines.reduce((s, l) => {
const inp = l.querySelector("input[type=number]");
return s + (Number(inp ? inp.value : 0) || 0);
}, 0);
const reste = Math.round((total - used) * 100) / 100;
const badge = document.getElementById("transfertResteBadge");
if (!badge) return;
badge.textContent = formatEuro(reste);
badge.className   = "reste-badge " + (Math.abs(reste) < 0.01 ? "ok" : "nok");
}

function closeTransfertModal() {
document.getElementById("transfertModal").classList.remove("active");
_transfertSrc = null;
}

document.getElementById("transfertModal").addEventListener("click", function(e) {
if (e.target === this) closeTransfertModal();
});

function confirmTransfert() {
if (!_transfertSrc) return;
const period    = _transfertPeriod;
const srcId     = _transfertSrc.category_id;
const isDeficit = _transfertSrc.remaining < 0;
const allCats   = (_transfertData || []).flatMap(b => b.categories);

const onError = (err) => { hideSpinner(); console.error("Erreur transfert:", err); showInfoModal("❌ Erreur: " + (err.message || err)); };

if (_transfertMode === "split") {
// — MODE VENTILÉ —
const total = Number(document.getElementById("transfertSplitTotal").value) || 0;
if (!total) return;
const lines = […document.querySelectorAll("#transfertSplitLines .transfert-split-line")];
const parts = lines.map(l => ({
catId:  l.querySelector("select").value,
amount: Number(l.querySelector("input[type=number]").value) || 0,
})).filter(p => p.catId && p.amount > 0);
if (!parts.length) return;

```
closeTransfertModal();
showSpinner();

// Modifier source d'abord
const srcBudget = isDeficit ? _transfertSrc.budgeted + total : _transfertSrc.budgeted - total;
let remaining = parts.length;

_gas()
  .withSuccessHandler(() => {
    // Modifier chaque destination en série
    let i = 0;
    function nextPart() {
      if (i >= parts.length) {
        hideSpinner();
        invalidateBudgetCache(period);
        loadBudget(true);
        return;
      }
      const p = parts[i++];
      const destCat    = allCats.find(c => c.category_id === p.catId);
      const destBudget = isDeficit
        ? (destCat ? destCat.budgeted - p.amount : 0)
        : (destCat ? destCat.budgeted + p.amount : 0);
      _gas()
        .withSuccessHandler(nextPart)
        .withFailureHandler(onError)
        .saveBudget(period, p.catId, destBudget);
    }
    nextPart();
  })
  .withFailureHandler(onError)
  .saveBudget(period, srcId, srcBudget);
```

} else {
// — MODE SIMPLE —
const destId = document.getElementById("transfertDest").value;
const amount = Number(document.getElementById("transfertAmount").value);
if (!amount || amount <= 0) return;
if (!destId) { showInfoModal("⚠️ Choisissez une catégorie destination."); return; }

```
const srcBudget  = isDeficit ? _transfertSrc.budgeted + amount : _transfertSrc.budgeted - amount;
const destCat    = allCats.find(c => c.category_id === destId);
const destBudget = isDeficit ? (destCat ? destCat.budgeted - amount : 0) : (destCat ? destCat.budgeted + amount : 0);

closeTransfertModal();
showSpinner();

_gas()
  .withSuccessHandler(() => {
    _gas()
      .withSuccessHandler(() => {
        hideSpinner();
        invalidateBudgetCache(period);
        loadBudget(true);
      })
      .withFailureHandler(onError)
      .saveBudget(period, destId, destBudget);
  })
  .withFailureHandler(onError)
  .saveBudget(period, srcId, srcBudget);
```

}
}

// ================= PREVISIONS =================
let _receivedCollapsed = true;

function _buildPrevRow(p) {
const div = document.createElement("div");
const isReceived = p.is_fully_received || false;
const amtReceived = p.amount_received || 0;
const amtTotal    = Math.abs(Number(p.amount) || 0);
const pct         = amtTotal > 0 ? Math.min(100, Math.round(amtReceived / amtTotal * 100)) : 0;
const partial     = amtReceived > 0 && !isReceived;

div.className = "prevision-row" + (isReceived ? " received" : "") + (!isReceived ? " prevision-row-clickable" : "");
if (!isReceived) {
div.addEventListener("click", e => {
if (e.target.closest("button")) return;
openEditPrevision(p.id);
});
}

// Transactions liées à cet attendu
const linkedTxs = allTransactions.filter(t => t.linked_prevision_id === p.id);
const linkedHtml = linkedTxs.map(t =>
`<div class="prev-linked-tx"> <span>${t.date} · ${t.description || t.category || "—"}</span> <span class="prev-linked-amt">+${formatEuro(Math.abs(Number(t.amount)))}</span> <button class="btn-prev-unlink-tx" onclick="event.stopPropagation();_unlinkTxFromPrev('${t.id}')" title="Délier">✕</button> </div>`
).join("");

// Barre progression
const barColor = pct >= 100 ? "var(--green)" : pct >= 60 ? "#F39C12" : "var(--primary)";
const progressHtml = amtReceived > 0 ? `<div class="prev-progress-bar"> <div class="prev-progress-fill" style="width:${pct}%;background:${barColor};"></div> </div> <div class="prev-progress-label">${formatEuro(amtReceived)} / ${formatEuro(amtTotal)} (${pct}%)</div>` : "";

div.innerHTML = `<div class="prevision-content"> <div class="prevision-main"> <span class="prevision-cat">${p.category || "—"}</span> <span class="prevision-amount"> ${isReceived ?`<span class="received-badge">✅ Soldé</span>`: partial ?`<span class="partial-badge">⏳ ${pct}%</span>`:`+${formatEuro(amtTotal)}`} </span> </div> <div class="prevision-meta">${p.date}${p.description ? " · " + p.description : ""}</div> ${progressHtml} ${linkedHtml} </div> <div class="prevision-actions"> ${!isReceived ? `
<button class="btn-prev-recu" onclick="openLinkTxModal('${p.id}')" title="Lier une transaction">🔗 Lier</button>
<button class="btn-prev-close" onclick="_closePrevision('${p.id}')" title="Clôturer sans régler">✕ Clôturer</button>
`: ""} </div>`;
return div;
}

function toggleReceivedSection() {
_receivedCollapsed = !_receivedCollapsed;
const list   = document.getElementById("prevReceivedList");
const toggle = document.getElementById("prevReceivedToggle");
if (list)   list.style.display   = _receivedCollapsed ? "none" : "";
if (toggle) toggle.className = "prev-received-toggle" + (_receivedCollapsed ? " collapsed" : "");
}

function renderPrevisions() {
const container = document.getElementById("previsionsContainer");
if (!container) return;
container.innerHTML = "";

// Calculer montant reçu par prévision depuis les transactions liées
const _prvReceived = {};
allTransactions.forEach(t => {
if (t.linked_prevision_id) {
const amt = Math.abs(Number(t.amount) || 0);
_prvReceived[t.linked_prevision_id] = (_prvReceived[t.linked_prevision_id] || 0) + amt;
}
});
// Enrichir les prévisions avec amount_received + is_fully_received
const enriched = allPrevisions.map(p => ({
…p,
amount_received: _prvReceived[p.id] || 0,
is_fully_received: (_prvReceived[p.id] || 0) >= Number(p.amount) - 0.01
}));

const pending  = enriched.filter(p => !p.is_fully_received);
const received = enriched.filter(p =>  p.is_fully_received);

_updatePrevisionsCount();
if (!allPrevisions.length) {
container.innerHTML = `<div class="previsions-empty">Aucun revenu attendu saisi</div>`;
updateProjection();
return;
}

// En attente
let total = 0;
if (!pending.length) {
container.innerHTML += `<div class="previsions-empty" style="font-size:12px;">Tous les revenus ont été reçus 🎉</div>`;
} else {
pending.forEach(p => {
total += Number(p.amount) || 0;
container.appendChild(_buildPrevRow(p));
});
const tot = document.createElement("div");
tot.className = "previsions-total";
tot.innerHTML = `<span class="previsions-total-label">Total en attente</span> <span class="previsions-total-value">+${formatEuro(total)}</span>`;
container.appendChild(tot);
}

// Sous-section Reçus (repliable)
if (received.length) {
const section = document.createElement("div");
section.className = "prev-received-section";

```
const toggle = document.createElement("div");
toggle.id = "prevReceivedToggle";
toggle.className = "prev-received-toggle" + (_receivedCollapsed ? " collapsed" : "");
toggle.onclick = toggleReceivedSection;
toggle.innerHTML = `
  <div class="prev-received-toggle-line"></div>
  <span class="prev-received-toggle-label">✅ Reçus (${received.length})</span>
  <span class="prev-received-toggle-icon">▼</span>
  <div class="prev-received-toggle-line"></div>
`;
section.appendChild(toggle);

const list = document.createElement("div");
list.id = "prevReceivedList";
list.style.display = _receivedCollapsed ? "none" : "";
received.forEach(p => list.appendChild(_buildPrevRow(p)));
section.appendChild(list);

container.appendChild(section);
```

}

updateProjection();
}

function _deletePrevFromModal() {
if (!_editingPrevId) return;
const id = _editingPrevId;
closePrevisionModal();
openDeletePrevision(id);
}
function openPrevisionModal(id) {
_editingPrevId = id || null;
document.getElementById("previsionModalTitle").textContent =
id ? "Modifier le revenu attendu" : "Nouveau revenu attendu";
const _pd = document.getElementById("prevModalDeleteBtn");
if (_pd) _pd.style.display = id ? "block" : "none";
if (id) {
const p = allPrevisions.find(x => x.id === id);
if (!p) return;
const parts = (p.date||"").split("/");
document.getElementById("prevModalDate").value   = parts.length===3 ? `${parts[2]}-${parts[1]}-${parts[0]}` : p.date;
document.getElementById("prevModalDesc").value   = p.description || "";
_tpeSet("prevModalAmount", Math.abs(p.amount));
fillCategorySelect("prevModalCat", allCategories, p.category_id);
} else {
document.getElementById("prevModalDate").value   = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
document.getElementById("prevModalDesc").value   = "";
_tpeSet("prevModalAmount", 0);
fillCategorySelect("prevModalCat", allCategories);
}
document.getElementById("previsionModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closePrevisionModal() {
document.getElementById("previsionModal").classList.remove("active");
_editingPrevId = null;
}

document.getElementById("previsionModal").addEventListener("click", function(e) {
if (e.target === this) closePrevisionModal();
});

let _linkTxPrevId     = null;
let _linkTxSelectedIds = new Set();

// ── Ouvrir le modal de liaison depuis une prévision ──
function openLinkTxModal(prevId) {
_linkTxPrevId = prevId;
_linkTxSelectedIds = new Set();

const p = allPrevisions.find(x => x.id === prevId);
if (!p) return;

// Info prévision
const amtTotal    = Math.abs(Number(p.amount) || 0);
const amtReceived = p.amount_received || 0;
const amtLeft     = amtTotal - amtReceived;
const info = document.getElementById("linkTxPrevInfo");
if (info) info.innerHTML = `<strong>${p.category}</strong> · ${p.description || ""} · <span style="color:var(--primary);font-weight:700;">Attendu : ${formatEuro(amtTotal)}</span>${amtReceived > 0 ? ` · <span style="color:var(--green);">Déjà reçu : ${formatEuro(amtReceived)}</span>` : ""}`;

// Transactions entrantes : liables = pas skip_link, sauf déjà liées à CET attendu
const allEntries = allTransactions.filter(t => Number(t.amount) < 0);
const entries    = allEntries.filter(t =>
!t.skip_link && (!t.linked_prevision_id || t.linked_prevision_id === prevId)
);
const skipped    = allEntries.filter(t =>
t.skip_link && !t.linked_prevision_id
);

const list = document.getElementById("linkTxList");
const none = document.getElementById("linkTxNone");
const confirmBtn = document.getElementById("linkTxConfirmBtn");
list.innerHTML = "";
confirmBtn.disabled = true;
confirmBtn.style.opacity = "0.4";

function _renderLinkList() {
list.innerHTML = "";
if (!entries.length && !skipped.length) {
list.style.display = "none";
none.style.display = "block";
return;
}
list.style.display = ""; none.style.display = "none";

```
// Transactions liables
entries.forEach(t => {
  const alreadyLinked = t.linked_prevision_id === prevId;
  const div = document.createElement("div");
  div.className = "tx-pick-item" + (alreadyLinked ? " selected" : "");
  if (alreadyLinked) _linkTxSelectedIds.add(t.id);
  div.innerHTML = `
    <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;">
      <div style="font-weight:600;">${t.date} · ${t.category}${t.description ? " · " + t.description : ""}</div>
      ${alreadyLinked ? '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--green);">Déjà lié</div>' : ""}
    </div>
    <span style="color:#27ae60;font-weight:700;white-space:nowrap;margin-right:6px;">+${formatEuro(Math.abs(Number(t.amount)))}</span>
    <button class="btn-link-toggle" title="Marquer comme ponctuel (masquer)" onclick="event.stopPropagation();_setTxSkipLink('${t.id}', true)">🚫</button>
  `;
  div.addEventListener("click", e => {
    if (e.target.classList.contains("btn-link-toggle")) return;
    if (_linkTxSelectedIds.has(t.id)) { _linkTxSelectedIds.delete(t.id); div.classList.remove("selected"); }
    else { _linkTxSelectedIds.add(t.id); div.classList.add("selected"); }
    confirmBtn.disabled = _linkTxSelectedIds.size === 0;
    confirmBtn.style.opacity = _linkTxSelectedIds.size > 0 ? "1" : "0.4";
  });
  list.appendChild(div);
});

// Section ponctuels masqués (repliable)
if (skipped.length) {
  const sepDiv = document.createElement("div");
  sepDiv.style.cssText = "font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);padding:8px 4px 4px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;cursor:pointer;";
  sepDiv.textContent = "🚫 Ponctuels " + skipped.length;
  let skippedVisible = false;
  const skippedContainer = document.createElement("div");
  skippedContainer.style.display = "none";
  sepDiv.onclick = () => {
    skippedVisible = !skippedVisible;
    skippedContainer.style.display = skippedVisible ? "" : "none";
    sepDiv.textContent = (skippedVisible ? "🔼" : "🚫") + " Ponctuels " + skipped.length;
  };
  skipped.forEach(t => {
    const div = document.createElement("div");
    div.className = "tx-pick-item";
    div.style.opacity = "0.5";
    div.innerHTML = `
      <div style="flex:1;min-width:0;font-size:13px;">${t.date} · ${t.category}${t.description ? " · " + t.description : ""}</div>
      <span style="color:#27ae60;font-weight:700;white-space:nowrap;margin-right:6px;">+${formatEuro(Math.abs(Number(t.amount)))}</span>
      <button class="btn-link-toggle" style="color:var(--green);" title="Remettre comme attendu" onclick="event.stopPropagation();_setTxSkipLink('${t.id}', false)">↩</button>
    `;
    skippedContainer.appendChild(div);
  });
  list.appendChild(sepDiv);
  list.appendChild(skippedContainer);
}
```

}
_renderLinkList();
document.getElementById("linkTxModal").classList.add("active");
}

function _closeLinkTxModal() {
document.getElementById("linkTxModal").classList.remove("active");
_linkTxPrevId = null;
_linkTxSelectedIds = new Set();
}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", () => {
const m = document.getElementById("linkTxModal");
if (m) m.addEventListener("click", e => { if (e.target === m) _closeLinkTxModal(); });
});

function _confirmLinkTx() {
if (!_linkTxPrevId || _linkTxSelectedIds.size === 0) return;
const prevId = _linkTxPrevId;
const txIds  = […_linkTxSelectedIds];
_closeLinkTxModal();
showSpinner();
// Un seul appel GAS avec toutes les tx
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(data => {
hideSpinner();
allTransactions = _normalizeTxList(data.transactions);
allPrevisions   = data.previsions || allPrevisions;
renderPrevisions();
updateProjection();
})
.withFailureHandler(err => {
hideSpinner();
showInfoModal("❌ Erreur liaison : " + (err.message || err));
})
.linkTransactionsToPrevision(txIds, prevId);
}

// ── Marquer une tx comme ponctuelle (skip_link) ou attendue ──
function _setTxSkipLink(txId, skip, e) {
if (e) { e.stopPropagation(); closeAllMenus(); }
const tx = allTransactions.find(t => t.id === txId);
if (tx) tx.skip_link = skip;
showSpinner();
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(data => {
hideSpinner();
allTransactions = _normalizeTxList(data.transactions || data);
if (_linkTxPrevId) openLinkTxModal(_linkTxPrevId); // rafraîchir modal si ouvert
else applyFilters(); // rafraîchir la liste banque
})
.withFailureHandler(() => { hideSpinner(); })
.setTransactionSkipLink(txId, skip);
}

// ── Délier une transaction depuis la ligne de prévision ──
function _closePrevision(prevId) {
const p = allPrevisions.find(x => x.id === prevId);
if (!p) return;
const label = (p.category || "") + (p.description ? " · " + p.description : "");
if (!confirm("Clôturer cet attendu sans le solder ?\n" + label + "\n\nIl disparaîtra de la liste et de la projection.")) return;
showSpinner();
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(updated => {
hideSpinner();
allPrevisions = updated || allPrevisions;
renderPrevisions();
updateProjection();
})
.withFailureHandler(err => {
hideSpinner();
showInfoModal("❌ Erreur : " + (err.message || err));
})
.closePrevision(prevId);
}

function _unlinkTxFromPrev(txId) {
showSpinner();
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(data => {
hideSpinner();
allTransactions = _normalizeTxList(data.transactions);
allPrevisions   = data.previsions || allPrevisions;
renderPrevisions();
updateProjection();
})
.withFailureHandler(err => {
hideSpinner();
showInfoModal("❌ Erreur : " + (err.message || err));
})
.unlinkTransactionFromPrevision(txId);
}

function unlinkPrevision(id) {
// Ancienne fonction conservée pour compatibilité
_unlinkTxFromPrev(id);
}
function openEditPrevision(id) { openPrevisionModal(id); }

function openDeletePrevision(id) {
_deletePrevId = id;
const p = allPrevisions.find(x => x.id === id);
document.getElementById("deleteModalDesc").textContent =
p ? `${p.date} — ${p.category} — ${formatEuro(p.amount)}` : id;
document.getElementById("deleteModal").classList.add("active");
// Hijack confirmDelete for prevision
window._deleteIsPrevision = true;
}

function savePrevisionModal() {
// IMPORTANT: capturer AVANT closePrevisionModal() qui efface _editingPrevId
const editId = _editingPrevId;
const fn     = editId ? "updatePrevision" : "addPrevision";
const form   = {
id:          editId,
date:        document.getElementById("prevModalDate").value,
description: document.getElementById("prevModalDesc").value,
category_id: document.getElementById("prevModalCat").value,
amount:      Math.abs(Number(document.getElementById("prevModalAmount").value) || 0)
};
if (!form.amount) return;
closePrevisionModal(); // efface _editingPrevId — mais editId et fn déjà capturés
showSpinner();
_gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
hideSpinner();
allPrevisions = updated;
renderPrevisions();
updateProjection();
})[fn](form);
}

// ================= VERROUILLAGE RAPPROCHEMENT =================
function openLockModal() {
// Calculer le solde pointé
let soldePointe = 0;
allTransactions.forEach(t => {
if (t.cleared) soldePointe += -(Number(t.amount) || 0);
});

const hasCleared = allTransactions.some(t => t.cleared && !t.locked);
if (!hasCleared) {
showInfoModal("ℹ️ Aucune transaction pointée non verrouillée à verrouiller.");
return;
}

document.getElementById("lockModalSolde").textContent = formatEuro(soldePointe);
document.getElementById("lockModalSolde").style.color = soldePointe >= 0 ? "#27ae60" : "#c0392b";
document.getElementById("lockModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeLockModal() {
document.getElementById("lockModal").classList.remove("active");
}

document.getElementById("lockModal").addEventListener("click", function(e) {
if (e.target === this) closeLockModal();
});

function confirmLockAll() {
closeLockModal();
showSpinner();
_gas().withSuccessHandler(updated => {
hideSpinner();
afterMutation(updated, "Verrouillage rapprochement");
}).lockAllCleared();
}

// ================= UNDO =================
// ===== UNDO / REDO =====

function _setUndoBtn(label) {
// Bouton header (desktop)
const btn = document.getElementById("undoTopBtn");
if (btn) {
if (label) {
btn.classList.add("available");
btn.title = "↩ Annuler : " + label;
btn.style.opacity = "";
} else {
btn.classList.remove("available");
btn.title = "Rien à annuler";
btn.style.opacity = "";
}
}
// Bouton nav (mobile — toujours visible)
const navBtn = document.getElementById("undoNavBtn");
if (navBtn) {
if (label) {
navBtn.classList.add("available");
navBtn.title = "↩ Annuler : " + label;
} else {
navBtn.classList.remove("available");
navBtn.title = "Rien à annuler";
}
}
}

function showUndoBar(label) {
_setUndoBtn(label);
// Redo becomes unavailable when a new action is recorded
}

function closeUndoBar() { _setUndoBtn(null); }

function doUndo() {
const topBtn  = document.getElementById("undoTopBtn");
const drawBtn = document.getElementById("drawerUndoBtn");
const navBtn  = document.getElementById("undoNavBtn");
const avail   = (topBtn  && topBtn.classList.contains("available"))
|| (drawBtn && drawBtn.classList.contains("available"))
|| (navBtn  && navBtn.classList.contains("available"));
if (!avail) return;
const raw = (topBtn  && topBtn.title  && topBtn.classList.contains("available"))  ? topBtn.title.replace("↩ Annuler : ","").replace("Annuler : ","").trim()
: (navBtn  && navBtn.title  && navBtn.classList.contains("available"))   ? navBtn.title.replace("↩ Annuler : ","").replace("Annuler : ","").trim()
: (drawBtn && drawBtn.title && drawBtn.classList.contains("available"))  ? drawBtn.title.replace("Annuler : ","").trim()
: "Dernière action";
document.getElementById("undoPopupAction").textContent = raw;
const cb = document.getElementById("undoPopupConfirmBtn");
if (cb) cb.textContent = "↩ Annuler";
const lb = document.getElementById("undoPopupLabel");
if (lb) lb.textContent = "Annuler la dernière action";
const popup = document.getElementById("undoPopup");
if (popup) { delete popup.dataset.mode; popup.classList.add("visible"); }
clearTimeout(window._undoPopupTimer);
window._undoPopupTimer = setTimeout(closeUndoPopup, 6000);
if (typeof closeDrawer === "function") closeDrawer();
}

function closeUndoPopup() {
clearTimeout(window._undoPopupTimer);
const popup = document.getElementById("undoPopup");
popup.classList.remove("visible");
}

function doUndoConfirmed() {
const popup = document.getElementById("undoPopup");
closeUndoPopup();

const btn = document.getElementById("undoTopBtn");
if (btn) btn.classList.remove("available");
showSpinner();

const gasFn = "undoLastAction";

_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(result => {
hideSpinner();
if (!result) { showInfoModal("Rien à annuler."); return; }
if (result.error) { showInfoModal("❌ " + result.error); if (btn) btn.classList.add("available"); return; }
if (result.transactions) refreshHistory(result.transactions);
if (result.previsions) {
allPrevisions = result.previsions;
renderPrevisions();
updateProjection();
}
if (result.settings) {
allCategories = result.settings.categories || allCategories;
allBuckets    = result.settings.buckets    || allBuckets;
allDebtors    = result.settings.debtors    || allDebtors;
renderSettings();
_refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
}
if (result.budget && result.period) {
invalidateBudgetCache(result.period);
loadBudget(true);
}
// Refresh both buttons
_checkUndoAvailable();
})
.withFailureHandler(err => {
hideSpinner();
if (btn) btn.classList.add("available");
showInfoModal("Erreur: " + (err&&err.message?err.message:String(err)));
})
[gasFn]();
}

function _checkUndoAvailable() {
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(info => {
const label = (info && info.label) ? info.label : null;
_setUndoBtn(label);
// Bouton drawer également
const drawerBtn = document.getElementById("drawerUndoBtn");
const drawerSub = document.getElementById("drawerUndoSub");
if (drawerBtn) {
if (label) {
drawerBtn.style.opacity = "1"; drawerBtn.classList.add("available");
drawerBtn.title = "Annuler : " + label;
if (drawerSub) drawerSub.textContent = label;
} else {
drawerBtn.style.opacity = "0.5"; drawerBtn.classList.remove("available");
drawerBtn.title = "Rien à annuler";
if (drawerSub) drawerSub.textContent = "Rien à annuler";
}
}
})
.getUndoInfo();
}

// ===== DEBTORS DATALIST =====
// ===== AUTOCOMPLETE DÉBITEUR CUSTOM =====
// wrapId = l'id du div.debtor-wrap, catSelectId = select catégorie associé

function fillDebtorDatalist() {
// Compat : mise à jour des éventuels datalist restants (modal d'ajout banque)
["modalDebtorList"].forEach(id => {
const dl = document.getElementById(id);
if (!dl) return;
dl.innerHTML = "";
allDebtors.forEach(d => {
const opt = document.createElement("option");
opt.value = d.name;
dl.appendChild(opt);
});
});
// Rafraîchir tous les wraps ouverts
document.querySelectorAll(".debtor-dropdown.open").forEach(dd => {
const wrapId = dd.id.replace("Dropdown","");
_renderDebtorOptions(wrapId, document.getElementById(wrapId.replace("Wrap","") + "Input") || document.querySelector(`#${wrapId} input`));
});
}

// Auto-fill catégorie quand débiteur sélectionné par son nom
function _applyDebtorCategory(name, catSelectId) {
if (!name) return;
const d = allDebtors.find(x => x.name.toLowerCase() === name.toLowerCase());
if (d && d.default_category_id && catSelectId) {
const sel = document.getElementById(catSelectId);
if (sel) sel.value = d.default_category_id;
}
}

// Compat ancienne signature
function onDebtorChange(debtorInputId, catSelectId) {
_applyDebtorCategory(document.getElementById(debtorInputId).value, catSelectId);
}

// Rendre les options dans le dropdown
function _renderDebtorOptions(wrapId, inputEl) {
const dd     = document.getElementById(wrapId + "Dropdown");
if (!dd) return;
const query  = (inputEl ? inputEl.value : "").toLowerCase().trim();
const _sortDebtors = arr => […arr].sort((a, b) => {
const catA = (allCategories.find(x => x.id === a.default_category_id) || {}).name || "zzz";
const catB = (allCategories.find(x => x.id === b.default_category_id) || {}).name || "zzz";
const cmp = catA.localeCompare(catB, 'fr', {sensitivity:'base'});
if (cmp !== 0) return cmp;
return (a.name || '').localeCompare(b.name || '', 'fr', {sensitivity:'base'});
});
const list = _sortDebtors(
query ? allDebtors.filter(d => d.name.toLowerCase().includes(query)) : allDebtors
);

dd.innerHTML = "";
if (!list.length) {
dd.innerHTML = `<div class="debtor-empty">${query ? ("Aucun résultat pour \"" + query + "\"") : "Aucun bénéficiaire enregistré"}</div>`;
const _addE = document.createElement("div");
_addE.className = "debtor-add-btn";
_addE.innerHTML = `<span class="debtor-add-icon">＋</span> Créer "${query || "bénéficiaire"}"`;
_addE.addEventListener("mousedown", e => e.preventDefault());
_addE.addEventListener("click", () => { closeDebtorDropdown(wrapId); openAddDebtor(query); });
dd.appendChild(_addE);
return;
}
let _lastCat = null;
list.forEach((d, i) => {
const cat = allCategories.find(c => c.id === d.default_category_id);
const catName = cat ? cat.name : null;
// Insérer un séparateur de catégorie quand elle change
if (catName !== _lastCat) {
const sep = document.createElement("div");
sep.className = "debtor-cat-sep";
sep.textContent = catName || "Sans catégorie";
dd.appendChild(sep);
_lastCat = catName;
}
const div = document.createElement("div");
div.className = "debtor-option";
div.dataset.idx = i;
div.textContent = d.name;
div.addEventListener("mousedown", e => e.preventDefault());
div.addEventListener("click", () => {
if (inputEl) inputEl.value = d.name;
_applyDebtorCategory(d.name, dd.dataset.catSelect);
closeDebtorDropdown(wrapId);
});
dd.appendChild(div);
});
const _addD = document.createElement("div");
_addD.className = "debtor-add-btn";
const _hint = inputEl && inputEl.value.trim() ? `"${inputEl.value.trim()}"` : "";
_addD.innerHTML = `<span class="debtor-add-icon">＋</span> Créer ${_hint || "un bénéficiaire"}`;
_addD.addEventListener("mousedown", e => e.preventDefault());
_addD.addEventListener("click", () => {
const _n = inputEl ? inputEl.value.trim() : "";
closeDebtorDropdown(wrapId);
openAddDebtor(_n);
});
dd.appendChild(_addD);
}

function openDebtorDropdown(wrapId) {
const dd    = document.getElementById(wrapId + "Dropdown");
const input = document.querySelector("#" + wrapId + " input");
if (!dd || !input) return;
dd.dataset.catSelect = dd.dataset.catSelect || "";
dd.classList.add("open");
_renderDebtorOptions(wrapId, input);
_debtorHighlight(wrapId, -1);
}

function closeDebtorDropdown(wrapId) {
const dd = document.getElementById(wrapId + "Dropdown");
if (dd) { dd.classList.remove("open"); _debtorHlIdx[wrapId] = -1; }
}

function scheduleCloseDebtor(wrapId) {
window._closeDebtorTimer = setTimeout(() => closeDebtorDropdown(wrapId), 200);
}

function toggleDebtorDropdown(wrapId, catSelectId) {
const dd = document.getElementById(wrapId + "Dropdown");
if (!dd) return;
dd.dataset.catSelect = catSelectId;
if (dd.classList.contains("open")) {
closeDebtorDropdown(wrapId);
} else {
const input = document.querySelector("#" + wrapId + " input");
openDebtorDropdown(wrapId);
}
}

function onDebtorTyping(wrapId, catSelectId) {
const dd    = document.getElementById(wrapId + "Dropdown");
const input = document.querySelector("#" + wrapId + " input");
if (!dd) return;
dd.dataset.catSelect = catSelectId;
dd.classList.add("open");
_renderDebtorOptions(wrapId, input);
_debtorHighlight(wrapId, -1);
// Auto-fill catégorie si correspondance exacte
_applyDebtorCategory(input.value, catSelectId);
}

// Gestion clavier : ↑↓ pour naviguer, Tab/Entrée pour sélectionner
const _debtorHlIdx = {};

function _debtorHighlight(wrapId, idx) {
const dd = document.getElementById(wrapId + "Dropdown");
if (!dd) return;
const opts = […dd.querySelectorAll(".debtor-option")];
opts.forEach(o => o.classList.remove("highlighted"));
_debtorHlIdx[wrapId] = idx;
if (idx >= 0 && idx < opts.length) {
opts[idx].classList.add("highlighted");
opts[idx].scrollIntoView({ block: "nearest" });
}
}

function onDebtorKeydown(e, wrapId, catSelectId) {
const dd    = document.getElementById(wrapId + "Dropdown");
const input = document.querySelector("#" + wrapId + " input");
if (!dd) return;

const isOpen = dd.classList.contains("open");
const opts   = […dd.querySelectorAll(".debtor-option")];
let hlIdx    = _debtorHlIdx[wrapId] || -1;

if (e.key === "ArrowDown") {
e.preventDefault();
if (!isOpen) { dd.dataset.catSelect = catSelectId; openDebtorDropdown(wrapId); return; }
hlIdx = Math.min(hlIdx + 1, opts.length - 1);
_debtorHighlight(wrapId, hlIdx);
} else if (e.key === "ArrowUp") {
e.preventDefault();
hlIdx = Math.max(hlIdx - 1, 0);
_debtorHighlight(wrapId, hlIdx);
} else if ((e.key === "Tab" || e.key === "Enter") && isOpen && hlIdx >= 0 && opts[hlIdx]) {
if (e.key === "Tab") e.preventDefault();
opts[hlIdx].click();
} else if (e.key === "Escape") {
closeDebtorDropdown(wrapId);
}
}

document.body.classList.add("drawer-open");
document.getElementById("drawerOverlay").classList.add("open");
// Mettre à jour le solde affiché
updateDrawerSolde();
}

// Ouvre la modale de gestion (categories / buckets / debtors)
function openSettingsModal(type) {
_currentSettingsType = type;
const titles   = { categories: "📂 Catégories", buckets: "🗂 Groupes", debtors: "👤 Bénéficiaires" };
const addFns   = { categories: "openAddCat",    buckets: "openAddBucket", debtors: "openAddDebtor" };
const titleEl  = document.getElementById("settingsMgmtTitle");
const addBtn   = document.getElementById("settingsMgmtAddBtn");
const bodyEl   = document.getElementById("settingsMgmtBody");

titleEl.textContent = titles[type] || type;
addBtn.onclick = () => window[addFns[type]]();

renderSettingsMgmt(type, bodyEl);
document.getElementById("settingsMgmtModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeSettingsModal() {
document.getElementById("settingsMgmtModal").classList.remove("active");
_currentSettingsType = null;
}

grouped[cat.bucket_id].push(cat);

```
    div.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
      if (e.target.classList.contains('debtor-sel-chk') || e.target.type === 'checkbox') return;
      openEditDebtor(d.id);
    });
    container.appendChild(div);
  });
}
```

}
}

// Après mutation settings → rafraîchit la modale si ouverte
function _refreshSettingsMgmtIfOpen() {
if (!_currentSettingsType) return;
const bodyEl = document.getElementById("settingsMgmtBody");
if (bodyEl) renderSettingsMgmt(_currentSettingsType, bodyEl);
openDrawer(); // Mettre à jour les compteurs du menu
}

function closeDrawer() {
if (_drawerPinned) return;
_doCloseDrawer();
}

function _doCloseDrawer() {
document.getElementById("sideDrawer").classList.remove("open");
document.body.classList.remove("drawer-open");
document.getElementById("drawerOverlay").classList.remove("open");
// Remettre settingsSection dans le DOM principal
const section = document.getElementById("settingsSection");
const sheet   = document.getElementById("mainSheet");
if (section && sheet) {
section.style.display = "none";
sheet.appendChild(section);
}
}

function togglePin() {
_drawerPinned = !_drawerPinned;
const btn = document.getElementById("btnPin");
const drawer = document.getElementById("sideDrawer");
const overlay = document.getElementById("drawerOverlay");
if (_drawerPinned) {
btn.classList.add("pinned");
document.body.classList.add("drawer-pinned");
btn.title = "Épinglé — cliquer pour désépingler";
drawer.classList.add("drawer-pinned");
overlay.classList.remove("open");
document.body.classList.add("drawer-pinned-mode");
_syncSelectionBar();   // APRÈS l'ajout de drawer-pinned-mode
} else {
btn.classList.remove("pinned");
document.body.classList.remove("drawer-pinned");
btn.title = "Épingler le volet";
drawer.classList.remove("drawer-pinned");
document.body.classList.remove("drawer-pinned-mode");
_syncSelectionBar();   // APRÈS la suppression de drawer-pinned-mode
}
}

// Settings est maintenant dans le drawer
openDrawer();
}

// –– CATEGORIES LIST ––
// ===== Helpers section collapse =====
function toggleSettingsSection(bodyId, chevronId) {
const body    = document.getElementById(bodyId);
const chevron = document.getElementById(chevronId);
if (!body) return;
const isHidden = body.classList.toggle("hidden");
const header   = chevron ? chevron.closest(".settings-collapse-header") : null;
if (header)   header.classList.toggle("closed", isHidden);
// Mettre à jour le label s'il existe
const labelId = bodyId.replace("Body","CollapseLabel");
const label   = document.getElementById(labelId);
if (label) {
const section = bodyId.replace("Body","");
const counts = { buckets: allBuckets.length, debtors: allDebtors.length };
const n = counts[section] || 0;
label.textContent = isHidden ? `Voir (${n})` : "Replier";
}
}

// ===== Refresh all category dropdowns after settings mutation =====
function _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns() {
// Refresh tiers filter too
if (typeof populateFilters === "function") populateFilters();
fillCategorySelect("simpleCategory",      allCategories);
fillCategorySelect("modalSimpleCategory", allCategories);
fillCategorySelect("prevModalCat",        allCategories);
fillCategorySelect("editModalCat",        allCategories);
// Refresh tiers filter with updated debtors list
populateFilters();
fillCategorySelect("catModalBucket",      allBuckets, null, true); // bucket select
fillDebtorDatalist();
}

function expandAllCatGroups() {
document.querySelectorAll("#categoriesSettingsList2 .smgmt-group-items").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("hidden"));
document.querySelectorAll("#categoriesSettingsList2 .smgmt-bucket-header").forEach(el => el.classList.remove("closed"));
}
function collapseAllCatGroups() {
document.querySelectorAll("#categoriesSettingsList2 .smgmt-group-items").forEach(el => el.classList.add("hidden"));
document.querySelectorAll("#categoriesSettingsList2 .smgmt-bucket-header").forEach(el => el.classList.add("closed"));
}
function renderCategoriesList() {
const container = document.getElementById("categoriesSettingsList");
if (!container) return;
container.innerHTML = "";

// Grouper les catégories par bucket
const grouped = {};
const noBucket = [];
allCategories.forEach(cat => {
if (cat.bucket_id) {
if (!grouped[cat.bucket_id]) grouped[cat.bucket_id] = [];
grouped[cat.bucket_id].push(cat);
} else {
noBucket.push(cat);
}
});

// Fonction pour créer un item catégorie (avec drag & drop)
function makeCatItem(cat, idx, total) {
const div = document.createElement("div");
div.className = "settings-item";
div.dataset.id = cat.id;
div.innerHTML = ` <div class="settings-item-info"> <span class="settings-item-name">${cat.name}</span> </div> <div class="settings-item-actions" style="display:flex;gap:4px;align-items:center;"> <button class="btn-icon" title="Monter" onclick="_moveItem(this,'up','cat')" ${idx===0?'disabled style="opacity:.3"':''}>↑</button> <button class="btn-icon" title="Descendre" onclick="_moveItem(this,'down','cat')" ${idx===total-1?'disabled style="opacity:.3"':''}>↓</button> <button class="btn-icon" onclick="openEditCat('${cat.id}')">✏️</button> <button class="btn-icon" style="border-color:#FEE2E2;color:#D14343;" onclick="confirmDeleteCat('${cat.id}','${cat.name}')">🗑</button> </div>`;
return div;
}

// Afficher les buckets dans l'ordre, avec leurs catégories
const orderedBuckets = […allBuckets].sort((a,b) => (a.order||0)-(b.order||0));
orderedBuckets.forEach(bucket => {
const cats = grouped[bucket.id] || [];
if (!cats.length) return; // Ne pas afficher les groupes vides

```
const groupEl = document.createElement("div");
groupEl.className = "settings-bucket-group";

const headerEl = document.createElement("div");
headerEl.className = "settings-bucket-header";
const bucketId = "bktGroup_" + bucket.id;
headerEl.innerHTML = `<span class="settings-bucket-name">📁 ${bucket.name} <span style="color:#aaa;font-weight:400">(${cats.length})</span></span><span class="settings-bucket-chevron">▼</span>`;
headerEl.onclick = () => {
  const body = document.getElementById(bucketId);
  if (!body) return;
  const closed = body.classList.toggle("hidden");
  headerEl.classList.toggle("closed", closed);
};
groupEl.appendChild(headerEl);

const bodyEl = document.createElement("div");
bodyEl.id = bucketId;
bodyEl.className = "settings-bucket-items";
cats.forEach((cat,i) => bodyEl.appendChild(makeCatItem(cat, i, cats.length)));
groupEl.appendChild(bodyEl);
container.appendChild(groupEl);
```

});

// Catégories sans groupe
if (noBucket.length) {
const groupEl = document.createElement("div");
groupEl.className = "settings-bucket-group";
const headerEl = document.createElement("div");
headerEl.className = "settings-bucket-header";
headerEl.style.background = "#F5F5F5";
headerEl.innerHTML = `<span class="settings-bucket-name" style="color:#999">— Sans groupe (${noBucket.length})</span><span class="settings-bucket-chevron" style="color:#999">▼</span>`;
headerEl.onclick = () => {
const body = document.getElementById("bktGroupNone");
if (!body) return;
const closed = body.classList.toggle("hidden");
headerEl.classList.toggle("closed", closed);
};
groupEl.appendChild(headerEl);
const bodyEl = document.createElement("div");
bodyEl.id = "bktGroupNone";
bodyEl.className = "settings-bucket-items";
noBucket.forEach((cat,i) => bodyEl.appendChild(makeCatItem(cat, i, noBucket.length)));
groupEl.appendChild(bodyEl);
container.appendChild(groupEl);
}
}

// ── Modal catégorie depuis budget ──
var _budgetCatModalId = null;
var _budgetCatModalPeriod = null;

function _toggleHiddenCats(btn, bucketId, period) {
const row = btn.closest("tr");
const hiddenIds = JSON.parse(row.dataset.hiddenIds || "[]");
const tbody = row.closest("tbody");
const showing = btn.dataset.showing === "1";

if (showing) {
// Cacher les lignes fantômes
tbody.querySelectorAll(".cat-ghost[data-bucket='" + bucketId + "']").forEach(r => r.remove());
btn.dataset.showing = "0";
btn.textContent = "👁 " + hiddenIds.length + " catégorie" + (hiddenIds.length > 1 ? "s" : "") + " masquée" + (hiddenIds.length > 1 ? "s" : "");
return;
}

// Afficher les lignes fantômes juste avant le bandeau
hiddenIds.forEach(catId => {
const budData = (window._budgetCatDetails || []).find(c => c.category_id === catId);
const catMeta = allCategories.find(c => c.id === catId);
if (!catMeta) return;
const ghostRow = document.createElement("tr");
ghostRow.className = "cat-row cat-ghost";
ghostRow.dataset.bucket = bucketId;
ghostRow.innerHTML = ` <td class="cat-name" colspan="5" style="padding:6px 14px;"> <span style="color:#bbb;margin-right:6px;">⠿</span> <span class="cat-name-link" onclick="event.stopPropagation();openBudgetCatModal('${catId}','${period}')" style="cursor:pointer;">${catMeta.name}</span> <span style="font-size:11px;color:#bbb;margin-left:8px;">masquée</span> </td>`;
tbody.insertBefore(ghostRow, row);
});

btn.dataset.showing = "1";
btn.textContent = "↑ Replier";
}

function openBudgetCatModal(catId, period) {
_budgetCatModalId = catId;
_budgetCatModalPeriod = period;
const cat = allCategories.find(c => c.id === catId);
if (!cat) return;

// Trouver les données budget de cette cat (depuis le dernier render)
const budData = (window._budgetCatDetails || []).find(c => c.category_id === catId);
const budgeted  = budData ? Number(budData.budgeted)  : 0;
const remaining = budData ? Number(budData.remaining) : 0;

const bkt = allBuckets.find(b => b.id === cat.bucket_id);
document.getElementById("budgetCatModalTitle").textContent = cat.name;
document.getElementById("budgetCatModalGroup").textContent = bkt ? "📁 " + bkt.name : "";
document.getElementById("budgetCatModalRename").value = cat.name;

const isActive = cat.active !== false;
const canHide  = budgeted === 0 && remaining === 0;

const toggleBtn  = document.getElementById("budgetCatModalToggleBtn");
const hint       = document.getElementById("budgetCatModalHideHint");

if (isActive) {
toggleBtn.textContent = "Masquer";
toggleBtn.style.background = "transparent";
toggleBtn.style.borderColor = canHide ? "#D14343" : "#ccc";
toggleBtn.style.color       = canHide ? "#D14343" : "#ccc";
toggleBtn.disabled = !canHide;
hint.textContent = canHide
? "La catégorie ne sera plus affichée dans le budget."
: "Impossible — budget assigné ou restant non nul.";
} else {
toggleBtn.textContent = "Afficher";
toggleBtn.style.background = "transparent";
toggleBtn.style.borderColor = "#34D399";
toggleBtn.style.color       = "#34D399";
toggleBtn.disabled = false;
hint.textContent = "La catégorie réapparaîtra dans le budget.";
}

// Reset bouton au cas où précédente save l'a laissé bloqué
var _saveBtn = document.querySelector("#budgetCatModal .btn-primary");
if (_saveBtn) { _saveBtn.disabled = false; _saveBtn.textContent = "Enregistrer"; }
document.getElementById("budgetCatModal").classList.add("active");
}

function closeBudgetCatModal() {
document.getElementById("budgetCatModal").classList.remove("active");
_budgetCatModalId = null;
}

function _renameCatFromBudget() {
if (!_budgetCatModalId) return;
const newName = document.getElementById("budgetCatModalRename").value.trim();
const cat = allCategories.find(c => c.id === _budgetCatModalId);
if (!newName || !cat) return;
if (newName === cat.name) { closeBudgetCatModal(); return; }
const btn = document.querySelector("#budgetCatModal .btn-primary");
if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = "⏳…"; }
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
allCategories = s.categories; allBuckets = s.buckets; allDebtors = s.debtors;
_refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
invalidateBudgetCache(); loadBudget(true);
if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = "Enregistrer"; }
closeBudgetCatModal();
})
.withFailureHandler(function() {
if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = "Enregistrer"; }
})
.updateCategory({ id: _budgetCatModalId, name: newName, bucket_id: cat.bucket_id });
}

function _toggleCatVisibility() {
if (!_budgetCatModalId) return;
const cat = allCategories.find(c => c.id === _budgetCatModalId);
if (!cat) return;
const newActive = cat.active === false ? true : false;
const btn = document.getElementById("budgetCatModalToggleBtn");
btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = "⏳…";
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
allCategories = s.categories; allBuckets = s.buckets; allDebtors = s.debtors;
invalidateBudgetCache(); loadBudget(true);
btn.disabled = false;
closeBudgetCatModal();
})
.withFailureHandler(function() {
btn.disabled = false;
btn.textContent = newActive ? "Afficher" : "Masquer";
})
.toggleCategoryActive(_budgetCatModalId, newActive);
}

function openEditCat(id) {
_editingCatId = id;
const cat = allCategories.find(c => c.id === id);
if (!cat) return;
var _cdb = document.getElementById("catModalDeleteBtn");
if (_cdb) _cdb.style.display = id ? "block" : "none";
document.getElementById("catModalTitle").textContent = "Modifier catégorie";
document.getElementById("catModalName").value = cat.name;
fillBucketSelect("catModalBucket");
document.getElementById("catModalBucket").value = cat.bucket_id || "";
document.getElementById("catModal").classList.add("active");
}
function closeCatModal() { document.getElementById("catModal").classList.remove("active"); }

// ─── Suppression depuis modal settings ────────────────────────
function _settingsRefresh(s) {
allCategories=s.categories; allBuckets=s.buckets; allDebtors=s.debtors;
renderSettings(); fillDebtorDatalist(); _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
_refreshSettingsMgmtIfOpen();
}
function deleteCatFromModal() {
if (!_editingCatId) return;
var id = _editingCatId;
closeCatModal();
showSpinner();
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(function(s){hideSpinner();_settingsRefresh(s);})
.withFailureHandler(function(e){hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur : "+e.message);})
.deleteCategory(id);
}
function deleteBucketFromModal() {
if (!_editingBucketId) return;
var id = _editingBucketId;
closeBucketModal();
showSpinner();
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(function(s){hideSpinner();_settingsRefresh(s);})
.withFailureHandler(function(e){hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur : "+e.message);})
.deleteBucket(id);
}
function deleteDebtorFromModal() {
if (!_editingDebtorId) return;
var id = _editingDebtorId;
closeDebtorModal();
showSpinner();
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(function(s){hideSpinner();_settingsRefresh(s);})
.withFailureHandler(function(e){hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur : "+e.message);})
.deleteDebtor(id);
}
function saveCatModal() {
const name = document.getElementById("catModalName").value.trim();
if (!name) return;
const bucket_id = document.getElementById("catModalBucket").value;
showSpinner();
function _afterCatSave(s) {
hideSpinner();
allCategories = s.categories; allBuckets = s.buckets; allDebtors = s.debtors;
renderSettings(); _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns(); _refreshSettingsMgmtIfOpen();
invalidateBudgetCache(); loadBudget(true);
closeCatModal();
}
if (_editingCatId) {
_gas().withSuccessHandler(_afterCatSave)
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.updateCategory({ id:_editingCatId, name, bucket_id });
} else {
_gas().withSuccessHandler(_afterCatSave)
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.addCategory({ name, bucket_id });
}
}
function confirmDeleteCat(id, name) {
_showConfirmModal(
'🗑 Supprimer la catégorie',
`Supprimer <b>${name}</b> ? Cette action est irréversible.`,
() => {
showSpinner();
_gas().withSuccessHandler(s=>{
hideSpinner();
allCategories=s.categories; allBuckets=s.buckets; allDebtors=s.debtors;
renderSettings(); _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();
invalidateBudgetCache(); loadBudget(true);
})
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.deleteCategory(id);
}
);
}

// Lit les IDs de tous les .smgmt-item[data-id] dans un container (y compris sous-groupes)
function _readSmgmtIds(contId) {
const cont = document.getElementById(contId);
if (!cont) return [];
return […cont.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-item[data-id]")].map(el => el.dataset.id);
}

// (anciennes fonctions _setOrderDirty/_saveSmgmtCatOrder/_moveItem supprimées — remplacées par drag-and-drop)

// ── Drag & Drop Groupes (desktop + touch mobile) ──
var _bktDragSrc = null;

// ── Drag catégories (dans un groupe) + save manuel ──
var _catDragSrc = null;

var _orderSaveType = null;

function _showOrderFloating(type) {
_orderSaveType = type;
var el = document.getElementById("orderSaveFloating");
if (!el) return;
// Reset état (au cas où précédente save l'a laissé bloqué)
el.style.pointerEvents = "auto";
el.textContent = "💾 Enregistrer l'ordre";
el.style.display = "block";
el.onclick = function() { _doSaveOrder(); };
el.ontouchend = function(e) { e.preventDefault(); _doSaveOrder(); };
}

function _hideOrderFloating() {
var el = document.getElementById("orderSaveFloating");
if (el) {
el.style.display = "none";
el.style.pointerEvents = "auto";
el.textContent = "💾 Enregistrer l'ordre";
}
_orderSaveType = null;
}

function _doSaveOrder() {
if (_orderSaveType === "cat") _saveCatOrderNow();
else if (_orderSaveType === "bkt") _saveBktOrderNow();
}

function _showCatSaveBar(container) {
_showOrderFloating("cat");
}

// _saveCatOrderNow : voir définition principale plus haut

function _attachCatDragEvents(el, groupBody, topContainer) {
var handle = el.querySelector(".bkt-drag-handle");

function _getGroup() {
return el.parentElement;  // smgmt-group-items courant
}

// Desktop
el.addEventListener("dragstart", function(e) {
_catDragSrc = el;
el.classList.add("dragging");
e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = "move";
});
el.addEventListener("dragend", function() {
el.classList.remove("dragging");
if (topContainer) topContainer.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-cat-draggable").forEach(function(d) { d.classList.remove("drag-over"); });
_catDragSrc = null;
});
el.addEventListener("dragover", function(e) { e.preventDefault(); });
el.addEventListener("dragenter", function() {
if (_catDragSrc && _catDragSrc !== el && _catDragSrc.parentElement === el.parentElement)
el.classList.add("drag-over");
});
el.addEventListener("dragleave", function() { el.classList.remove("drag-over"); });
el.addEventListener("drop", function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
el.classList.remove("drag-over");
if (!_catDragSrc || _catDragSrc === el || _catDragSrc.parentElement !== el.parentElement) return;
var grp = el.parentElement;
var items = […grp.querySelectorAll(":scope > .smgmt-cat-draggable")];
var fromIdx = items.indexOf(_catDragSrc), toIdx = items.indexOf(el);
if (fromIdx < toIdx) grp.insertBefore(_catDragSrc, el.nextSibling);
else                  grp.insertBefore(_catDragSrc, el);
_showCatSaveBar(topContainer);
});

// Touch : long press
var _touchTimer = null, _touchStartY = 0, _dragClone = null;

function _startTouch(e) {
_touchStartY = e.touches[0].clientY;
_touchTimer = setTimeout(function() {
_catDragSrc = el;
el.classList.add("dragging");
_dragClone = el.cloneNode(true);
_dragClone.style.cssText = "position:fixed;z-index:9999;width:" + el.offsetWidth + "px;opacity:0.85;pointer-events:none;border-radius:10px;background:var(--card,#fff);box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);";
var r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
_dragClone.style.left = r.left + "px";
_dragClone.style.top  = r.top  + "px";
document.body.appendChild(_dragClone);
if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(40);
}, 400);
}

function _moveTouch(e) {
if (!_catDragSrc) {
if (Math.abs(e.touches[0].clientY - _touchStartY) > 10) { clearTimeout(_touchTimer); _touchTimer = null; }
return;
}
e.preventDefault();
var y = e.touches[0].clientY;
if (_dragClone) _dragClone.style.top = (y - el.offsetHeight / 2) + "px";
var grp = el.parentElement;
var items = […grp.querySelectorAll(":scope > .smgmt-cat-draggable")];
items.forEach(function(it) { it.classList.remove("drag-over"); });
var target = items.find(function(it) {
if (it === _catDragSrc) return false;
var r = it.getBoundingClientRect();
return y >= r.top && y <= r.bottom;
});
if (target) target.classList.add("drag-over");
}

function _endTouch(e) {
clearTimeout(_touchTimer); _touchTimer = null;
if (_dragClone) { document.body.removeChild(_dragClone); _dragClone = null; }
if (!_catDragSrc) return;
el.classList.remove("dragging");
var y = e.changedTouches[0].clientY;
var grp = el.parentElement;
var items = […grp.querySelectorAll(":scope > .smgmt-cat-draggable")];
items.forEach(function(it) { it.classList.remove("drag-over"); });
var target = items.find(function(it) {
if (it === _catDragSrc) return false;
var r = it.getBoundingClientRect();
return y >= r.top && y <= r.bottom;
});
if (target) {
var fromIdx = items.indexOf(_catDragSrc), toIdx = items.indexOf(target);
if (fromIdx < toIdx) grp.insertBefore(_catDragSrc, target.nextSibling);
else                  grp.insertBefore(_catDragSrc, target);
_showCatSaveBar(topContainer);
}
_catDragSrc = null;
}

if (handle) {
handle.addEventListener("touchstart", _startTouch, { passive: true });
handle.addEventListener("touchmove",  _moveTouch,  { passive: false });
handle.addEventListener("touchend",   _endTouch,   { passive: true });
}
el.addEventListener("touchstart", function(e) {
if (e.target.classList.contains("bkt-drag-handle")) return;
_touchStartY = e.touches[0].clientY;
_touchTimer = setTimeout(function() {
_catDragSrc = el;
el.classList.add("dragging");
_dragClone = el.cloneNode(true);
_dragClone.style.cssText = "position:fixed;z-index:9999;width:" + el.offsetWidth + "px;opacity:0.85;pointer-events:none;border-radius:10px;background:var(--card,#fff);box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);";
var r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
_dragClone.style.left = r.left + "px"; _dragClone.style.top = r.top + "px";
document.body.appendChild(_dragClone);
if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(40);
}, 500);
}, { passive: true });
el.addEventListener("touchmove", _moveTouch, { passive: false });
el.addEventListener("touchend",  _endTouch,  { passive: true });
}

function _bktSaveOrder(container) {
_showOrderFloating("bkt");
}

function _saveBktOrderNow() {
var cont = document.getElementById("bucketsSettingsList2");
if (!cont) return;
var ids = […cont.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-bkt-draggable[data-id]")].map(el => el.dataset.id);
if (!ids.length) return;
var floatEl = document.getElementById("orderSaveFloating");
if (floatEl) { floatEl.style.pointerEvents = "none"; floatEl.textContent = "⏳ Sauvegarde…"; }
_gas()
.withSuccessHandler(function(s) {
allCategories = s.categories; allBuckets = s.buckets; allDebtors = s.debtors;
_refreshAllCategoryDropdowns(); invalidateBudgetCache(); loadBudget(true);
_hideOrderFloating();
switchSettingsTab("buckets");
})
.withFailureHandler(function() {
var floatEl = document.getElementById("orderSaveFloating");
if (floatEl) { floatEl.textContent = "⚠️ Réessayer"; floatEl.style.pointerEvents = "auto"; }
})
.reorderBuckets(ids);
}

function _attachBktDragEvents(el, container) {
var handle = el.querySelector(".bkt-drag-handle");

// ── Desktop drag ──
el.addEventListener("dragstart", function(e) {
_bktDragSrc = el;
el.classList.add("dragging");
e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = "move";
});
el.addEventListener("dragend", function() {
el.classList.remove("dragging");
container.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-bkt-draggable").forEach(function(d) {
d.classList.remove("drag-over");
});
_bktDragSrc = null;
});
el.addEventListener("dragover", function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
e.dataTransfer.dropEffect = "move";
});
el.addEventListener("dragenter", function() {
if (_bktDragSrc && _bktDragSrc !== el) el.classList.add("drag-over");
});
el.addEventListener("dragleave", function() {
el.classList.remove("drag-over");
});
el.addEventListener("drop", function(e) {
e.preventDefault();
el.classList.remove("drag-over");
if (!_bktDragSrc || _bktDragSrc === el) return;
var items = […container.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-bkt-draggable")];
var fromIdx = items.indexOf(_bktDragSrc);
var toIdx   = items.indexOf(el);
if (fromIdx < toIdx) container.insertBefore(_bktDragSrc, el.nextSibling);
else                  container.insertBefore(_bktDragSrc, el);
_bktSaveOrder(container);
});

// ── Touch : long press sur la poignée ──
var _touchTimer = null;
var _touchStartY = 0;
var _dragClone = null;

function _touchStart(e) {
_touchStartY = e.touches[0].clientY;
_touchTimer = setTimeout(function() {
_bktDragSrc = el;
el.classList.add("dragging");
// Créer un clone fantôme
_dragClone = el.cloneNode(true);
_dragClone.style.cssText = "position:fixed;z-index:9999;width:" + el.offsetWidth + "px;opacity:0.85;pointer-events:none;border-radius:10px;background:var(--card,#fff);box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);";
var r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
_dragClone.style.left = r.left + "px";
_dragClone.style.top  = r.top  + "px";
document.body.appendChild(_dragClone);
// Vibration courte si disponible
if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(40);
}, 400);
}

function _touchMove(e) {
if (!_bktDragSrc) {
// Pas encore en drag — annuler si mouvement trop grand
if (Math.abs(e.touches[0].clientY - _touchStartY) > 10) {
clearTimeout(_touchTimer); _touchTimer = null;
}
return;
}
e.preventDefault();
var y = e.touches[0].clientY;
// Déplacer le clone
if (_dragClone) {
_dragClone.style.top = (y - el.offsetHeight / 2) + "px";
}
// Trouver la cible sous le doigt
var items = […container.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-bkt-draggable")];
items.forEach(function(it) { it.classList.remove("drag-over"); });
var target = items.find(function(it) {
if (it === _bktDragSrc) return false;
var r = it.getBoundingClientRect();
return y >= r.top && y <= r.bottom;
});
if (target) target.classList.add("drag-over");
}

function _touchEnd(e) {
clearTimeout(_touchTimer); _touchTimer = null;
if (_dragClone) { document.body.removeChild(_dragClone); _dragClone = null; }
if (!_bktDragSrc) return;
el.classList.remove("dragging");
var y = e.changedTouches[0].clientY;
var items = […container.querySelectorAll(".smgmt-bkt-draggable")];
items.forEach(function(it) { it.classList.remove("drag-over"); });
var target = items.find(function(it) {
if (it === _bktDragSrc) return false;
var r = it.getBoundingClientRect();
return y >= r.top && y <= r.bottom;
});
if (target) {
var fromIdx = items.indexOf(_bktDragSrc);
var toIdx   = items.indexOf(target);
if (fromIdx < toIdx) container.insertBefore(_bktDragSrc, target.nextSibling);
else                  container.insertBefore(_bktDragSrc, target);
_bktSaveOrder(container);
}
_bktDragSrc = null;
}

if (handle) {
handle.addEventListener("touchstart", _touchStart, { passive: true });
handle.addEventListener("touchmove",  _touchMove,  { passive: false });
handle.addEventListener("touchend",   _touchEnd,   { passive: true });
}
// Long press sur toute la ligne aussi (fallback)
el.addEventListener("touchstart", function(e) {
if (e.target.classList.contains("bkt-drag-handle")) return; // déjà géré
_touchStartY = e.touches[0].clientY;
_touchTimer = setTimeout(function() {
_bktDragSrc = el;
el.classList.add("dragging");
_dragClone = el.cloneNode(true);
_dragClone.style.cssText = "position:fixed;z-index:9999;width:" + el.offsetWidth + "px;opacity:0.85;pointer-events:none;border-radius:10px;background:var(--card,#fff);box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.2);";
var r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
_dragClone.style.left = r.left + "px";
_dragClone.style.top  = r.top  + "px";
document.body.appendChild(_dragClone);
if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(40);
}, 500);
}, { passive: true });
el.addEventListener("touchmove",  _touchMove,  { passive: false });
el.addEventListener("touchend",   _touchEnd,   { passive: true });
}

function renderBucketsList() {
const container = document.getElementById("bucketsSettingsList");
if (!container) return;
container.innerHTML = "";
const ordered = […allBuckets].sort((a,b)=>(a.order||0)-(b.order||0));

ordered.forEach((bkt, idx) => {
const div = document.createElement("div");
div.className = "settings-item";
div.dataset.id = bkt.id;
div.innerHTML = ` <div class="settings-item-info"> <span class="settings-item-name">${bkt.name}</span> </div> <div class="settings-item-actions" style="display:flex;gap:4px;align-items:center;"> <button class="btn-icon" title="Monter" onclick="_moveItem(this,'up','bkt')" ${idx===0?'disabled style="opacity:.3"':''}>↑</button> <button class="btn-icon" title="Descendre" onclick="_moveItem(this,'down','bkt')" ${idx===ordered.length-1?'disabled style="opacity:.3"':''}>↓</button> <button class="btn-icon" onclick="openEditBucket('${bkt.id}')">✏️</button> <button class="btn-icon" style="border-color:#FEE2E2;color:#D14343;" onclick="confirmDeleteBucket('${bkt.id}','${bkt.name}')">🗑</button> </div>`;
container.appendChild(div);
});
}

function fillBucketSelect(selectId) {
const sel = document.getElementById(selectId);
if (!sel) return;
sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">— Aucun groupe —</option>';
allBuckets.forEach(b => { const o=document.createElement("option"); o.value=b.id; o.textContent=b.name; sel.appendChild(o); });
}

function openAddBucket() {
_editingBucketId = null;
document.getElementById("bucketModalTitle").textContent = "Nouveau groupe";
document.getElementById("bucketModalName").value = "";
document.getElementById("bucketModal").classList.add("active");
}
function openEditBucket(id) {
_editingBucketId = id;
const bkt = allBuckets.find(b => b.id===id);
if (!bkt) return;
var _bdb = document.getElementById("bucketModalDeleteBtn");
if (_bdb) _bdb.style.display = id ? "block" : "none";
document.getElementById("bucketModalTitle").textContent = "Modifier groupe";
document.getElementById("bucketModalName").value = bkt.name;
document.getElementById("bucketModal").classList.add("active");
}
function closeBucketModal() { document.getElementById("bucketModal").classList.remove("active"); }
function saveBucketModal() {
const name = document.getElementById("bucketModalName").value.trim();
if (!name) return;
showSpinner();
if (_editingBucketId) {
_gas().withSuccessHandler(s=>{hideSpinner();allCategories=s.categories;allBuckets=s.buckets;allDebtors=s.debtors;renderSettings();_refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();_refreshSettingsMgmtIfOpen();closeBucketModal();})
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.updateBucket({ id:_editingBucketId, name });
} else {
_gas().withSuccessHandler(s=>{hideSpinner();allCategories=s.categories;allBuckets=s.buckets;allDebtors=s.debtors;renderSettings();_refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();_refreshSettingsMgmtIfOpen();closeBucketModal();})
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.addBucket({ name });
}
}
function confirmDeleteBucket(id, name) {
_showConfirmModal(
'🗑 Supprimer le groupe',
`Supprimer le groupe <b>${name}</b> ? Les catégories seront conservées sans groupe.`,
() => {
showSpinner();
_gas().withSuccessHandler(s=>{hideSpinner();allCategories=s.categories;allBuckets=s.buckets;allDebtors=s.debtors;renderSettings();_refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();})
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.deleteBucket(id);
}
);
}

// –– DEBTORS LIST ––
function renderDebtorsList() {
const container = document.getElementById("debtorsSettingsList");
if (!container) return;
container.innerHTML = "";
if (!allDebtors.length) {
container.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#ccc;font-size:13px;text-align:center;padding:12px 0;">Aucun bénéficiaire / débiteur</p>';
} else {
// Tri par catégorie puis alphabétique
const _sortedDL = […allDebtors].sort((a, b) => {
const catA = (allCategories.find(x => x.id === a.default_category_id) || {}).name || "zzz";
const catB = (allCategories.find(x => x.id === b.default_category_id) || {}).name || "zzz";
const cmp = catA.localeCompare(catB, 'fr', {sensitivity:'base'});
if (cmp !== 0) return cmp;
return (a.name||'').localeCompare(b.name||'','fr',{sensitivity:'base'});
});
let _lastCatName = null;
_sortedDL.forEach(d => {
const cat = allCategories.find(c => c.id === d.default_category_id);
const catName = cat ? cat.name : "Sans catégorie";
// Séparateur de groupe catégorie
if (catName !== _lastCatName) {
const sep = document.createElement("div");
sep.className = "settings-debtor-sep";
sep.textContent = catName;
container.appendChild(sep);
_lastCatName = catName;
}
const div = document.createElement("div");
div.className = "settings-item";
div.innerHTML = ` <div class="settings-item-info"> <span class="settings-item-name">👤 ${d.name}</span> </div> <div class="settings-item-actions"> <button class="btn-icon" onclick="openEditDebtor('${d.id}')">✏️</button> <button class="btn-icon" style="border-color:#FEE2E2;color:#D14343;" onclick="confirmDeleteDebtor('${d.id}','${d.name}')">🗑</button> </div>`;
container.appendChild(div);
});
}
// Mettre à jour le label du collapse
const label = document.getElementById("debtorsCollapseLabel");
const body  = document.getElementById("debtorsBody");
if (label) {
const isOpen = body && !body.classList.contains("hidden");
label.textContent = isOpen ? "Replier" : "Voir (" + allDebtors.length + ")";
}
}

function openAddDebtor(prefillName) {
_editingDebtorId = null;
document.getElementById("debtorModalTitle").textContent = "Nouveau bénéficiaire";
document.getElementById("debtorModalName").value = prefillName || "";
fillCategorySelect("debtorModalCat", allCategories);
document.getElementById("debtorModalCat").value = "";
document.getElementById("debtorModal").classList.add("active");
}
function openEditDebtor(id) {
_editingDebtorId = id;
const d = allDebtors.find(x => x.id===id);
if (!d) return;
var _ddb = document.getElementById("debtorModalDeleteBtn");
if (_ddb) _ddb.style.display = id ? "block" : "none";
document.getElementById("debtorModalTitle").textContent = "Modifier débiteur";
document.getElementById("debtorModalName").value = d.name;
fillCategorySelect("debtorModalCat", allCategories);
document.getElementById("debtorModalCat").value = d.default_category_id || "";
document.getElementById("debtorModal").classList.add("active");
}
function closeDebtorModal() { document.getElementById("debtorModal").classList.remove("active"); }
function saveDebtorModal() {
const name = document.getElementById("debtorModalName").value.trim();
if (!name) return;
const default_category_id = document.getElementById("debtorModalCat").value;
showSpinner();
if (_editingDebtorId) {
_gas().withSuccessHandler(s=>{hideSpinner();allCategories=s.categories;allBuckets=s.buckets;allDebtors=s.debtors;renderSettings();fillDebtorDatalist();_refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();_refreshSettingsMgmtIfOpen();closeDebtorModal();})
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.updateDebtor({ id:_editingDebtorId, name, default_category_id });
} else {
_gas().withSuccessHandler(s=>{
hideSpinner();
allCategories=s.categories; allBuckets=s.buckets; allDebtors=s.debtors;
renderSettings(); fillDebtorDatalist(); _refreshAllCategoryDropdowns(); _refreshSettingsMgmtIfOpen();
closeDebtorModal();
// Si une TX attend ce bénéficiaire → continuer
if (_txSaveQueue.length) setTimeout(_processNextInQueue, 150);
})
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.addDebtor({ name, default_category_id });
}
}
function confirmDeleteDebtor(id, name) {
_showConfirmModal(
'🗑 Supprimer le bénéficiaire',
`Supprimer <b>${name}</b> ? Cette action est irréversible.`,
() => {
showSpinner();
_gas().withSuccessHandler(s=>{hideSpinner();allCategories=s.categories;allBuckets=s.buckets;allDebtors=s.debtors;renderSettings();fillDebtorDatalist();_refreshAllCategoryDropdowns();})
.withFailureHandler(e=>{hideSpinner();showInfoModal("Erreur: "+e.message);})
.deleteDebtor(id);
}
);
}

// ===== NAV LOCK (batch bar bloque la nav) =====
function _lockNav() {
document.querySelectorAll(".nav-item").forEach(b => {
b.style.pointerEvents = "none";
b.style.opacity = "0.4";
});
const ov = document.getElementById("navLockOverlay");
if (ov) ov.classList.add("active");
}
function _unlockNav() {
document.querySelectorAll(".nav-item").forEach(b => {
b.style.pointerEvents = "";
b.style.opacity = "";
});
const ov = document.getElementById("navLockOverlay");
if (ov) ov.classList.remove("active");
}

// ===== APPLY SETTINGS (after undo on settings) =====
function applySettings(settings) {
if (settings.categories) allCategories = settings.categories;
if (settings.buckets)    allBuckets    = settings.buckets;
if (settings.debtors)    allDebtors    = settings.debtors;
renderSettings();
fillCategorySelect("simpleCategory", allCategories);
fillCategorySelect("modalSimpleCategory", allCategories);
fillCategorySelect("prevModalCat", allCategories);
fillCategorySelect("editModalCat", allCategories);
}

}

}
